puruShottamadhyAnachakravAkyena 'tasyaiva' viShNoreva 'tat' sudhArNavadvayAshraya- lokavattvaM 'lakShaNatvena' liN^gatvena 'uchyate' pratipAdyate ityarthaH | 'hi' yasmAdityarthe | tasmAdetalliN^gabalAt viShNutvanishrayo yukta iti vAkyasheShaH | yadvA - brahmalokamiti hR^itpadmasya viShNulokatvokteH tadantargato viShNu- rityuktaM, brahmalokapadaM kuto viShNulokavAchItyata Aha - arashcheti | brahmalokapadasya viShNuloke 'arashcha' iti vAkye prayogAdatra hR^itpadme prayuktam 'etaM brahmalokam' iti padamapi viShNulokaparameva | na cha 'arashcha' iti shrutAvapi brahmalokapadaM kuto viShNulokaparamiti vAchyam | yatastatrAraNyAshrayatvaliN^gaM shrutamityarthaH | athApyaraNyA- shrayatvasya bhagavallokaliN^gatvaM kuta ityata Aha - arashcheti || asmin pakShe sautraM liN^gapadaM hR^itpadmasthasya brahmatvarUpapradAnasAdhye hetutvAbhAvAtsUtre liN^gashabdena pR^ithaguktiH | pUrvavyAkhyAnespi gatishabdayorivAsya liN^gasya viShNuniShThatAyA upapAdanasApekShatvena spaShTatvAbhAvAdgatishabdaliN^gairityanuktvA liN^gaM cheti pR^ithaguktiryuktA | anena - na kevalamuttarebhyo guNebhyaH, kintu gatishabdAbhyAM cha 'aharahaH' iti vAkye hR^itpadmasthaniShThatayA shrutAbhyAM suptaprApyabrahmashabdAbhyAM cha dahare viShNureveti j~nAyate | na kevalametAbhyAmeva, kintu yataH 'arashcha' iti shrutau 'tathA' gatishabdayoriva 'hi' viShNuliN^gatvena smR^itisiddhamaraNyAshrayalokavattvarUpaM liN^gaM hR^itpadmasthe viShNuloke prayukta- brahmalokapadasya hR^itpadme prayogAt 'dR^iShTaM' shrutamatospi dahare viShNureva | yadvA - kutostra prayuktasya brahmalokapadasya viShNulokaparatvam?  'arashcha' iti vAkye viShNuloke brahmalokapadaprayogAt | atrApi 'etaM brahmalokam' iti tasyaiva prayogAt | na cha tatrApi viShNulokaparatvaM kutaH?  yatosraNyAshrayatvaM liN^gaM 'dR^iShTaM' shrutamata iti sUtrArtha ukto bhavati |
(12) hetvantareNa viShNorhR^itpadmasthatvaM pratipAdayatsUtramupanyasya vyAchaShTe - dhR^iteriti || 'iti dhR^iteH' ityasya 'asminnasya' iti padAnuvartanenetyasminvAkyessya hR^itpadmasthasya dhR^itipadoktasarvAdhAratvashruterityarthaH | asya dahare viShNureveti pratij~nAvAkyenAnvayaH | shrutau vidhR^itiH seturityanvayaH | tatra vidhR^itirityetatsetutve hetuH | tathA cha ya AtmA hR^itpadmasthatvenoktaH sa eSha 'eShAM' bhUrAdilokAnAm 'asambhedAya' asAN^karyAya avidAraNAyeti, vyAsa- tIrthIyoktarItyA varNAshramasAN^karyAbhAvAyeti vA 'vidhR^itiH' dhAraNapoShaNasamarthosta eva seturiva 'setuH' Ashraya ityarthaH | dhArakatvaM cha na dhAryAdbahiShThatayA, kintvantaHkR^itajagattvena, 'shritamasmin jagatsarvamiti seturitIritaH' ityukteH mukhyArtha eva vA setushabdaH | yadyapi 'sa seturvidhR^itiH' iti ChandogashrutipAThaH | tathApi shAkhAntarANAma- pyatropasaN^grahAyaivamuktiH | evamanyatrApIti sampradAyavidaH |
(13) evaM setusamuchchAyakasautrachashabdasya yathAshrutAnvayena liN^goktiparatayA dhR^iteshchetyaMshaM vyAkhyAyedAnIM samagraM sUtraM samAnoktirUpasamAkhyAparatayA vyAchaShTe - eSha iti || dhR^iteritipadamatrAnuShajyate | asmin pakShe sautra- chashbada upalabdheshchetyanveti | tathA cha na kevalaM dhR^iterliN^gAt, kintu 'dhR^iteH' dhR^itiyuktAyAstadbodhikAyA upalabdheH vAsaneyake 'ya eShosntarhR^idaya AkAshastasmin shete sarvasya vashI' (bR^i. 6-4-21.) ityAdyuktvA AmnAtAyAH 'eSha sarveshvara eSha bhUtAdhipatireSha bhUtapAla eSha seturvidharaNa eShAM lokAnAmasambhedAya' ityukteH samAnokteshcha dahare viShNureveti yojanA | samAkhyAyAH kuto viShNuparatvamityata Aha - eSha iti | ityAdIti luptatR^itIyAvibhaktiko nirdeshaH | Adishabdena 'eSha sarvasya vashI eSha sarvasyAdhipatireSha sarveshvaraH' (bR^i. 6-4-21.) iti pUrvavAkyam 'eSha seturvidharaNa eShAM lokAnAmasambhedAya' ityuttaravAkyaM cha gR^ihyate | ata eva madhyasthavAkyagrahaNaM kR^itam | asya mahimna iti vyadhikaraNaShaShThyau | upalabdherityAvR^ittamatrAnveti | tathA cha 'asmin' vAjasaneyake 'eSha bhUtAdhipatiH' ityAdinA vAkyena 'asya' viShNorbhUtAdhipatitvAdimahimnaH 'asmin' daharAkAshagate vastuni 'upalabdheH' uktatvA- diti yojanA | ya eSha sarvasyAdhipatiH, yashchaiSha sarveshvaro, yashchaiSha prasiddho 'bhUtAdhipatiH' bhUta evAdhipatirnAsyAdhi- patyamAdimat, yashchaiSha bhUta eva pAlako, yashcha 'eShAM' bhUrAdilokAnAm 'asambhedAya' amelanAya eShAM 'vidharaNaH' vidhAraNasamarthaH, na kevalaM sAmarthyamAtraM, kintu ya eShAM lokAnAM 'setuH' Ashrayashcha, tametaM bhagavantaM brAhmaNA vividiShantIti shrutyarthaH | anena - na kevalaM pUrvoktahetubhyaH, kintu vidhR^iteshchAsmin prakaraNe 'sa seturvidhR^itiH' iti sarvAdhAratvaliN^gashravaNAdapi daharapadmastho viShNureva | na chAsya hR^itpadmasthatvaM kuta iti vAchyam | 'asya' hR^itpadmasthasya 'mahimnaH' apahatapApmatvAderlakShaNasya 'asmin' sarvAdhAre 'sarve pApmAnosto nivartante' (ChAM.8-4-1.) ityanena 'upalabdheH' uktatvAt | na kevalaM dhR^iterliN^gAt, kintu dhR^iterdhR^itiyuktAyA upalabdherukteH | 'ya eShosntarhR^idaya AkAshastasmin shete .... eSha seturvidharaNaH' iti vAjasaneyasamAkhyAyAshcha dahare viShNureva | samAkhyAyA api kuto viShNuviShayatvam?  'asmin' vAjasaneyake 'asya' viShNoH 'mahimno' bhUtAdhipatitvAderuktatvAditi sUtrArtha ukto bhavati | yadyapi 'asya mahimnaH' ityAdyaMsho bhAShye dhR^iteshchetyasya liN^gaparatayA yojanAyAM nAnvitaH | tathApi TIkAyAM 'sarve pApmAnostaH' iti tallakShaNokteshchetyuktatvAt liN^gasya hR^itpadmasthatvarUpapakShadharmopapAdakatayApi yojanIyaH |
(14) yaduktaM sarvAdhAratvaliN^gashravaNAt hR^itpadmastho viShNuriti, tatra sarvAdhAratvaM kuto viShNutvanishchAyakaM, tatsamAnAdhikaraNatvenAsiddhatvAdityata Aha - etasminniti || 'etasya vA akSharasya prashAsane' iti pratIkagrahaNena 'etasya vA akSharasya prashAsane gArgi sUryAchandramasau vidhR^itau tiShThataH, etasya 
vA akSharasya prashAsane gArgi dyAvApR^ithivyau' ityAdibahuvAkyAni sUchayati | imAnyakSharanaye vyAkR^itAni |
(15) nanu samAkhyAshrutyuktaH sarveshvaratvAdimahimA kuto viShNoravagata ityata Aha - sa hIti || 'sa hi' ityArabhya 'sa viShNuH' ityantamekaM vAkyaM shrutyantaragatam | 'saH' prakR^itaH | 'hiH' prasiddhau | 'patiM vishvasya' iti nArAyaNAnuvAkasthaM vAkyam | 'vishvasya' achetanaprapaJNchasya patiM 'AtmeshvaraM' chetaneshvaraM nArAyaNaM tadvishva- mupajIvatItyarthaH| ityAdIti | evamAdishrutivAkyebhya ityarthaH | AdishabdenaitajjAtIyaM gR^ihyate | tR^itIyArthe paJNchamI| 'tasya' viShNoH 'hiH' prasiddhau hetau vA | 'eSha sarveshvaraH' (bR^i.6-4-22.) ityAdimahimA | avagata iti sheShaH | tasmAnnaiteShAM viShNutvarUpasAdhyasAmAnAdhikaraNyAsiddhiriti vAkyasheShaH |
(16) nanu sarveshvaratvAdikaM viShNuvadanyasyApi kiM na syAdityata Aha - sarvesha iti || atra sarvajagachChabdau chetanAchetanaprapaJNchaparau | yadvA - jagataH patiriti pratiyogitvenaivoktasyAnuvAdaH | athavA - 'patiH' pAlakaH | tathA cha sarveshvaraH sarvapAlakashcha viShNureka eva nAnyosstItyarthaH | iti skAnda ityasya evakAroktapadAdhyAhAreNa tasyahyeSha mahimeti pUrveNAnvayaH | tasmAnnaitalliN^gAnAmanyatra sAvakAshatvaM shaN^kyamiti vAkyasheShaH |
(17) samAkhyAntararUpayuktyantareNa viShNorhR^itpadmagatAkAshasthatvaM sAdhayatsUtraM paThitvA vyAchaShTe - prasiddhe- shcheti || itItyanantaraM shrutAviti sheShaH | tasyetyanuvartate | 'tasya' viShNoH 'tasya' hR^itpadmasthasyeti tadarthaH | anena - sUtressyAsminnitipadadvayaM pUrvasUtrAdanuvartanIyam | tathA cha na kevalaM vAjasaneyasamAkhyAnAt, kintu 'asmin' tatrApIti taittirIyashrutivAkye 'asya' hR^itpadmasthasya viShNutvaprasiddheshcha tatsamAkhyAnAdapi daharapadmastho viShNureveti sUtrArtha ukto bhavati | 'divye brahmapure hyeSha vyomnyAtmA sampratiShThitaH' (muM. 2-2-7.) ityAtharvaNe prasiddheshcha | 'ya eShosntarhR^idaya AkAshastasminnayaM puruShaH' (tai. 1-2-1.) iti taittirIyavAkyAntare prasiddheshcheti sUtrasya yad.hvR^ittyantaraM TIkAyAM sUchitaM, tadbhAShyasthetishabdasyAdyarthatvamAshrityeti draShTavyam | shrutau 'daharaM vipApmaM paraveshmabhUtaM yatpuNDarIkaM puramadhyasaMstham' (mahAnA. 10-7.) iti vAkye yat 'daharam' alpaM parasya brahmaNaH sadmabhUtam, ata eva vigatapApaM dehAkhyabrahmapuramadhye saMsthaM hR^idayakamalaM prakR^itaM tattatreti parAmR^ishyate | tathA cha 'tatrApi' puNDarIkespi yat 'daharam' alpaM gaganamasti tasmin 'antaH' antare 'vishoko' vishokaM vishoka- padopalakShitaM jarAdishUnyaM yadbrahma tadupAsitavyamityarthaH | vishokaH iti liN^gavyatyayaH ChAndasaH | tattvapradIpe tu - liN^gavyatyAsastasya puruShatvaj~nApanArthaH | 'ya AtmAspahatapApmA vijaro vimR^ityurvishokaH' ityAdAvuditaguNAnAmadhi- karaNaikyabalena sannidhIyamAnAnAmanukarShaNArthashcheti prayojanamuktam |
(18) nanu sAkShAt padmagatasya viShNutvAbhyupagame suShirashrutivirodhaH | evaM padmagatAkAshasyaiva viShNutvAbhyu- pagamespi suShirashrutivirodhaH, suShirashabdasyAkAshavAchitvAt | etadvihAya 
daharapadmasyAkAshatvaM, viShNostvAkAsha- gatatvaM, tasyaiva sarvAdhAratvamityupagamespi suShirashrutivirodhaH | tatra sAkShAtsuShirasya sarvAdhAratvokterityata Aha - tadantasstheti || buddhyA viviktasuShirashrutipadaM ShaShThyantamatrAnvIyate | tathA cha 'suShirashruteH' iti suShirapada- ghaTitashruteH 'tadantassthApekShatvAt' padmagatasuShirAntassthaparamAtmAnamapekShya pravR^ittatvAttasya cha sarvAdhAratvAnna suShira- shrutivirodhossmadabhyupagamasyetyarthaH | yathA mandirasthamaJNjUShAntargatamapi vastu mandirasthamiti saN^gIyate, evamihA- pIti bhAvaH | tadantassthatveti pAThe paramAtmanaH suShirAntassthatvamapekShya shruteH pravR^ittatvAdityarthaH |
(19) bhagavato hR^itpadmasthatvamAkShipya samAdadhatsUtramupanyasyAkShepAMshaM tAvadvyAchaShTe - itareti || 'niShpadyate' ityanantaramityuktasyeti sheShaH | asya cha samAsapraviShTajIvapadenAnvayaH | anena sUtre asminnasyetyasyAnuvR^ittiH | itarapadaM siddhAntyabhimatabrahmapratiyogijIvaparam | ata eva shrutAveSha iti jIvaparAmarshaH | siddhAnte shrutyarthastu vakShyate |
(20) dhR^itisUtrAt 'asyAsmin upalabdheH' ityasyAnuvR^ittimabhipretyaparihArAMshaM vyAchaShTe - neti || hR^itpadma- stho na jIva ityarthaH | kuto netyatastatrAnuvR^ittavAkyena 'asmin' prakaraNe 'asya' apahatapApmatvAderupalabdherityasya hetorlAbhAttamanupanyasyoktahetorjIve niravakAshatvoktiparatayAssambhavAdityaMshaM vyAchaShTe - tasyeti || jIvasyetyarthaH | muktabhAvamAdAya jIve sambhavAt asiddhivArANAya - svata iti || svAtantryeNetyarthaH | satyakAmatvAdika- mAdishabdArthaH | anena - 'asmin' 'paraM jyotiH' itivAkyesbhivyaktikartR^itvenoktasya prakR^itasyopasampattikarmIbhUtA- dbrahmaNa itarasyAsya jIvasyAtmeti 'ya AtmA' ityuktahR^itpadmasthAtmatvavidhAnAya 'eShaH' ityetachChabdena 'parAmarshAt' upasthApanAt | jIvaparAmarshakaitachChabdashravaNAditi yAvat | dahare sa jIva eva, na viShNuriti chet - na hR^itpadmastho jIvaH| kutaH?  asminprakaraNessyApahatapApmatvAderupalabdheH shravaNAt | asya chAsmin jIve svatossambhavAditi sUtrArtha ukto bhavati |
(21) jIvasyApahatapApmatvAdyasambhavamAkShipya samAdadhatsUtramupanyasyAkShepAMshaM tAvadvyAchaShTe - uttarAditi || 'ityAdyuttaravachanAt' evaMrUpAddaharavAkyApekShayA parAmarshavAkyApekShayA vAsnantarAdvachanAdityarthaH | vachanAdityanantaram asyAsminnupalabdherityanuShajyate | sambhavAditi sheShaH | 'asya' satyakAmatvasya 'asmin' jIve pratItestata eva vishokatvAdeH 'upalabdheH' siddheruktaguNAnAM 
sambhavAditi tadarthaH | jIva ityanena pUrvasUtrAtsa ityasyAnuvR^ittiH sUchitA| neshvarA iti evashabdArthaH | hR^itpadmastha iti vartate |
(22) naJNanuvR^ittyA parihArAMshaM vyAchaShTe - neti || naitadvAkyabalena jIvasya satyakAmatvAdiguNAn sambhAvya hR^itpadmasthatvaM vAchyamityarthaH | kuto netyatosbhihitam 'AvirbhUtasvarUpastu' ityaMshaM tatreti padAdhyAhAreNa vyAchaShTe - tatreti || 'sa tatra' ityuttaravAkya ityarthaH | tatra 'AvirbhUtasvarUpaH' uchyate iti sambandhaH | AvirbhUtasvarUpaH ityasya vyAkhyAnaM mukta iti | hishabdo yata ityarthe | uttaravachanAdityatrApi sambadhyate | tathA cha 'uttaravachanAt' 'svena rUpeNa' iti jaDadehatyAgottarakAlInasvarUpAbhivyaktishruteH | atra muktasyokteH hR^itpadmasya cha dehAntaravR^ittitayA muktatvAyogAt nAyaM jIva iti bhAvaH | nanvasya muktaviShayatvespi muktasyApi jIvatve nAstyeva jIve.a- pahatapApmatvAdisambhavaH | na cha tasya hR^itpadmasthatvAyogaH, yato jIvo bhAvibhAvenApahatapApmatvAdiguNaH idAnIM hR^itpadmagatatayochyata ityata Aha - parameshvaraprasAdAditi | evetyanuvartate | anena tu shabdo vyAkhyAtaH | parameshvara- prasAdAdityanena uttarAdityetaduttamAdityapi vyAkhyAtam | atra mukta iti na sautrapadavyAkhyAnamAtram | kintUddeshya- samarpakaM cha | anena AvR^ittistushabdasya yathAshrutAnvayashcha sUchitaH | tathA cha yostra mukta uchyate sa tu parameshvara- prasAdAdeva 'AvirbhUtasvarUpaH' AvirbhUto vyaktaH svarUpaH apahatapApmatvAdiH svadharmo yasya sa tathoktaH | ato na svatospahatapApmatvAdiguNakaH, ato na daharasthaH jIva iti yojanA |
(23) nanu 'paraMjyotirupasampadya svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyate' (ChAM. 8-3-4.) ityatra muktasyAbhivyaktApahata- pApmatvAdiguNakatvamevochyate, na tu tadguNAnAM parameshvarAdhInatvam | atastatsvata evetyata Aha - yaditi || asya yachChabdasya dvitIyatachChabdenAnvayaH | prasAdo nAma ichChAvisheShaH | 'saH' jIvaH | punaH sa ityuktyA sUtresnuvR^ittasya sa ityasyAvR^ittiH sUchitA | pUrvokta ityanena sUtre uttaratretyasya pratiyogitayA pUrvatretyupaskAryamityuktaM bhavati | tatheti sheShaH | tathA cha 'yatprasAdAt' yasyAnugrahAt 'saH' jIvo 'muktaH' apahatapApmatvAdiguNo bhavati | 'saH' guNapradAtA bhagavAn, 'pUrvoktaH' 'paraMjyotirupasampadya' iti pUrvavAkye 'tathA' guNapradAtR^itayA ukta iti yojanA| anyathA lyabantapadaM vyarthaM syAditi bhAvaH | ukta ityanantaraM yata iti sheShaH | asyAtonAtra muktaguNaprApteH parameshvarAdhInatvoktyabhAva ityupaskR^itavAkyenAnvayaH | athavA - nanu jIvesnyAdhInasya tadguNajAtasya sattvAtsa evApahatapApmatvAdinokto hR^itpadmasthashchAstvityata Aha - yaditi | yojanA tu - yatprasAdAtsa jIvo jaDadehAnmukto bhavati, mukto bhUtvA cha sopahatapApmatvAdiguNo bhavati, sa bhagavAneva 'pUrvoktaH' 'eSha AtmAspahatapApmA' (ChAM. 8-1-5.) ityAdipUrvavAkye tathAspahatapApmatvAdinokto na jIvaH | dAtR^ipratigR^ihItrormadhye dAtureva mukhyatvAnmukhyA- mukhyayoshcha mukhyasyaiva grAhyatvAditi ||
anena - asya 'eSha samprasAdossmAchCharIrAtsamutthAya' (ChAM. 8-3-4.) ityaktasya jIvasya 'uttarAt' dahara- vAkyApekShayA parAmarshavAkyApekShayA vAsnantarAt 'sa tatra paryeti' ityAdivachanAt 'asmin' pUrvaprakR^ite jIve 'asya' satyakAmatvasya 'upalabdheH' pratIteH, tata evAsya vishokatvAdeH siddheshcha | ata evAsyoktaguNAsambhavAbhAvAtsa hR^itpadmastho jIva eva neshvara iti chet - na, yatastatra 'svena' ityuttaravAkyabalAdAvirbhUtasvarUpo mukta uchyate | sa cha dehAnantargatatayA na hR^itpadmastho bhavatIti bhAvaH | na cha muktasyApi jIvatvena tatrApahatapApmatva- hR^itpadmasthatvayorbhinnakAlInatvespi sAmAnAdhikaraNyopapatterasti punastasya prAptiriti vAchyam | yatostra vAkye yo mukta uchyate sa uttarAduttamAtparameshvaraprasAdAdevAvirbhUtasvarUpo na svataH | na chAtra muktasya tadguNatvamevochyate, na parameshvarAdhInatvaM tadguNajAtasyeti vAchyam | yataH pUrvatra 'paraM jyotiH' iti pUrvavAkye yatprasAdAtsa mukto bhavati sa paramAtmA tathA guNapradAtR^itayochyate | na cha yathAkathaM chit jIvasyApahatapApmatvAdiguNakatvAtpunastatprAptiriti vAchyam | yato yasmAduttarAduttamAdbhagavatastatprasAdAtsa muktaH 'AvirbhUtasvarUpaH' abhivyaktApahatapApmatvAdiguNakaH sa tu bhagavAneva pUrvatra 'eSha AtmAspahatapApmA' (ChAM. 8-1-5.) iti pUrvavAkye ukto, na muktajIva iti sUtrArtha ukto bhavati | shrutyarthastu 'eShaH' jIvo yataH 'samprasAdaH' samyagviShNuprasAdavAn ato 'asmAt charamasharIrAt' 'samutthAya' muktaH 'yatparaM' 'jyotiH' brahma 'upasampadya' prApya svena rUpeNa 'abhiniShpadyate' abhivyajyate 'sa uttamaH puruShaH' paraM jyotirakhyaH | muktasya viShayaishcharaNaprakAramAha - sa iti | 'saH' prAptinijAnandAvirbhAvo muktaH 'tatra' muktisthAne paramAtmAnugraheNaiva 'jakShan' svApekShitaM bhakShayan hasanvA j~nAtibhissaha muktaiH aj~nAtibhiH pUrvakalpamuktaiH 'krIDan' strIbhiH 'ramamANaH' ratiM prApnuvan prAkR^itastryAdiviShayasaukhyamanubhavan 'paryeti' paritaH saJNcharatIti |
(24) nanu 'eShaH' iti jIvaM parAmR^ishya 'AtmA' iti tasya hR^itpadmasthAtmatvAbhidhAnAdamukhyApahatapApmatvAdi- guNo.api jIvaH etachChabdaparAmarshabalena hR^itpadmasthAtmA kiM na syAdityAshaN^kAM pariharatsUtramupanyasya 'itara- parAmarshAtsa iti chenna' ityanuvR^ittapUrvavAkyenApekShitasya siddhAntapratij~nAyAshcha lAbhAnnetyuktasAdhye hetutayA sUtraM vyAchaShTe - anyeti || shrutau 'paraMjyotiH' iti napuMsakapadanirdiShTasya yamiti pulliN^gena nirdesho liN^gasyAvivakShi- tatvAdvA visheShyashabdavivakShayA vA yuktaH | anena shrutau paraMjyotiriti ekaM padam | yadvakShyati 'paraMjyotiHshabdena paramAtmaivochyate' iti, tachcha 'paraMjyotiH paraMbrahma' iti paurANikarUDhyA viShNuvAchItyuktaM bhavati | jyotiH prakAsharUpaM paraM brahmeti bhinne pade ityapi kechit | asmin pakShe uktabhAShyavirodhaH | kiM cha yaM 'paraMjyotirAkhyaM bhagavantam' iti yachChabdavyAkhyAnaparaTIkAvirodhaH | 'paraMjyotiH paramAtmAnam' iti viShNutattvanirNayaTIkAvirodha- shcha | shrutAvupasampadyetyasyArthaH prApyeti | sautrAnyapadaM pUrvapakShyabhimatajIvapratiyogitayA vyAkhyAti - paramAtmeti || paramAtmaivArtho.abhidheyo yasya sa tathoktaH | 'parAmarshaH' etachChabdaH | yadvA - paramAtmana 
evAtmatvavidhAnamarthaH prayojanaM yasya sa, tathoktaH | tathAtve 'parAmarshaH' etachChabdena parigrahaNamityarthaH | sUtrabhAShyayoshchashabdastu na kevalaM jIvapakShe.apahatapApmatvAsambhavAkhyabAdhakasadbhAvaH, kintu parAmarshAkhyasAdhakAbhAvashcheti samuchchayArthastushabdArtho vA | chandrikAyAM tu - na kevalaM parAmarshasya IshvarapakShe bAdhakatvAbhAvaH, kintu jIvapakShasAdhakatvAbhAvashchetyuktatvAtparAmarsho jIvAnyeshvarArtha eva ityavadhAraNArthatayA vyAkhyAtaH | anena - 'itaraparAmarshAt' itaraM jIvaM 'eShaH' iti parAmR^ishya tasya hR^itpadmasthatvavidhAnAtsa hR^itpadmastha AtmA jIva eva neshvara iti chet - na, kutaH? yataH 'eShaH' iti parAmarshaH 'anyArthaH' jIvAnyeshvarArtha eva, na jIvArthaH, ataH | athavA - na kevalamasambhavAt, kintu yataH parAmarsho.anyArtho.api | yadvA - asambhavAnna hR^itpadmastho jIvaH, kintvIshvara eva | na chaivaM parAmarshAyogaH | yataH 'parAmarshaH' etachChabdastu anyArtha iti tredhAsUtrArtha ukto bhavati | 'yaM prApya' yatsamIpaM prApyeti | anena jIvaH paraM jyotirAkhyaM paramAtmAnamupasampadyAparokShato j~nAtvA atha samIpaM prApyavidyAvidhUnanenAnandAdinA svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyate AvirbhUtasvaguNo bhavatIti yAvat | yaM prApya svarUpeNAbhiniShpadyate jIvaH, sa eSha AtmA ya Atmeti prAguktaH paramAtmeti hovAcha brahmAdIn prati rameti siddhAnte shrutyarthaH |
(25) uktamAkShipya samAdadhAtsUtramupanyasya shrutyudAharaNenAkShepAMshaM tAvadvyAchaShTe - alpeti || 'daharaH' iti pratIkagrahaNena 'daharo.asminnantara AkAshastasminyadantaH' iti vAkyaM gR^ihyate | alpapadaM chAlpasthAnasthitiparam | shruterityanantaramasambhavAdityanuvartate | asminniti chAsti | tathA cha 'daharaH' iti vAkye 'asmin' daharagate vastunyalpasthAnasthitirUpaliN^gashrutestasyAshchAsminparamAtmani 'asambhavAt' anupapatterityanvayaH | asmAddhetorna dahare viShNuH, kintu sa jIva evetItarasUtrAnuvR^ittapratij~nayA.anvayaH ||
(26) sUtre.anuvR^ittanaJNa AvR^ittimabhipretya parihArAMshaM vyAkhyAti - neti || nAlpasthAnasthitishravaNaM viShNAva- nupapannamityarthaH | kuto netyataH pravR^ittaM taduktamityaMshaM yata ityadhyAhArAbhiprAyeNa hetutayA vyAkhyAti - nichAyyatvA- diti | atrApIti sheShaH | tathA cha 'nichAyyatvAt' ityatra sarvagatasyApi viShNorvyomavadalpasthAnasthiteruktatvA- dityarthaH |
(27) nanu yuktaM vyomnoM.ashato.alpaukastvam, aMshasyApUrNatvAt | brahmaNi tu aMsho.api pUrNa iti kathaM tasyAMshato.alpaukastvamityataH sUtrasheShaM prakarAntareNa vyAchaShTe - eSha ma iti || cha shabdo yuktisamuchchaye | sUtra- kR^ichChrutyuktisamuchchaye vA | 'guNAH shrutAH' iti shrutisamuchchaye vA | 'yasmin' iti smR^itisamuchchaye vA | anena 'alpashruteH' 'daharaH' iti vAkye sarvagate vastunyalpasthAnasthitishravaNAt, tasyAshcha viShNAvasambhavAdanupapatterna dahare viShNuH, kintu sa jIva eveti chet - na, yataH 'taduktaM' tatra nichAyyatvAditi pUrvatra tasya sarvagatasyApi viShNorvyomavattadalpasthAnasthitatvam, tasmAdupAsanArthaM yuktamityuktam | na chAMshatopi sarvagatatayA tatra tadanupapattiH | yatastasyAM 'eSha ma AtmA' (ChAM. 3-14-3.) iti Chandogashrutau tena sarvajyAyastvena vR^iddhatamatvena vyAptatvenaiva prakAreNa tasya viShNostaddhR^idayasthatvamuktaM smR^ityuktaM chAta iti sUtrArtha ukto bhavati | na cha shrutismR^ityuktamapi 
kathametadaN^gIkArArhaM, yuktivirodhAditi vAchyam | brahmaNo.achintyashaktitvAdupapatteH | 'guNAH shrutAH' (sauparNashrutiH) 'yasminviruddhagatayaH' ityAdivachanAchcha | mama hR^idaye ya 'AtmA' paramAtmA.asti | upalakShaNametat | sarvahR^idaye cha ya Aste eShaH hR^idayasthAMsharUpo bhagavAn 'jyAyAn' vR^iddhatamaH deshakAlaguNaiH pUrNa iti shrutyarthaH | upaniShaddra- ShTR^iR^iShivAkyametat | ('viruddhagatayo.api' anyatra bhinnAshrayA apyaNutvamahattvAdayo dharmAH yasmin 'patanti' vartante cha | na kAlabhedenetyAha - anishamiti | muktasAdhAraNyamAshaN^kyAha -vidyAdaya iti | yasmAdviShNoranyatrANutva- mahatvAdivividhashaktayo dharmAH | vidyA AhiH j~naptikAraNaM yeShAM te tathoktAH | j~nAnaj~neyA iti yAvat | harau viruddhadharmasattve pramANamAha - AnupUrvyeti | 'AnupUrvI shrutirvedastrayI chAmnAya uchyate' ityabhidhAnAchChrutyA siddhA ityarthaH | yachChabdasya 'tadbrahmAhaM prapadye' iti uttaravAkyagatatachChabdenAnvayaH) || 5 ||
|| iti daharAdhikaraNam || 5 ||
|| 6. anukR^ityadhikaraNam ||
(1) atrAdhikaraNe 'kathaM nu tadvijAnIyAm' iti vAkyoktaM j~nAnArthaM j~neyaprArthanAviShayatvaM vA 'kathaM nu tadvijAnIyAM kimu bhAti' iti brahmaj~nAnAnukUlAbhivyaktyAkhyabhAnaprArthanAviShayatvarUpaM vA AnukUlyena gR^ihyamANatvaM liN^gaM brahmaNi samanvIyate | shrutyAdisaN^gatiM viShayAdikaM cha sUchayan sayuktikaM pUrvapakShaM darshayati - adR^ishyatvAditi| 'uktAH' AnandamayAdhikaraNe udAhR^itAdR^ishya iti vAkye iti bhAvaH | uktA ityanantaraM tatra praviShTamiti sheShaH | prathamAdipadenAniruktatvAdeH, dvitIyena 'kathaM nu tadvijAnIyAM kimu bhAti na bhAti vA' (kaTha. 5-14) iti samanveta- vyaliN^gabodhakottarArdhasya cha grahaNam | na kevalaM viShNoH, kintu j~nAnisukhasyApItyaperarthaH | evArtho vA.apishabdaH AnumAnikasUtragatApipadavat | 'aj~neyatvaM' sAkalyenAj~neyatvaM durj~neyatvamiti yAvat | chashabdaH parasparasamuchchaye, AnukUlyena gR^ihyamANatvarUpasamanvetavyaliN^gasamuchchaye vA | pUrvashratyanusArAdadR^ishyatvAdaya iti, etachChrutyanusArAda- nirdeshyatvamiti vyutkramaH| yadyapi 'tadetaditi' etadevodAhartavyam | tathApi pUrvapakShe tachChabdArthapradarshanAya 'teShAm' iti pUrvavAkyaikadeshopanyAsaH | ata eva tattvapradIpe teShAmiti prastutiH pUrvapakShotthApiketyuktam | tathAchetthaM yojanA - pUrvamAnandamayAdhikaraNe ye.adR^ishyatvAdayo guNAH parameshvarasyoktAH | tatra teShu praviShTamanirdeshyatvamaj~neyatvaM cha 'teShAM sukham' iti prakR^ityAmnAtena 'tadetat' ityAdinA kAThakavAkyena pUrvapakShirItyA samIpasthAttachChabdAt parAmR^iShTasya 'j~nAnisukhasyApi' j~nAnisukhasyaivochyata iti | pUrvArdhenAnirdeshyatvasyottarArdhe cha 'kimu bhAti na bhAti' ityanena durj~neyatvaparyavasitAj~neyatvasya chArthAduktatvAditi bhAvaH | TIkAyAmadR^ishyatvapadasyAnirdeshyatvaparatvAdanirdeshyatvamiti pAThAbhyupagamAdvA na 
tadvirodhaH | atrAnirdeshyatvamaj~neyatvaM chochyata iti phaloktiH, AnukUlyena gR^ihyamANatvasyaivAtra vichAryatvAt | tattu dvitIyAdishabdopAttavAkyena chashabdena vA sUchitamiti draShTavyam | yata evamataH pUrvokta- mayuktamiti bhAvaH | anenAnandamayAdhikaraNoktAdR^ishyatvAj~neyatvarUpasyAnirdeshyatvAniruktatvarUpasya cha tatrAnyatra cha sattve j~nAnisukhe.ativyAptyAkShepAt itaramAtraniShThatvetvasambhavAkShepAtphalatastenAsyAkShepikI saN^gatiruktA bhavati | tathA chashabdasUchitamAnukUlyena gR^ihyamANatvaM viShayaH | viShNoranyasya veti sandehaH | j~nAnisukhasyaiveti pUrvaH pakShaH | anirdeshyatvAj~neyatve cha tasyaiveti phalaM, sukhashrutiH, prakR^itatvAdirupayuktishcha sUchitA bhavati |
(2) siddhAntayatsUtramavatArya vyAchaShTe - ata iti || 'ityanukR^iteH' ityanubhAnashruterityarthaH | anubhAnaM nAma tadichChAnurodhena bhAnaM kriyAvisheShaH | sUtre tasyetyasyAnukR^iterityanenApi sambandhe tenaivAnukaraNapratisambandhina AnukUlyena gR^ihyamANasya tatkartuH sUryAditejasashcha lAbho bhavatIti spaShTatvAttadubhayAnuktiH | yadvA - pUrvasUtrAttadi- tyasya vipariNatasyehAnuvartanAdubhayalAbho bhavatItyAshayena tadubhayAnuktiH | na kevalaM tasyetyetat samanvetavyAnu- kUlyena gR^ihyamANatvAkhyaliN^gadharmiNaH, sUryAditejasashcha parAmarshakaM, kintu shrutipratIkarUpamapi sarvajagatprakAshakatvaparaM chetyAshayena taddhetvantaraparatayA vyAchaShTe - tasyeti | 'iti vachanAt' ityanena sUtre ityukteriti sheSho darshitaH | yadyapi sUtrabhAShyayoH 'anubhAti' itishrutyanusArAdanubhAnAditi vAchyam | tathApi 
tApinI pAchinI chaiva shoShiNI cha prakAshinI |
naiva rAjan raveshshaktiH shaktirnArAyaNasya sA ||
iti aitareyabhAShyodAhR^itapAdmavachanAtsUryAdikartR^ikapratapanAdikamapi paramAtmAdhInamiti darshayitumanukR^iterityuktam | sUtre tadanusAribhAShye cha chashabdo dvitIyasUtrasya vakShyamANavyAkhyAnabhedena sarvajagatprakAshakatvarUpoktahetusamuchchaye vA, sUryAdyaprakAshyatvarUpAnuktahetusamuchchaye vA draShTavyaH | sUtre samanvayasUtrAdanuvR^ittasya vidheyaparasya tattvityasyArthamAha - paramAtmaiveti | na tu j~nAnisukhamityevashabdArthaH | liN^gasamanvayena bhavatphalaM darshayati - anirdeshyeti | anirdeshya- shchAsau sukharUpashcha iti vA, anirdeshyaM yatsukhaM tadrUpa iti vA vigrahaH | atra rUpashabdo bhinnakramaH | tathA chAni- rdeshyaM paramaM sukhaM paramAtmarUpamityanvayaH | eka ityAdau pulliN^gena prakR^itasyaitaditi napuMsakaliN^gena grahaNAya rUpa- shabdaprayogaH | upalakShaNametat | anugrAhyaschetyapi draShTavyam | vastutastu - vachanAchchetishabdasya sukharUpashchetyapi sambandhe tenaivAnukUlyena gR^ihyamANAkhyaH sAdhyadharmI sUchita iti dhyeyam | yadyapyanirdeshyatvamaj~neyatvaM chetyupakramAdubhayaM grAhyaM, na tvekaM, sukharUpamiti chAdhikam | tathApi pUrvapakShyuktasukhashruteH sukharUpe brahmaNi 
sAvakAshatvaj~nApanAya 'tadetat' itivAkyoktamanirdeshyasukharUpatvameva gR^ihItam | aj~neyatvamapi draShTavyam | yadyapyatra bhAShye liN^gadvayasyA- nukUlyena gR^ihyamANasya vA anirdeshyasukharUpasya vA viShNutve sAdhye sAkShAddhetutvaM bhAti | TIkAyAM tu - 'tadetat' iti shrutisthatachChabdena samIpoktaj~nAnisukhaparityAgena 'chetanashchetanAnAm' (kaTha. 5-13.) iti vyavadhAnena prakR^itapara- mAtmagrahaNe liN^gadvayaM hetutvena yojitam | tathApi hetudvayena tachChabdena j~nAnisukhaparityAgena paramAtmana eva grahaNa- siddhau tata eva tachChabdagR^ihItasya paramAtmana evAnirdeshyasukharUpatvaM paryavasyatItyAshayena bhAShye liN^gadvayasya prakR^ita- sAdhyahetutvenoktirityavirodhaH | kechittu - 'paramAtmaivAnirdeshyasukharUpaH' iti bhAShyamevAnukR^itisUtre 'Anandamayo- bhyAsAt' ityAdAviva samanvetavyashabdAderviShNuparatva eva heturnochye, kintvanirdeshyaM sukhamityatra samIpoktaj~nAni- sukhaparityAge heturuchyate ityatra j~nApakaM, TIkApi tadanusAriNItyAhuH | tathA chAyaM siddhAnte shrutyarthaH-
eko vashI sarvabhUtAntarAtmA ekaM rUpaM bahudhA yaH karoti |
tamAtmasthaM ye.anupashyanti dhIrAH || (kaTha. 5-12.) ||
iti pUrvavAkye 'ya eko' j~nAnAnandAdyabhinnaH samAbhyadhikashUnyo vA yaH sarvamasya vashe.astIti 'sarvavashI' yaH 'sarvabhUtAntarAtmA' sarvaprANinAmantarniyAmakaH 'ya ekaM' svasvarUpaM bahudhA karoti niyamyAnantyAt | 'taM' prakR^itam 'AtmasthaM' jIvahR^idayasthitaM ye 'dhIrAH' j~nAninaH anupashyantIti prakR^itA ye j~nAninasteShAmeva 'shAshvataM sukhaM' nityAbhivyaktasaukhyaM netareShAm | anena brahmasAmarthyamuktaM bhavati | evaM 'nityo nityAnAm' iti vAkyamapi brahma- mAhAtmyaparatayA vyAkhyeyam | 'tadetat' ityAdinApi prakR^itabhagavatsvarUpameva visheShataH pratipAdyate iti | manyante ityasyottaratrAnvayaH | tathA cha 'yato vAcho nivartante' (tai. 2-4-1.) 'eSho.asya parama AnandaH' (bR^i. 6-3-32.) ityAdau prasiddham anirdeshyaM paramaM sukhaM kathaM nu tadvijAnIyAmiti manyante ityAnukUlyena gR^ihNanti | j~nAnArthaM tadbhAnaM vA prArthayante | 'kimu bhAti na bhAti vA' iti tasya durj~neyatvaM cha vadanti j~nAninaH | tat brahmaNo rUpaM svarUpabhUtaM sukhametadekaM rUpaM bahudhA yaH karotItiprakR^iteshvararUpAbhinnamiti manyante j~nAnina iti | etachChabdasyeshvara- paratve.api rUpashabdasAmAnAdhikaraNyAt napuMsakaliN^gatopapattiH | taduktaM nyAyavivaraNe - 'yadbrahmAnirdeshyaM sukhamiti vadanti tadetatsvarUpamiti manyanta iti' | kAThakabhAShye tu - tad 'guhyaM brahma sanAtanam' ityupakrAntam | 'rUpaM rUpaM pratirUpo babhUva' (kaTha. 5-9.) iti jIvasya pratibimbatvamuktam | rUpashabdena prakR^itametat 'ekaM rUpam' ityatra prakR^itaM cha bhagavadrUpam 'anirdeshyam' itthamiti sAkalyena nirvaktumashakyaM paramaM sukhamiti 
manyante j~nAnina iti sukharUpatva- vidhiparatayA vyAkhyAtam | bhAShye.apyanirdeshyasukharUpa ityetAvanmAtragrahaNena shrutau sukharUpatvaM vidheyamiti sUchitam | tadanirdeshyaparamasukhAtmakaM bhagavadrUpaM tatparasAdamR^ite kimu bhAti na bhAti veti samyagbhAti na bhAtIti kathaM nvahaM jAnIyAmiti shiShTavAkyArthastatraivoktaH | vivR^itaM chaidvyAsatIrthIye - 'tat' anirdeshyaparamasukhAtmakaM bhagavadrUpaM tatpra- sAdamR^ite kimu samyagbhAti?  na bhAti vAti?  iti prashnottarabhUtam ekaM nishchitArthaM 'kathamahaM vijAnIyAM' na kenApi prakAreNeti | atretishabda ubhayAnvayI | tathA cha kimu bhAtIti prashnasyottarabhUtaM na bhAtItivAkyokta- mekamaj~neyatvarUpamarthamiti yojanA | kechittu - yadevaM brahma tatprasAdamR^ite 'nu' idAnIM 'kathamahaM vijAnIyAm' prArthanIyAM liN^ | na kathamapItyarthaH | j~nAnivAkyAnukaraNametat | bhagavatprasAdAdapi kiM sAkalyena tajj~nAnaM bhavatIti nachiketA yamaM pR^ichChati - kimu bhAtIti | ushabdaH samyagityarthe | kimvityekaM vA | tathAtve samyagiti sheShaH | uttaramAha yamaH - na bhAtIti | vAshabdoSh.avadhAraNe | na bhAtyeveti vyAkhyAti |
(3) nanu 'tameva bhAntam' iti vAkye sUryAditejasAM paramAtmAdhInaprakAshakartR^itvasya 'tasya bhAsA' itivAkye cha sarvasya jagatastatprabhAprakAshyatvasya cha shravaNena asiddhiparihAre kutastayorviShNutvasAdhyenAvyabhicharitatvam, yena talliN^gadvayabalAtsamIpoktaj~nAnisukhapAmarshaparityAgaH syAdityata Aha - na hIti || sarvamityubhayAnvayI | bhAtIti sheShaH | tathA cha 'hi' yasmAt 'sarvaM' sUryAditejaH j~nAnisukhamanusR^itya 'na bhAti' na prakAshate | tathA 'tadbhAsA' tasya j~nAnisukhasya prakAshena 'sarvaM' jagat 'na bhAti' na prakAshate chetyarthaH | vakShyamANapramANavirodhAditi bhAvaH | chashabdaH samuchchaye | ato na liN^gadvayamanyatrAvakAshavaditi vAkyasheShaH |
(4) astvetadubhayaM j~nAnisukhe.anupapannam | tathApyanena kutaH paramAtmano grahaNaM, asya paramAtmatvasAdhya- sAmAnAdhikaraNyAnishchayAdityatastatra dvitIyasUtrasthApipadena sUchitAM shrutimAha - ahamiti || ahamitItyanantaraM shruteriti sheShaH | itishabda AdyArthe | tena 'tameva bhAntamanubhAti sarvaM tasya bhAsA sarvamidaM vibhAti' (kaTha. 5-15.) ityAtharvaNashrutirapi gR^ihyate | nArAyaNeti | nArAyaNAdhInabhAsetyarthaH | hishabdo yata ityarthe, prasiddhau cha | 'sarvaM' sUryAditejaH 'bhAti' prakAshate | yadvA - 'nArAyaNabhAsA' nArAyaNIyabhAsA 'sarvaM' jagat 'bhAti' prakAshasya ityarthaH | 'iti j~nAyate' iti sheShaH | shrutau 'rashmIt' ityanena sUryAditejasAM nArAyaNAdhInaprakAshakartR^itvasya, 'tejaH' ityanena sarvasya jagato nArAyaNIyaprakAshaprakAshyatvasya choktatvAditi bhAvaH | 'aham' iti, shrutistvantarnaye vyAkhyAtA | anena - taduktamityataH sUtre tadityanuvartate | tasyetyAvartate vipariNamyate cha | asambhavAditi chAnu- 
vartate | tathA cha -
tadetaditi manyante.anirdeshyaM paramaM sukham |
kathaM nu tadvijAnIyAm || (kaTha. 5-14.) ||
ityAnukUlyena gR^ihyamANaM tadetachChabdaparAmR^ishyaM sukham anirdeshyaM sukhaM tattu viShNurUpameva, na samIpoktaj~nAnisukham | kutaH? 'tasya' sUryAditejasaH 'tasya' AnukUlyena gR^ihyamANasya sukhasya tasmin 'tameva bhAntam' iti 'anukR^iteH' anubhAnashravaNAttasyaitadadhInaprakAshakartR^itvashravaNAdasyAnyatejoniyantR^itvashravaNAditi yAvat | tathA tasya sarvasya jagatastasya tatprakAshaprakAshyatvasya 'tasya bhAsA' (kaTha. 5-15.) iti shrutAvuktatvAttasya sarvajagatprakAshatvokteriti yAvat | tasya cha liN^gadvayasya 'ahaM tattejaH' (chaturvedashikhA.) ityAdishrutyA smR^ityA cha tasminviShNAveva nishchaye- nopapatterj~nAnisukhe cha 'asambhavAt' anupapatteH | tathA tasminnupasaMhAre tasyAnukUlyena gR^ihyamANasya 'na tatra sUryo bhAti' iti vAkye tasya sUryAdyaprakAshyatvasyachokteshcheti sUtrArtha ukto bhavati |
(5) yadetalliN^gadvayasya viShNuniShThatvam 'aham' iti shrutyopapAditam | tatsmR^ityA.apyupapAdayatsUtraM paThitvA tAM smR^itimudAharati - apIti || iti smaryata ityanvayaH | 'yat' AdityAdiShu sthitaM tejastat 'mAmakaM' madadhInaM madIyaM cha, matteja evAdityAdiShu prerakatvenAsti | tadevAkhilaM jagat 'bhAsayate' prakAshayatIti gItAsmR^ityarthaH |
(6) kiM cha pAThake 'na tatra sUryo bhAti na chandratArakaM nemA vidyuto bhAnti kuto.ayamagniH' ityAdyAnukUlyena gR^ihyamANasya sukhasya sUryAdyaprakAshyatvamuchyate | tachcha viShNoreva smaryate, ato viShNureva 'tadetat' ityatra pratipAdyaH, na j~nAnisukhamiti sUtrasyArthAntaramapipadasya yuktisamuchchayArthatvaM chAbhipretya tAM smR^itimudAharati - na taditi || atrApItishabdasya smaryata ityanvayaH | j~nAnino 'yadgatvA' yatprApya punastasmAnnanivartante, tanmama paramaM 'dhAma' svarUpaM, tadetaddhAma sUryo 'na bhAsayate' na prakAshayate, evaM 'shashAN^kaH' chandraH | yadA chaivaM tadA kuto.a- yamavamo.agniriti gItAsmR^ityarthaH | anena - pUrvavyAkhyAne na kevalamanukR^ityAdiH 'ahaM tattejaH' iti shrutyantare 'tamevabhAntamanubhAti' ityAtharvaNAdau viShNudharmatvena shrUyate, kintu yadAdityeti smaryatepIti shrutisamuchchayArthe.a- pishabdaH | dvitIyavyAkhyAne tu 'tameva bhAntamanubhAti' ityuttaravAkyoktAnukR^ityAdihetoH 'na tatra sUryo bhAti' iti pUrvavAkyoktasUryAdyaprakAshyatvahetoshcha samuchchaye.apishabdaH | tathA cha na kevalaM 'tadetat' ityatroktAnukUlyena gR^ihyamANasya viShNutvarUpapradhAnasAdhye hetUkR^itamanukR^ityAdikam 'ahaM tattejo rashmIt' ityAdau shrUyate, kintu yadAdityeti smaryate.apIti vA apiH | kiJNcha - yato na kevalaM prathamasUtroktaliN^gadvayaM, kintu tato.anyadapi 'na tatra' iti kAThakavAkye tasyAnukUlyena gR^ihyamANasyoktaM sUryAdyaprakAshyatvarUpaM liN^gaM tasya viShNoH sambandhitvenaiva 'na tat' iti smaryate | atastadetat 'kathaM nu tadvijAnIyAm' ityatra viShNureva pratipAdya iti vA sUtrasyArthadvayamuktaM bhavati 
| 'na tatra' ityAderayamarthaH | pUrvaM brahma na samyagbhAtIti tasya durj~neyatvamuktaM, tatkuta ityataH idamuchyate - yasyaivaMvidhaM sukhaM rUpaM 'tatra' brahmaNi sUryo 'na bhAti' tanna prakAshayatIti yAvat | chandratArakamiti dvandvaikavadbhAvaH| evaM tat vidyuto.api 'na bhAnti' na bhAsayantIti | 'tameva bhAntam' ityuttaravAkyaM tu yadyapi vyAsatIrthakR^itA- tharvaNaTIkAyAm - 'etatsamAkhyArUpamAtharvaNavAkyaM' 'bhAntaM' bhAsayantaM paramAtmAnamanusR^ityaiva sUryAdayo 'bhAnti' prakAshate iti vyAkhyAtam | tathApi TIkAnusArAt 'sarvaM' sUryAditejaH 'bhAntaM' prakAshamAnaM bhagavantamanusR^ityaiva 'bhAti' prakAshate | 'tasya' bhagavato 'bhAsA' prakAshena 'idaM sarvaM' jagati 'bhAti' prakAshyata iti vyAkhyeyam | vyAsatIrthIyaM tu vyAkhyAnAntaraM TIkAkR^idabhipretaM bhaviShyatIti  tadvirodhaH || 6 ||
|| iti anukR^ityadhikaraNam || 6 ||
|| 7. vAmanAdhikaraNam ||
(1) atrAdhikaraNe IshAnanAmasamanvayaH kriyate | shrutyAdisaN^gatiM viShayasaMshayau cha sUchayati - viShNureveti | jij~nAsAsUtre viShNurevasarvairmumukShubhirmokShArthaM jij~nAsya ityuktamityarthaH | na cha tatra jij~nAsyatvAyogavyavachCheda eva kR^itaH, na tvanyayogavyavachCheda iti vAchyam | anyasyApi jij~nAsyatve tasyApi mokShadAtR^itvApattyA 'yato nArAyaNaprasAdamR^ite' ityAdivivaraNAnupapatteranyayogavyavachChedasyApi tatrAbhipretatvAt | ato.atraivakAra ubhayAnvayitayA vyAkhyeyaH | tataH kimityata Aha - tatreti | idaM chAvartate | tatretyavyayaM tadityarthe.api | tathA cha 'athAto brahmajij~nAsA' iti yatpUrvaM viShNorjij~nAsyatvamuktaM 'tatra' jij~nAsyatve 'tatra' 'IshAno bhUtabhavyasya' ityuktvA AmnAte 'Urdhvam' iti kAThakavAkye 'kashchit' IshAno dharmitvena pratIyate | katham? yato.ayaM 'sarvadevopAsyaH' tairjij~nAsyaH pratIyate ata iti vAkyayojanA | na cha vAyoH sarvadevopAsyatve.api na viShNossarvadevopAsyatvahAniriti vAchyam | tAvatA.api sarvairmumukShubhirviShNureva jij~nAsya iti niyamasyAsiddheH | na cha shrutigatavishvedevashabdasya gaNavisheShavAchitvAt sarvadevo- pAsya ityuktiranupapanneti vAchyam | gaNavisheShaparatve tasya guNAdhikyAsiddhyA sarvadevaparatvAvashyaMbhAvAt | anena - IshAnashabdasyAnyaniShThatvAkShepamukhena phalato mumukShukartR^ikajij~nAsyatvasyAnyaniShThatvAkShepAt jij~nAsAdhikaraNenAsyA- kShepikI saN^gatiruktA bhavati | tatheshAnAkhyo viShayashcha sUchitaH |
(2) sayuktikaM pUrvapakShayati - sa cheti || atretthaM yojanA - 'sa cha' sarvadevopAsyashcheshAno vAyureva bhavet, na viShNuH | kutaH?  atra prANavyavasthApakatvashravaNAt | tathA madhyamatvokteH sarvadevatopAsyatvokteshcha | na chaiShAM vAyvekaniShThatvAsiddhiH | yato.ayaM vAyuH 'evamevaiSha prANaH' (prashna. 3-4.) 'yo.ayaM madhyamaH' 'kuvidaN^ga' (R^i. 7-91-1.) ityAdinA vAkyena prANavyavasthApakatvadimAn pratIyate, ata iti | kAThake hi -
aN^guShThamAtraH puruSho madhya Atmani tiShThati |
IshAno bhUtabhavyasya || (kaTha. 4-12.) ||
ityanena bhagavato.aN^guShThamAtratvaM pUrNaShaDguNatvaM dehamadhyasthatvaM bhUtabhaviShyadvartamAneshAnatvamityAdimAhAtmyamabhidhA- yeshAnapadoktasya tasyaiva 'Urdhvam' ityAdinA mahimAntaramuchyate | tatra madhyashabdaH siddhAnte UrdhvaMpratyakChabdasama- bhivyAhArAt deshavisheShavachanaH, natvavAntareshvaratvAdirUpamadhyamatvArthakaH | tathA cha yaH prANAkhyarUpeNa 'prANaM' prANA- khyavAyumUrdhvam 'unnayati' udgamayati UrdhvagatimattayA prerayati | apAnarUpI chApAnAkhyaM vAyuM 'pratyak' adhastAdviNmUtrAdiniShkAsanahetutayA 'asyati' nirasyati prerayatIti yAvat | taM 'dehamadhye' hR^idaye 'AsInam' upaviShTaM 'vAmanaM' saundaryapradhAnAH striyo vAmAH tAH netAraM viShNuM 'vishve devAH' sarve devAH 'upAsate' jij~nAsanta iti siddhAntarItyA shrutyarthaH | pUrvapakShI tvidaM vAyuparaM matvA madhyashabdo 'yo.ayaM madhyamaH' iti shrutyantarasamAkhyA- nAnmadhyameshvaratvavachano na deshavisheShavachana ityAha | 'evam' iti ShaTprashnavAkyaM cha 'yathA samrADevAdhikR^itAnvi- niyuN^kte etAngrAmAnadhitiShThasveti' iti dR^iShTAntavAkyena saha vyAkhyeyam | tatprakArastu - yathA 'samrAT' sArvabhaumaH 'adhikR^itAn niyogino.adhikR^itya viniyuN^kte' | katham?  tvam 'etAn' pATalIputrAdIn grAmAn 'adhitiShThasva' tadAdhipatyena tiShThasveti | 'evamevaiShaH' 'Atmata eSha prANo jAyate' (prashna. 3-2.) ityAtmajAtatvenokto mukhya- prANaH 'itarAn' bhinnAn svajanyatvenopachAreNAtmapravibhAgAn prANAn vAyUn pR^ithaksthAneShu hR^idayAdiShu sthApayatIti | 'yo.ayam' ityAdibR^ihadAraNyakavAkyam | tatra hi pUrvaM vAgAdInAM mR^ityugrastatvamuktvA 'athainameva nApnot' ityanena mukhyaprANasya tadanAttatvena tebhyaH shraiShThyamabhidhAya 'yo.ayam' ityanena prANashabdavAchyeShu viShNuvAyutaditareShu chetaneShu triShu viShNoruttamatvAdanyeShAmadhamatvAdvAyormadhyamatvAdasmAnnimittAdvA avAntareshvaratvAdvA mukhyaprANasya sarvottamatvarUpa- kAShThAtvAvirodhimadhyasthatvamevochyate, na tu madhyadeshasthatvam | tathA tatraiva chaturthAdhyAye 'ayaM vAva shishuH yo.ayaM madhyamaH prANaH' (bR^i. 4-2-1.) iti chandrikodAhR^ite vAkye sthUladehAkhyavistR^itapradeshagataliN^gasharIrarUpagR^ihe viShNu- rUpAyAM sthUNAyAm annAkhyena shrIrUpeNa dAmnA baddho govatsarUpovAyurmadhyamatvenochyate |
kuvidaN^ga namasA ye vR^idhAsaH purA devA anavadyAsa Asan |
te vAyave manave bAdhitAyA.avAsayannuShasaM sUryeNa ||
iti R^iN^mantre 'aN^ga' iti priyasambodhanam | tathA cha ye devAH vAyoH 'namasA' namaskAropalakShitasevAdinA 'vR^idhAsaH' vR^iddhA j~nAnAdiguNapUrNAH 'anavadyAsaH' anavadyAH aj~nAnarAgAdyavadyavidhurAshcha purA sasUryA Asan | te 'kuvit' kvachidrahasyasthAne sUryeNa sAkaM 'manave' j~nAnine 'bAdhitAyA' saMsArakleshavadbhiH sharaNaM prAptAya 'vAyave' vAyumuddishya 'uShasam' uSha prakAshe, asun, buddhim 'avAsayan' tadviShayAmakurvanniti shrutyarthaH |
siddhAntayatsUtramavatArya vyAchaShTe - ata iti || 'vAmanashabdAt' vAmanashruteH | evakAro vAyuliN^gasadbhA- vAt vAyureveshAnaH kiM na syAditi chodyaparihArAya liN^gebhyaH shruteH prAbalyamAha | yathoktaM sudhAyAm - evashabda- vyAkhyAnaM balavaditi 'shabdAdeva pramitaH' iti yatheti | samanvayasUtrAdanuvR^ittasya tadityasyArtho viShNuriti | vidheyabhUtaviShNutvasyAnvayayogyoddeshyadyotanAyetishabdaprayogaH | Avartate chAyam | itishabdAtparamapi evashabdo yojyaH | tenAnuvR^ittastu shabdo vyAkhyAtaH | tathA cha 'IshAno bhUtabhavyasya' (kaTha. 4-12.) iti shruta IshAno viShNureva bhavet | kutaH? yastatra pramito viShNAveva mahAyogavidvadrUDhibhyAM prasiddho 'madhye vAmanam' itishruto vAmana- shabdastasmAdeveti yojanA | pramitapadaM shruterniravakAshatvasUchakam | anena sUtre itishabdo.adhyAhArya iti sUchitam | tathA cha 'IshAno bhUtabhavyasya' itishrutaIshAnaH 'tattu' viShNureva bhavet | kutaH? yastatra viShNAveva pramito mahAyoga- vidvadrUDhibhyAM prasiddho.anyatra niravakAsho 'madhye vAmanamAsInam' (kaTha. 5-3.) itishruto liN^gAtprabalo vAmanashabda- stachChrutistasmAditi sUtrArthaH |
(3) sUtre evakAraprayogena sUchitaM shruteH prAbalyaM liN^gasya prAbalyaniShedhamukhena darshayati - na hIti || shrute- riti paJNchamI | hishabdo vakShyamANapramANavirodhAditi hetusUchakaH | tathA cha 'hi' yasmAt na shruterliN^gaM balavat, kintu durbalameva | tasmAlliN^agAt prabalAt vAmanashabdAdeveshAno viShNurevetyarthaH |
(4) kuto na shruterliN^gaM balavadityatastathAsati shruterliN^gAtprAbalyavachanavirodhApatterityAshayena tadvAkyaM paThati - shrutiriti || iti skAnda ityanantaraM vachanAditi sheShaH | asya na hItyanenAnvayaH | vAchakashabdaHshrutiH | asAdhAraNadharmo vA, tadbodhakashabdo vA liN^gam | nirNItasyAnyatra samAnoktiH samAkhyA | sA dvividhA - arthata- shshabdato.apIti | samabhivyAhR^itapadairevAkAN^kShApUrtau tachChAntyarthaM padAntaranirapekShANi padAni vAkyam | ekaprameyaprati- pAdakAnekavAkyAni prakaraNam | anuktasthAnasamuchchaye tathetishabdaH | anekaprameyapratipAdakamekArthatAtparyayuktaM vachanaM sthAnam | atra 'vAkyaM prakaraNaM sthAnaM samAkhyA cha tathAvidhA' ityanuvyAkhyAnusAreNa samAkhyAyAH sthAnAnantaryameva grAhyaM, na tvatroktakramAnusAreNa vAkyAdyapekShayA prAthamyam | atroktakramasyAvivakShitatvAt | uktaM hi pramANalakShaNa- TIkAyAM - samAkhyAditvena grahaNaM 'shrutirliN^gaM samAkhyA cha' ityavivakShitakramaM vAkyamanusR^ityeti | ata eva jaiminiH - 'shrutiliN^gavAkyaprakaraNasthAnasamAkhyAnAM samavAye pAradaurbalyamarthaviprakarShAt' iti smR^ityuktAdanyathAkramamAha - pUrvaM- pUrvamiti | pUrvoddiShTamityarthaH | ekatra samavetaM viruddhamiti cha sheShaH | 'balIyaH' atishayena svabhAvato balavat yathA.atraivAdhikaraNe anantaroddiShTaliN^gApekShayA pUrvoddiShTA vAmanashrutiH svataH prabalA| vAkyApekShayA prabalaM liN^gam| yathA - daharAdhikaraNe daharAkAshasya sAkShAtsarvAdhAratvaprApakAt 'kiM tadatra vidyate ..... ubhe asmin dyAvApR^ithivI' (ChAM. 8-1-2,3.) iti vAkyAtprabalaM viShNostatprApakApahatapApmatvAdikaM liN^gam | prakaraNApekShayA prabalaM vAkyam| yathA - jyotirdarshanAt ityadhikaraNe jIvasya 'hR^idyantarjyotiH' (bR^i. 6-3-7.) itivAkyabodhyajyotiShTvasAdhakAjjIva- prakaraNAtprabalaM viShNorjyotiShTvaprApakaM 'katama AtmA' (bR^i. 6-3-7.) iti prashnavAkyam | sthAnApekShayA 
prabalaM prakaraNam | yathA - samagropaniShada IshvaraparatvasAdhakAt ShaTprashnarUpasthAnAt prabalam 'Atmata eSha prANo jAyate' (prashna. 3-3.) ityetatkhaNDarUpaM mukhyaprANaprakaraNam | ata evAtrAdhikaraNe ShaTprashnoktaprANavyavasthApakatvAdInAM mukhyaprANaliN^gatvamupetya shrutyA bAdha uktaH | samAkhyApekShayA prabalaM sthAnam | yathA - annamayAdishabdAnAM kosha- paratvasAdhakAt 'annamayaprANamayamanomayavij~nAnamayAnandamayA me shudhyantAm' (yAj~nikI. 66.) iti nArAyaNAnuvAka- samAkhyAyAH prabalaM teShAM viShNutvasAdhakaM brahmaparAnekaprakaraNasandarbharUpaM sthAnam | etAnyeva shrutyAdinA.arthanirNaya- sthalAni | AdyayA samAkhyayA nirNetavyaM yathA - puruShasUktasamAkhyayA vaishvAnarasya viShNutvam | dvitIyayA yathA - ambhraNIsUktasamAkhyayA vishvakarmasUktoktasyAjasya viShNutvam | astvevaM tataH kimityata Aha - evamiti | viruddhaiteShAM samavAye sati prabalena pUrveNottarabAdhe cha sati 'AgamanirNayaH' AgamArthasya vipratipannasyaitaiH nirNayo bhavatItyarthaH |
(5) nanvastu shruteH svabhAvataH prAbalyam | tathApi bAhulyena pUrvapakShyuktaliN^gAnAmapi prAbalyAtsAmyenAnirNaya evetyata Aha - tachcheti || chastvarthaH | liN^gamiti samudAyaikavachanam | tathA cha 'tat' pUrvavAdyuktaM liN^gajAtaM tu viShNoreva yuktam, na vAyorityarthaH | tathA cha bAhulye.api liN^gAnAM sAvakAshatvAttebhyaH shruterekasyA api niravakA- shAyAH prAbalyAnnAnirNaya iti bhAvaH | nanu na liN^gaM viShNau sAvakAshaM, pUrvapakShyudAhR^itasamAkhyArUpashrutyantareNa tasya prANaniShThatayaivoktatvAdityata Aha - tasyaiveti | 'tadvai tvam' iti shrutau 'tasya' viShNoH prANatvasya prANashabdavAchyatvasyokteruktatvAdityarthaH | evaM 'ata eva' ityatrAdhyAtmikAsheShashabdasya samanvayaM bruvatA tathA - 'shAstradR^iShTyA' ityatrAntaryAmiparatvaM bruvatA sUtrakAreNetaravyAvR^ittyA tasyaiva prANatvokteH sAdhitatvAdityapi vyAkhyeya- metat | tathA cha shrutyantare prANaniShThatayA liN^gasyoktAvapi na tadvirodhaH | tasya prANasya viShNutvAbhyupagamAditi bhAvaH | nanu tathApi 'kuvidaN^ga' iti R^ichi vAyuniShThatayA liN^goktestadvirodha ityasyApIdamevottaram | asmin pakShe prANatvamiti vAyutvamupalakShyate | tathA chAntarnaye AdhidaivikAsheShashabdasamanvayaM bruvatA sUtrakAreNa 'tasyaiva' viShNoreva 'prANatvokteH' vAyushabdavAchyatvarUpavAyutsyoktatvAdityarthaH | tathA cha na tadvirodhopIti bhAvaH | na cha siddhAnte.api sthAnApekShayA prabalAtprakaraNAt 'evamevaiShaH' itishrutyantaragataprANashabdasya, tathA 'yo.ayaM madhyamaH' (bR^i. 3.5-21.) ityasya, tathA 'kuvidaN^ga' iti mantrasthavAyushabdasya mukhyavAyuparatvaM, tatroktaliN^gAnAmapi tatparatva- mupetya teShAM shrutyA bAdhasyoktatvAt kathaM shrutyantarasthaprANavAyushabdayoH viShNuparatvAN^gIkAreNa samAdhAnam | ata eva chandrikAyAm - madhyamashabdo.api 'UrdhvaM prANam' (kaTha. 2-2-3.) iti prANasya sthAnAntaranirdeshAttatyAgena madhyamasthAnasthabrahmaparaH, na tu shrutyantare 
madhyamashabdoktaprANapara ityuktam | ataH 'evamevaiShaH' (prashna. 3-4.) iti vAkyaM sthAnAtprakaraNasya prAbalye udAhR^itamiti vAchyam | uktarItyA mukhyataH shrutyantaragataprANashabdAderbrahmaparatvena liN^gAnAM tattadantaryAminiShThatve.api samAkarShanyAyenAnyaparatvasyApyaN^gIkArAt | shrutyantaroktaliN^gAnAmanyaniShTha- tve.api vA nAnupapattiH | na chaivaM kAThakoktaliN^gAnAmapyanyaniShThatvApattyA anyeShAmIshAnatvAdyApattiH | niravakAsha- shrutyA kAThakoktaliN^gAnAM viShNuniShThatAnirNayopapatteH | nanu tathApi kathamIshAno viShNurbhavechChrutAvIshAnasyAN^guShTha- parimitatvokteH | sarvagate cha harau tadayogAt | na cha vyomavatsarvagatasyApyaNutvaM yujyata iti pratipAditamiti vAchyam | tathApi 'aN^guShThamAtraH' iti tanmAtraparimANatvokterayogAt | na cha 'aN^guShThamAtraH' ityatra shrutaH pari- mANArthako mAtrach.hpratyaya eva, na tvavadhAraNArthako mAtrashabdaH | 'dehAN^guShThamito dehe jIvAN^guShThamito hR^idi' iti smR^itau mita ityanena parimANasyaivokteH | tathA cha nAnupapattiriti vAchyam | tathAtve.aN^guShThamAtratvAbhidhAtryAm 'aN^guShThamAtraH' (kaTha. 4-12.) iti shrutau 'madhya Atmani' ityasya smR^itau hR^idItyasya cha vaiyarthyApAtAt | tanmAtra- parimitatvoktyarthaM hi tatra hR^idayarUpasUkShmasthAnoktiH | tasmAdavadhAraNArthakamAtrashabda evAyamaN^gIkAryaH uktaM hi chandrikAyAm - mAtrashabdasyAvadhAraNArthakatvAditi |
(6) tathA cha sarvagate harAvaN^guShThamAtratvoktiranupapanneti nAtreshAno viShNurityAshaN^kAM pariharatsUtramupanyasya tadakSharANi vyAchaShTe - hR^idIti || sarvagatasyApItyanena tushabdo yadyapitathApItyarthatayA vyAkhyAtaH | hR^idyapekShayetyanena sUchitahetoranvayayogyaM sAdhyaM darshayati - tasyeti | yojanA tu - yadyapi viShNuH sarvagatastathApi 'tasyAN^guShTha- mAtratvam' aN^guShThamAtratvoktiryujyate | katham? yato 'hR^idyavakAshopekShayA' hR^idi vidyamAno yo.ayamavakAsho.aN^guShTha- parimitadeshastadapekShayA tatrAbhivyaktatAvatparibhitabhagavanmUrtivisheShamapekShya tasya viShNoraN^guShThamAtratvam astyata iti| yadvA - 'hR^idyavakAshApekShayA' hR^idi vidyamAnAvakAshamapekShya tatsambandhAttasyAN^guShThamAtratvavachanaM yujyata ityAvR^ittiM vinA yojanA | prathamapakShe shaktyA.aparimite.api bhagavati mUrtivisheShe vyaktyAtmanA.aN^guShThamAtratvasya sthAnini brahmaNi tatsambandhAdupachAreNoktiriti bhedaH | atra TIkAyAM hR^idyavakAshApekShayeti bhAShyaM sAvadhAraNaM kR^itvA sautratushabdo.a- vadhAraNatayA vyAkhyAtaH | tena viShNoN^guShThamAtratvaM hR^idyapekShayaiva, na tu lokavatparichChinnatvAdityuktaM bhavati | tatta- tsthAneShu vyaktamUrtivisheShApekShayA vA upachAreNa vA tattatparimANatvoktyA 'yastvetameva prAdeshamAtram' (ChAM. 5-18-1.) iti ChAndogye 'prAdeshamAtraM puruSham' ityanyatra 'prAdeshaH puruShottamaH' ityaparatra cha hR^idgatasya viShNoH prAdeshaparimitatvokteH | 'aN^guShThamAtraH puruSho.aN^guShThaM cha samAshritaH' (mahAnA. 16.3.) iti shrutyantare 'aN^guShTha- mAtraH puruShaH' iti kaThavalyAM cha 'aN^guShThamAtraH puruShaH' ityaparatra chAN^guShThaparimitatvokteH 'aN^guShThAgrapramANakaH' iti kvachidaN^guShThAgrapramANakatvoktervirodha iti chodyaM parihR^itaM bhavati | dehe hR^idayAkAshe prAdeshaparimitarUpavisheShasya hR^idayagatakamalakarNikAmUlagatAkAshe.aN^guShThAgrapramANakarUpAntarasya 
karNikAgragatAkAshechAN^guShThaparimitarUpAntarasya cha vyaktisambhavAt, tattatsthAnadharmasya sthAninyupacharitatvasambhavAchcha | yathoktaM bR^ihadAraNyakabhAShye -
hR^idaye sarvasho vyApI prAdeshaH puruShottamaH |
jIvAnAM sthAnamuddiShTaH sarvadaivasanAtanaH ||
hR^itkarNikAmUlagataH so.aN^guShThAgrapramANakaH |
mUlesha iti nAmAsmin sarve jIvAH pratiShThitAH ||
aN^guShThamAtre puruShe karNikAgrasthite harau |
prAvishanti suShuptau tu prabudhyante tatastathA || iti ||
asmin mUleshavyApinormadhye.aN^guShThamAtratvaM cha dehe dehAN^guShThamitatvaM jIvahR^idi jIvAN^guShThamitatvamiti vivektavyam | atra 'aN^guShThaM cha samAshritaH' ityanena karmendriyAdhiShThitatvamuchyata iti prameyadIpoktamapi j~nAtavyam | nanu 'dakShiNA- kShimukhe vishvo manasyantastu taijasaH' ityAdivachanAjjAgradAdyavasthAprerakavishvataijasaprAj~nAnAM dakShiNAkShyAdiShu sattvaM tAva- tsiddham | yadi chaivaM tadA jIvo.api jAgradavasthAyAM dakShiNAkShisthaH svapne kaNThadeshasthaH suptau hR^idayastho bhavati, 'hR^idayasthAtparAjjIvo dUrastho jAgradeShyati' ityukteH | dUrastho.akShistho jAgrajjAgratvamiti tasyArthaH | tathA cha kathaM hR^idayavyAptaprAdeshaparimitabhagavadrUpasya sarvadA jIvasthAnatvam?  kathaM cha hR^itkarNikAmUlagatabhagavadrUpe sadA pratiShThito jIvaH? suptau hR^itkarNikAgragate harau pravishatItyuktiriti chet - na, yatassarvadA hR^idi sthitameva jIvasvarUpaM jAgaritA- dAvakShyAdiShvapi visheShasannihitaM dIpaprakAshavadityaN^gIkR^itam | yathoktamaitareyabhAShye - hR^ide sthitameva tasya rUpaM jAgarite.apyakShyAdiShu visheShasannihitaM bhavatIti | ekasyaiva jIvasya sthApanadhR^ityAkhyapratiShThApanasuptiprApaNAkhya- prayojanabhedAdekadehe anekadhA sthitAnAM bhagavanmUrtInAM shaktyA sarvagAnAmapi tatra tatra vyaktyAtmanA anekAlpapari- mANavattvaM cha yujyata iti na kAchidanupapattiH |
(7) nanu tathApi nAN^guShThaparimANavattvaM viShNoryuktam | tathA hi kiM tattadaN^guShThamAtratvaM vA yatkiJNchida- N^guShThamAtratvaM vA | nAdyaH, pashvAdInAmaN^guShThAbhAvena tadantargatasya viShNoraN^guShThaparimitatvAyogAt | na dvitIyaH, aN^guShThamAtratvoktestaistaistathopAsanArthatvena tasya chAN^guShThavyaktivisheShanirdhAraNa vinA.ayogena yatkiJNchidaN^guShThamAtra- tvoktervyarthatvAt | pipIlikAdihR^idayasthe.aN^guShThamAtratvasAbhAnyasyApyasambhavAchchetyAshaN^kAM pariharan manuShyAdhikAra- tvAt itisUtrasheShaM tushabdasya kAkAkShinyAyena atrApyanvayaM tasyApyarthatvaM cha abhipretya tatsambandhipradarshanapUrvakaM vyAchaShTe - itareti || pashvAdInAmityarthaH | apirAvartate | aN^guShThamAtratvamityetat vipariNAmevAnuvartate | 'na virodhaH' iti virodhasUtrAdAkR^iShTe pade | tathA cha 'api' tattadaN^guShThaparimitatvAN^gIkAre.apItaraprANinAmaN^guShThA- bhAve.api na viShNoraN^guShThamAtratvasya 
virodhenAN^guShThamAtratvokterasambhavaH | kutaH?  aN^guShThamAtratvokteretadvidyAyA 'manuShyAdhikAratvAt' manuShyAnadhikR^itya pravR^ittatvAt | tadapi kutaH? vedavidyopAsanasya 'manuShyAdhikAratvAt' manuShyamAtrAdhikAratvAditi yojanA | sUtre bhAShye cha manuShyANAmadhikAro yasmin athavA - adhikriyate.atretyadhikAra upAsanaM shAstraM vA, manuShyANAmeva adhikAro manuShyAdhikArastasya bhAvasatasmAditi vigrahaH | 'manuShyAdhikAritvAt' itipAThe manuShyA adhikAriNo yasmin tattathoktam | tathA cha manuShyAdhikArikatvAdityarthaH | manuShyapadaM cha vakShyamANanyAyena mananAdishIlachetanaparam | tena devAnAM jaritAryAdInAM vakShyamANanyAyena vedavidyAdhikAriNAmeta- dvidyAdhikArasiddhiH | tatra jaritAryAdInAM svasvAN^guShThaparimitatvena bhagavadupAsanA.asambhavAt, teShAmetadvidyotpannavA- kyArthaj~nAna evAdhikAro, nopAstAvapi | ata eva TIkAyAM manuShyANAmeva vedavidyopAsanAdhikAritveneti manuShyatvaM vyApakatvenoktam | na chAnadhikAriNAM pashvAdInAM dehasthitasya bhagavato.aN^guShThaparimitatvAbhAve parimANAntarAnuktera- dravyatvApattiriti vAchyam | pashvAdidehagatasya paramAtmanaH tattadAkArayuktatvena tadanusAriparimANavattvAt | yathoktamaitareyabhAShye - 
saN^karShaNashcha pradyumnastadAkArau nR^iShu sthitau |
nArAyaNAniruddhau tu pashvAkArau pashusthitau || iti ||
anena - sUtre tushabdo.apyarthevadhAraNe cha | tatrApyarthasyobhayatrAnvayaH | aN^guShThamAtratvaM yujyata iti sheShaH | taditi pradhAnasUtrAdanuvR^ittasyeha vipariNAmenAnvayaH | na virodhaH ityasyAkarShaH | 'tasya manuShyAdhikAritvAt' ityA- vartate | tathA cha 'tu' api sarvagatasyApi 'tasya viShNoraN^guShThamAtratvaM' taduktiryujyate | na cha virodhaH | yato.atra 'hR^idyapekShayA tu' hR^idyavakAshApekShayaiva aN^guShThamAtratvamuchyate, na tu parichChinnatvAt | tachcha mUrtivisheShe tanmAtratvasya sattvAdupachAreNa vA yujyate | na cha nAN^guShThamAtratvaM viShNoryuktaM, yatkiJNchidaN^guShThamAtratvoktervyarthatvenAsambhavena cha tattadaN^guShThamAtratve vAchye tasya cha pashvAdInAmaN^guShThAbhAvena tadantargataviShNAvayogAditi vAchyam | yataH 'tu' api itaraprANinAmaN^guShThAbhAve.api na viShNostattadaN^guShThamAtratvasya 'virodhaH' asambhavaH | kutaH?  aN^guShThamAtratvavacha- nasya yadbodhakavidyAyAH 'manuShyAdhikAratvAt' manuShyAnevAdhikR^itya pravR^ittatvAt | tadapi kutaH? 'tasya' vedavidyo- pAsanasya 'manuShyAdhikAratvAt' manuShyamAtre.adhikAratvAditi sUtrArtha ukto bhavati |
|| iti vAmanAdhikaraNam || 7 ||
|| 8. devatAdhikaraNam ||
(1) asminnadhikaraNe devAnAM brahmavidyAdhikAraH samarthyate | prAsaN^gikatvAnnAdhyAyapAdasaN^gatI mArgaNIye | shrutyAdisaN^gativiShayasaMshayatadbIjAni darshayati - manuShyANAmiti || 'uktaM' pUrvasUtre | tushabdArthAvadhAraNasya samA- sapraviShTamanuShyapadenApi sambandho.astIti bhAvena manuShyANAmevetyanuvAdaH | netareShAmityevashabdArthaH | 'vedavidyAdhi- kAro' vedavidyopAsanAdhikAraH | anena - devatAdhikArAbhAvamukhena 'vishve devA upAsate' ityAdipUrvodAhR^itashrutyupa- lakShitAsheShashrutiprAmANyasyAkShepAtpUrvAdhikaraNenAsyAkShepikI saN^gatiH vedavidyAdhikArAkhyo viShayashchokto bhavati | 'aN^guShThamAtraH' iti shrutimUlAyAH 'manuShyANAmeva' ityukteH 'vishve devA upAsate' (kaTha.2-2-3.) iti shruteshcha koTidvayopasthApakatvena sandehabIjatvAttaduktyaiva devAnAmadhikAro.asti uta nAstIti saMshayo, nAstIti pUrvapakShashcha sUchitaH |
(2) tataH kimityatassaMshayabIjaM vighaTayan siddhAntayituM sUtramavatArayati - tiryagAdIti || vishiShTa- buddhyAdirahitatiryagAdivyAvR^ittyarthamityarthaH | manuShyatvavisheShaNaM sAvadhAraNatvenAbhipretam | manuShyapadam 'uktaM' prayuktaM, tatreta sheShaH | pUrvasUtra iti tadarthaH | svaprayuktaivakAravyAvarttyaM darshayati - na tviti || 'devAdyapekShayA' devAdivyAvR^i- ttyartham | tushabdo visheShArthaH | na tu devAdyarthamapItyapishabdArtho vA | 'ityAha' ityabhipretya sUtrakAro devAnAmadhi- kArabhAvamAhetyarthaH |
(3) tatsUtraM paThati - taduparIti || atra taduparIti sAdhyadharmisUchakaM padamanUdya teShAM tasmAttasyA iti vigrahAshrayeNa vyAchaShTe - taduparIti || vedavidyAkAra ityanuShajyate | na kevalaM manuShyANAM satAM, kintu taduparya- pItyaperarthaH | tathA cha 'teShAM' manuShyANAM satAM devatApadayogyAnAM jIvAnAM padaprApteH pUrvaM manuShyasharIraM prAptAnAM satAM 'tasmAt' manuShyatvAt 'upari' manuShyasharIrApagamena 'tasyA upari' devopadevAdipadaprApteruparitanakAle.api devabhAvamApannAnAmapi vedavidyAdhikAro.astyeveti yojanA | kuta ityatastaddhetutayA sambhavAditi hetuM vyAchaShTe | 'hi' yataH | 'vedavidyAdhikAraH' ityatrApi sambadhyate | 'teShAM' devAnAm | adhikArasambhavo.api kuta ityato.atrApi sambhavAdityetadevAvR^ittya hetutayA yojayati - vishiShTeti || teShAmityatrApyanvIyate | tathA cha 'teShAM' yogyamanuShyANAM vidyAkarmabhyAM devAditvaprAptimatAM 'sambhavAt' vishiShTabuddhyAdibhAvAdarthagrahaNAnuShThAnopayuktabuddhivisheShAdisadbhAvA- dityarthaH | arthitvasAmarthye Adipadena grAhye | na chArthitvAbhAvaH ityatrApi teShAM sambhavati hItyeva hetuH | vidyAbhi- steShAM mokShasiddhiH sambhavati hIti tadarthaH | anena - sUtre tadityAvartate | manuShyaparAmarshi chedaM buddhisthaparAmarshi cha| apiH samuchchaye | adhikAra iti buddhyA vivichyAtrAnveti | anadhikArAdhikArAbhidhAyakajaiminibAdarAyaNoktirUpa- vipratipattisUchanAya bAdarAyaNapadam | tattvapradIparItyA tAtparyaj~nApanArthamadhikArAdhikyaj~naptidArDhyArthaM cha bAdarAyaNaH svayameva vaktItyAha iti vA | sambhavAditi chAvartate | tathA cha yato na kevalaM devAdipadayogyajIvAnAM padaprApteH pUrvaM bhUmau kiJNchitkAlaM manuShyANAM satAM tasyAM dashAyAmeva adhikAraH, kintu 'taduparyapi' tasmAnmanuShyatvAdupari tadatyayena tAbhyAM vidyAkarmabhyAM tasyAH devAditvaprApteruparitanakAle.api devabhAvamApannAnAmapi 
vedavidyAyAmadhi- kAro.astyeva | na cha tatkAraNAbhAvaH | 'sambhavAt' adhikAropayogino vishiShTabuddhyAdesteShu sambhavAt | na cha devAdInAM vishiShTabuddhisAmarthyasadbhAve.apyarthitvAbhAvAdadhikArAbhAva iti vAchyam | kutaH? 'sambhavAt' vidyAsAdhya- j~nAnamokShayorarthitvasambhavAditi bhagavAn bAdarAyaNo manyata iti sUtrArtha ukto bhavati |
(4) nanu na devA vedavidyAdhikAriNaH, tathA sati sUtre.amanuShyamAtravyAvartakamanuShyapadaprayogena tiryagAdi- vadamanuShyatvAnna devA vedavidyAdhikAriNa ityanumAnasUchanAttadvirodhApatterityata Aha - tiryagAdInAmiti || Adipadena sthAvarANi mUDhamanuShyA vA gR^ihyante | 'tadabhAvAt' vishiShTabuddhyAderabhAvAt 'abhAvaH' tasya vedavidyAdhikArasya | anenAdhikArAbhAve vishiShTabuddhyAdirAhityasya prayojakatvoktyA paroktAmanuShyatvahetoH sopAdhikatvaM sAdhyavyatireka- sAdhakopAdhivyatirekAkhyapratipakShagrastatvaM choktaM bhavati | sautramanuShyapadaM cha mananAdishIlaparaM sat vishiShTa- buddhyAdirahitameva chetanaM vyAvartayati, na tu martyabhinnamAtramiti na tadvirodha iti bhAvaH | nanu vishiShTabuddhyAdi- rAhityamupAdhiH | tiryakShu adhikArAbhAvarUpasAdhyAvyApakatvAt | ata eva na tadabhAvo.api sAdhyavyatirekahetu- rityata Aha - teShAmapIti || apirubhayatrAnveti | tatrAdyassamuchchaye | adhikAra iti sheShaH | tathA cha na kevalaM devAnAM, kintu 'teShAM' tirashchAmapyadhikAre.api na virodhaH nanu kathamavirodhastiryakShu sarvatra vedAdhikAre mAna- virodhApAtAdityata Aha - teShAmapIti || tirashchAM madhye.apItyarthaH | 'yatra' yeShu vishiShTabuddhyarthitvAkhya- rAgAdibhAvaH tatsattvaM tatraivAdhikAre 'avirodho' mAnAvirodhaH | bAdho na sarvatretyarthaH | anenApinA sautro.apishabdo jaritAryAdisamuchchAyakashcheti sUchitam | yadAha tattvapradIpikAkAraH - 'teShAmapItyAdirapipadavyAkhyA' iti | AnandamAlAkAro.api - 'tiryaJNcho.api kechidapishabdagR^ihItAH' ityAha | tathA cha manuShyabhinneShvapi tiryakShvadhikAra- sadbhAvAdvyabhichArAdadhikArAbhAve nAmanuShyatvaM hetuH, kintu vishiShTabuddhyAdirAhityamevAvyabhichArAt | ato bhavatyeva sa upAdhiH | ata eva sautramanuShyapadasya vyAvarttyasaN^kocho.api yukta iti bhAvaH |
(5) nanu kathaM tirashchAmapyadhikAre.apyavirodhaH | teShAmadhikAraniShedhasya taddarshanasya vA virodhitvAdityA- shaN^kya nAdya ityAha - niShedheti || teShAmityatrApi sambadhyate | adhikAre ityAdau saMyojyam | tena niShedharAhitye sati vishiShTabuddhyAdimattvamevAdhikAre prayojakam, na kevalaM yena shUdrAdau vyabhichAraH syAditi sUchitam | na dvitIya ityAha - dR^ishyante hIti || vedAdhikAritayeti sheShaH | hishabdo bhAratAdiprasiddhisUchakaH | ata eva bhArate -
evamukto bhrAtR^ibhistu jaritArirvibhAvasum |
tuShTAva prAJNjalirbhUtvA yattachChR^iNu narAdhipa ||
ityAdinA jaritArisArisR^ikkastambamitradroNAkhyeShu pakShiShu madhye jaritAriragrajaH svabhrAtR^ibhirasmAnmochayeti prArthitaH 'ayamagne jaritA' (R^i.10-142-1.) ityAgneyasUktenAgniM stutvA khANDavavanadahane svabhrAtR^InagnidAhAdamochayaditi pratipAditam | yata ityarthe vA hishabdaH | atra jaritAryAdaya ityeva pATho yuktaH, na tu jaritaryAdaya iti hrasvayukta- pAThaH, bhAratavirodhAt, tattvapradIpavirodhAchcheti dhyeyam | dR^ishyante hItyanena - devA vedavidyAdhikAriNaH niShedha- rAhitye sati vishiShTabuddhyAdimattvAt tAdR^ishamartyavaditi siddhAntyabhimatAnumAne manuShyatvopAdhirnirasto bhavati | jaritArau AdishabdagR^ihItasArisR^ikkAdau cha sAdhyAvyApaktavAt | 
(6) devAnAM vedavidyAdhikArasiddhyarthaM taduparItyanenoktaM sAditvamAkShipya samAdadhatsUtraM paThitvA.a.akShepAMshaM tAvadvyAchaShTe - virodha iti || manuShyA eveti | devAdipadayogyA jIvAH pUrvaM bhUmau kiJNchitkAlaM manuShyAH santa eva atha devAdayo bhavantItyarthaH | na tu manuShyabhAvaM vinetyevashabdArthaH | ityuktamiti || atroktamityanantaraM tada- yuktamiti sheShaH | kuta ityatastatpakShe bAdhakoktiparaM virodha ityaMshaM sahetukaM vyAchaShTe - tatrayadIti || yadItyArabhya bhavantItyantaM pUrvavAkyArthAnuvAdastasyApAdakatvapradarshanArthaH | tatretyavyayaM tarhItyarthakaM bhavantItyataH paraM yojyam | yadvA - manuShyA eva devAdayo bhavantItyantaM pUrvavAkyArthAnuvAdastasyApAdakatvapradarshanArthaH | tatretyavyayaM tarhItyarthakaM bhavantItyataH paraM yojyam | yadvA - manuShyA eva devAdayo bhavantItyuktyA prAptAbhedashaN^kAM vArayituM manuShyA evetyAdisvapadAni varNayati - tatreti || yadvA - tatra devatoddiShTakarmaNIti sAmAnAdhikaraNyam | atra pakShe yadIti shravaNAttarhIti labhyate | bhavantItyanantaramityuktamityasti | ubhayatrAdipadenopadevAdayo gR^ihyante | karmapadaM shabdasyA- pyupalakShakam | tathA cha yadi pUrvaM manuShyAH santo.apyatha devAdayo bhavantItyuktamityuchyate, tarhi 'tatpUrvaM' tebhyaH pUrvaM teShAM devAdipadaprApteH pUrvaM sAdhakatvAvasthAyAM 'devatAbhAvAt' devatAyA asattvAt yena karmaNA devAditvaM sAdhya- mityuktam, 'tatra' tasminneva 'devatoddiShTakarmaNi' pUrvakalpe devatoddeshena pravR^ittakarmaNi devatAvAchakashabde cha 'virodhaH' tayorvaiyarthyamiti yojanA | uddeshyAbhAvAdvAchyAbhAvAchcheti bhAvaH |
(7) parihArAMshaM vyAchaShTe - neti || idaM chAvartate | yojanA tu - na karmaNi virodha, kutaH? yato na pUrvaM devatAbhAva iti | teShAM pravAhato.anAditvenaitaddevAnAM pUrvamabhAve.api devatAntarasadbhAvAditi bhAvaH | na cha tatra pramANAbhAva ityataH prAptamaneketyaMshaM pratipattishabdasya j~nAnArthatvabhramaM vArayan tatsambandhipradarshanapUrvakaM vyAchaShTe - anekeShAmiti || 'tehanAkam' (tai.A.3-12.) iti shrutau 'anekeShAm' ekaikagaNasho.anantAnAM devatvAdiyogya- manuShyANAM vidyAkarmabhyAM pUrvapUrvadevatApadaprApterdarshanAdityarthaH | 
anenataduparItyatroktaM devAnAM sAditvamayuktaM, tathA sati yena karmaNA devAditvaM sAdhyamityuktam, tatra karmaNi shabde cha virodhastasya vaiyarthyaM syAt tatpUrvaM devatA- bhAvAditi chet - na, yato na pUrvaM devatA.abhAvaH | tatkatham? etaddevAnAM pUrvamabhAve.api devAntarasadbhAvAt | na cha tatra mAnAbhAvaH | 'anekapratipatterdarshanAt' anekeShAM yogyamanuShyANAM pUrvapUrvapadaprApteH 'teha nAkam' ityatro- ktatvAditi sUtrArtha ukto bhavati | shrutau 'yaj~nena yaj~namayajanta devAH | tAni dharmANi prathamAnyAsan' iti pUrvavAkye prakR^itAH devAstachChabdena gR^ihyante | hashabdaH punararthe prasiddhau vA | tathA cha ye 'devAH' devatvayogyAH manuShyA j~nAna- karmAtmakena 'yaj~nena' 'yaj~naM' viShNum 'ayajanta' apUjayan | tatastena j~nAnapUrvakakarmaNA devapadaM prApya 'prathamAni' prathamAH mukhyAH 'dharmANi' dharmAH lokadhArakA Asan | 'mahimAnaH' mahAtmAnaH mahimaguNAtmakA vA | 'te' devAH 'ha' punaH anantaraM svAdhikArAvasAne 'nAkaM' kaM sukhaM tadanyat duHkhamakaM, tanneti nAkaM, naJNdvayena pUrNasukhAtmakamiti labhyate | evaMbhUtaM mokShaM 'sachante' Apnuvan | laN^arthe laT | laN^vA, etvADabhAvau ChAndasau | 'yatra' mokShe 'pUrve' pUrvakalpe muktAH 'sAdhyAH' bahuvachanamAdyarthe |
R^ijavo brahmamukhyA hi suparNashsheSha eva cha |
sarasvatI suparNI cha vAruNI sAdhyanAmakAH ||
ityuktAH sAdhyAdayo devAH santIti shrutyarthaH | na cha vasurudrAdityamarutsAdhyeShu vasUnAmAditvAt TIkAyAM vasvAdidevA iti vaktavyam, na tu sAdhyAdIti | ata eva tattvapradIpe 'pUrve sAdhyAH vasvAdayo devAH pUrvasiddhA muktA vA' ityuktamiti vAchyam | sAdhyashabditAnAM prAdhAnyena kramollaN^ghanAt | ChandogashrutikramAnusAreNa tattvapradIpa- pravR^itteH| na chaivaM vyAkhyAne puruShArthAdhikaraNe.asyAH prAptapadevatAparatvenodAharaNAnupapattiriti vAchyam | ye padaM prApya jagaddhArakA abhUvan te devA yaj~nena yaj~namayajanta te ha nAkaM mokShagatAtishayaM sachante iti shruterarthAntaravivakShayA tadupapattestadanusAreNa taTTIkAyAM vyAkaraNasyApyupapatteshcha |
(8) yaddevAnAmadhikArasiddhyartham AdyantavattvamuktaM taduparyaneketyAbhyAM, tadAkShipya samAdadhatsUtraM paThitvA.a.a- kShepAMshaM tAvadvyAchaShTe - shabda iti || anekapratipatterdarshanAnna virodha ityAdyanuShajyate | yaditarhyorapyanuShaN^gaH | tathA chetthaM yojanA - yadyanekeShAM pUrvapUrvamuktyA devatApadaprApterdarshanAnna karmaNi virodha iti uchyate, tarhi tatraiva shabde darshanapadokte vede.aprAmANyAkhyo virodhaH syAt | kutaH? devAnAmanityatvAt | aneketyAdinA devAnAmanityatva- syAntavattvasyoktatvAt | nanu devAnAmanityatve.api vedAnAmaprAmANyaM kuta ityataH - taduditAnAmityAha | hetugarbha- visheShaNametat | anenAnityadevavAchakatvAditi hetuH sUchitaH | nanu devAnAmanityatve.api na tadvAchakavedasya vAchyahInatvarUpAprAmANyaM prasajyate, devavadvAchakavedasyApyanityatvena kadApi vAchyahInatvAbhAvAdityata uktaM 
- vedasya nityatvAditi || vedasya nityatvameva kuta ityata uktaM - vAcheti || shruterityasya vedasya natyatvAdityanenAnvayaH | j~nAnopalakShakaM chaitat | Adishabdena 'nityayAnityayA' (pauShyAyaNashrutiH) 'nityA vAva shrutiH' ityAdikaM gR^ihyate | nanu na nityo vedaH | na cha shrutivirodhaH, shruterbahukAlInatvarUpanityatvArthakatvenopacharitArthatvAdityato.apyAha | tathA sati vedasyAnityatvAdaprAmANyAkhyavirodhaH syAditi | nanu vedasyAnityatve.apyAptimUlatvena prAmANyaM sambhava- tItyata Aha - AptyanishchayAditi || vedakarturiti sheShaH | tathA cha kartuH sArvaj~nAdau mAnAbhAvena vedakartuH sArvaj~nAdirUpAptyanishchayAdityarthaH | yadvA - astu vA kartaryAptinishchayaH, tathApi na vede tanmUlatvanishchaya ityAha - AptyanishchayAditi || vedasyetyAkR^iShyate | tathA cha vedasyAptapraNItatvarUpAptimUlatvAnishchayAdityarthaH | tasmAnmA- nAbhAvenAptitanmUlatvAnishchayAdvedAnityatve tatprAmANyAbhAvApatteH na nityatvashruterupacharitArthatvaM vAchyamiti bhAvaH | na kevalaM shrutervedanityatvasiddhiH, kintu parisheShAnumAnAdapItyAha - nityatveti || mUlapramANasya nityatvApekShatvA- dvedasya nityatvAvagamAdityanvayaH | ayaM bhAvaH - prAmANyasiddhyarthaM vedasyAptapraNItatve mUlapramANena bhAvyaM, pauruSheyasya mUlapramANasApekShatvaniyamAt | anyathA.anAshvAsAdyaj~nAdeH puNyasAdhanatAdibodhakaM vedamUlaM cha bhavatpratyakShA- numAnayorasambhavAtparisheShAdvAkyameveti vAchyaM, tasya chAnityatAmupetya mUlAnveShaNe.anavasthApattyA nityatvameva vAchyaM, tato varaM vedasyaiva nityatvAN^gIkaraNaM, shrutisiddhatvAditi |
(9) nanu yathA vedAnityatve AptyanishchayAtprAmANyAbhAvApattirbAdhikA, tathA tasya nityatve.apyAptoktatva- rUpaguNajanyatvAbhAvena prAmANyAbhAvApattiriti samaM bAdhakamityata Aha - svata iti || vedasyetyanuvartate | tathA cha 'vedasya' vedajanyaj~nAnagatayAthArthyarUpaprAmANyasya 'svata eva' j~nAnasAmAnyakAraNAdeva 'prasiddheH' upapatteH pramitatvA- dityarthaH | yadvA - vedagatayathArthaj~nAnakaraNatvarUpakaraNaprAmANyasya 'svata eva' j~nAnakaraNatvasahajashaktyabhinnayathArtha- j~nAnajanakatvashaktirUpatvenaiva pramitatvAdityarthaH | asyApi vedasya nityatvasambhavAdityanenAnvayaH | tathA cha vedasya nityatvasya siddhatvAttadvAchyadevAnAmanityatve vAchyahInatvarUpAprAmANyApattiriti bhAvaH |
(10) nanvatItakalpe ekadevatA.abhAve devatAntarasadbhAvAdyathA karmaNyuddeshyAbhAvanimitto virodho nAsti, tathAtrApyekadevatAnAshe.api punaranyadevatotpattisambhavAnna vAchyahInatvAkhyo virodha ityata Aha - punaranyabhAvaniyamA- bhAvAchcheti| pUrvakalpIyanAshAnantaramityAnantaryArthe punashshabdaH | uttarakalpa ityarthe vA | anyabhAvaH anyotpattiH | tasya niyame pramANAbhAvAdityarthaH | atItadevatApravAhe tu pramANamastIti vaiShamyamiti bhAvaH | anenottarakAle devatAbhAvavirodhaH karmaNyapi samAna iti sautrashabdashabdena karmApyupalakShaNIyamityuktaM bhavati | na chaivamatrApi virodha- padAkarShaNamiti TIkavirodhaH | 'tadupari' itisUtrAdaperanukarShokteH tasya cha na kevalaM shabde uttarakAle devatAbhAva- virodhaH, karmaNyapItyetadarthakatvAditi vAchyam | AkarShaNashabdasyAnvayArthatvamAshritya na kevalaM pUrvasUtre virodha- 
padAnvayaH, kintvetatsUtre.apIti TIkArthAN^gIkAreNa apivirodhapadayorAkarShaNamityarthAnabhyupagamAt | astu vA dvandvaH, tathApi nAnupapattiH, apeH svarUpanityatvAbhAve.apItyarthAbhyupagamena karmasamuchchayArthatvAnabhyupagamAt | ata eva TIkAyAM devAnAM svarUpanityatvAbhAve.apItyuktiH | atra nityatvasAdhakayoH shrutyanumAnayoH samuchchaye ekashchashabdaH | anityatvabAdhakasya nityatve tadabhAvasya cha samuchchaye.anyaH | anityatvAnyabhAvaniyamAbhAvayoH samuchchaye.apara iti vivekaH |
'tasmai nUnamabhidyave vAchA virUpa nityayA |
vR^iShNe chodasva suShTutim' (R^i. 8-64-6.)
iti R^igyajurmantrArthastu na vilakShaNatvAdhikaraNaTIkAyAmuktaH | tatra yadyapi virUpeti svAtmAnaM prati sambodhanamityukteH viShNutattvanirNayaTIkAyAM virUpAkhyaR^iNessambodhanamityukteshcha virodho bhAti | tathApi virUparShikartR^ikaM svAntaryAmisambodhanamiti tadarthAbhyupagamAnna virodhaH | uktaM hi tattvapradIpe - prerayeti prArthanaM virUpasya R^iSherantaryAmiviShayamiti | virUpakartR^ikaM taduddeshyakaM sambodhanamiti pakShe.api svAtmashabditasvajIvaM pratisambodhanamiti TIkArthAbhyupagamAnna virodhaH | asmin pakShe tattvapradIpoktaM vyAkhyAnAntaraM bhaviShyati | na cha padmanAbhatIrthakR^itaviShNutattvanirNayaTIkAyAM nyAyaratnAvalyAM dharmeNa virUparShiM pratyetaduchyata ityuktatvAttadvirodha iti vAchyam | prathamaM yamadR^iShTasya mantrasyAnantaraM virUpeNApi dR^iShTatvasambhavena tadA svasambodhanasambhavenAvirodhAt | tathA cha he virUpa abhito dyauH prakAsho yasyAsAvabhidyuH, tasmai 'vR^iShNe' varShiNe atisamarthAyeti vA | tattvapradIparItyA vR^iShA shreShThastasya chaturthI vR^iShNe iti vA | tasmai bhagavate enamuddishya 'nUnaM' nishchitaM 'nityayA' anAdinidhanayA veda- lakShaNavAchA 'suShTutiM' shobhanAM stutiM 'chodasva' preraya kurvityarthaH |
(11) parihArAMshaM vyAkhyAti - neti || virodha ityasti | tathA cha vedasya vAchyahInatvaprayuktAprAmANyA- khyavirodho netyarthaH | kuta ityataH prAptaM prabhavAditi hetuM tatsambandhipradarshanapUrvakaM pravAhataHprabhavaniyamaparatayA cha vyAchaShTe - teShAM prabhavaniyamAditi | 'teShAM' vedavAchyadevAnAM 'prabhavasya' pravAhatautpatteH 'niyamAt' pratikalpaM niyame- notpatteriti yAvat | tathA cha devAnAM svarUpeNa nityatvAbhAve.api pravAharUpeNa nityatvAnna tadvAchakavedAprAmANyamiti bhAvaH | nanu pramANAbhAvAdasiddho heturityataH prAptamataHshabdamanUdya sAvadhAraNatvena vyAchaShTe - ata eva shabdAditi | ko.asau shabda ityato yasminvirodhaH shaN^kitastasmAdeva, nAnyasmAdaprakR^itAdityAshayena tadudAharati - sUryetyAdinA | shruto.asmin kalpe.apIti sheShaH | nanUtpAdakAbhAva ityato.apyAha - ata eveti | akAravAchyAt shrutyuktAddhAtu- rviShNoreva, nAnyasmAdityarthaH | asmin pakShe atashshabdAditi 
vyAkhyAnAntaram | nanvakalpayaditi laN^.hyogAdiyaM shrutiratItaviShayaiva, ato na devaprabhavaniyamaM pramApayatItyato.apyAha - ata eveti | tathA cha dhAtA yathA pUrvakalpe sUryAchandramasAvakalpayat tathA.asminkalpe.apIti pratikalpaM shrutyA kathane devAnAM sarvakalpeShu prajananAkhyasadbhAvasiddhe- radhyAhAraM vinA ataevashabdAt buddhisthAt yathaiveti spaShTashrutyantarAchcha teShAM sarvakalpeShu prabhavasiddhernoktachodyAvakAsha iti bhAvaH | nanu shrutAvupachAreNApyuktiH sambhavatIti na tayA devaprabhavaniyamanishchaya ityataH prAptaM pratyakShetyaMshaM vyAchaShTe - mahatAmiti | atItAnAgatavidAmityarthaH | asyApi teShAM prabhavaniyamAdityanenAnvayaH | nanu parapratyakSha- syApratyakShatvAttadanishchaya ityatopyAha - mahatAM pratyakShAditi |
yathartuShvR^ituliN^gAni nAnArUpANi paryaye |
dR^ishyante tAni tAnyeva tathA bhAvA yugAdiShu ||
ityAdirUpAt 'mahatAM' bhAratAchAryANAM 'pratyakShAt' pratyakShavachanAdityarthaH | asmin pakShe 'pratyakShAt' nishchitAtpratyakShAdityanvayaH |
(12) nanvayoginAM shrutipratyakShayoravishvAsena teShAM devaprabhavanishchayAbhAva ityataH prAptamanumAnetyaMshaM vyAchaShTe - yatheti | idAnIntanakAle yathA devAssanti tathoparibhAvikAle.api devA bhaviShyantItItareShAM mahadbhyo.anyevA- mayoginAmanumAnAdityarthaH | asyApi prabhavaniyamAdityanenAnvayaH | chashabdaH prabhavaniyame, shabdapratyakShAnumAnAkhya- pramANatrayasamuchchaye vakShyamANayuktyantarasamuchchaye cha | anumAnAkArastu - uparitanakAlo devavAn apralayakAlatvAt idAnIntanakAlavaditi | anena - devAnAmadhikArasiddhyarthaM yadyAdyantavattvamabhyupagamyate, tarhi pUrvasUtre yadbalA- tpUrvapUrvadevatApravAhasyAnAditvamuktaM, tasmin 'shabde' 'vAchA virUpa nityayA' ityAdishrutau nityatayA siddhe vede karmaNi chottarakalpe vAchyoddeshyahInatvarUpAprAmANyAkhyo virodhaH syAditi chet - na, kutaH? 'prabhavAt' devAnAM sarva- kalpeShu prabhavaniyamAnnityamenopapatteH | teShAM pravAhato nityatvAditi yAvat | na chotpAdakAbhAvaH | 'ato' viShNo- reva prabhavAt | na chAsiddhiH | 'ato' 'dhAtA yathApUrvam' (mahAnA. 5-7.) itiprakR^itAchChabdAchChruteH 'yathA' iti spaShTashruteshcha | tathA mahatAmatItAnAgatakAlavidAM yoginAM 'pratyakShAt' 'yatharturShu' iti pratyakShavachanAt j~nApitAt mahatAmatItAnAgatakAlayordevaprabhavaniyamagrAhipratyakShAt | tathA mahadbhyaH itareShAmayoginAmanumAnAchcha tatsiddheriti sUtrArtha ukto bhavati | 'yathaiva' iti shrutyarthastu - yathA pUrvayugAtyaye kalpAtyaye vA punaryugakalpAntarotpattiriti kAle prabhavaniyamaH, tathA surAderdevopadevAdeH pUrvapUrvakalpAtyaye punaranyabhAvaniyamo.asti | yathoktam -
sa hi vishvasR^ijo vibhushambhupurandarasUryamukhAnaparAnaparAn |
sR^ijatIDyatamo.avati hanti nijaM padamApayati praNatAnsudhiyA ||
iti | pratikalpamiti sheShaH | tasmAtpUrvakalpa ivottarakalpe.api pUrvakalpasadR^ishasarvotpattiniyamAdeva 'tasmAt' viShNossakAshAdetadvishvaM 'kvApi' kadApi 'anIdR^ishaM' pUrvapUrvavisadR^ishaM devatAprabhavashUnyaM na bhaviShyati, kintu tatsa- dbhAvopetameva bhaviShyatIti | yadvA - 'etat' chetanAchetanAtmakaM vishvamanIdR^ishaM na bhaviShyati, kintu nAmarUpAbhyA- mIdR^ishameva bhaviShyatItyarthaH | tattvapradIpe tviyaM shrutiH 'yathaiva kAlaniyamaH' iti vyatyAsena paThitA |
(13) yuktyantareNa devapravAhasya nityatAM sAdhayatsUtraM paThitvA vyAchaShTe - ataeveti || ataevetyanuvAdaH | tasya vyAkhyAnaM - 'shabdasya' vedasya nityatvAdeveti | evakAreNa na devapravAhanityatve yuktyantaraM gaveShaNIyaM, kintu yatpUrvapakShiNA vedanityatvaM sapramANakamuktaM, tata eva tadanyathA.anupapataà¤¼à¥tyaitatsidhyatIti sUchayati | nityatvAdevetyupa- lakShaNaM, pramANasya sAdhitatvenAprAmANyAbhAvAdevetyapi ataHshabdavyAkhyAnaM draShTavyam | anyathA pUrvapakShI aprAmANye- nAnyathopapattiM brUyAt devapravAhasya | yuktamiti cha sUtrasheShoktiH | 'yuktaM' vedanityatvAnyathA.anupapattyAkhya- yuktisiddham | chashabdastu samuchchetavyayuktInAM shabdAtpratyakShAdanumAnAdityanena darshitatvAttatsamuchchayArthakatayA.a- rthAdvyAkhyAtaH | ataeva pUrvasUtrabhAShye chashabdaH saMyojitaH | atrApi bhAShye chashabdena cha tadvAchyadevatAsvarUpasyaiva nityatvena anyathopapattiH | ataeva 'sUryAchandramasau' (mahAnA.5-7.) 'yathaiva' ityAdyudAhR^itashrutereva 'yamapyeti bhuvanaM sAmparAye' (nR^i.pU.2-5.) 'yatprayantyabhisaMvishanti' (tai.3-1.) ityAdi bahulaM pralayashruteshcha sUryAdidevAnAmutpatti- nAshAvagamAt, ataeva svarUpanityatvAyogena pravAharUpeNaiva teShAM nityatvAvashyaMbhAvAdityAdiTIkoktArthaH sarvo.api saN^gR^ihItaH |
(14) nanu na devAnAM pravAhanityatvenApi vedaprAmANyopapattiH | tathA hi - kiM pUrvakalpe muktA eva devA uttarakalpe punarAvartante, tadanye vA | nAdyaH | mukterapunarAvR^ittitvAt | na dvitIyaH | tathAtve dharmibhUta- devAnityatvahetukavirodhAbhAve.api nAmarUpAdidharmavaichitryakR^itavirodhaprApteH, vAchakavedasya pratikalpaM pAThabhedAbhAvenaika- vidhatvAt, anyathA nityatvavyAghAtAt | vAchyadevAnAM cha nAnAvidhanAmarUpavattvAdityAshaN^kAM pariharatsUtramupanyasya vyAchaShTe - samAneti || atrAtItapadaM prAchInaparam | anAgatapadaM cha tadanyabhaviShyadvartamAnaparam | dharmiprati- yogyubhayasamarpakametat | nAma indrAdi, rUpam AkR^itiH | sUtrAnusArAdatrApi chashabdaH saMyojyaH | samAnadharmakarmava- ttvAchcheti tadarthaH | 
svapadeShvati sheShaH | muktyA.a.avR^ittAvapItyuktiH pUrvapakShyAshaN^kitavirodhe hetusUchanArthA | yadyapi- tathA.apItyarthe.apishabdaH Avartate | shabda ityasti | tathA chetthaM yojanA - 'prAptapadAnAM' prAchInAnAM devAnAM 'muktyA' prAptamuktitvena kAraNena punasteShAmeva svapadeShu 'avR^ittAvapi' asattve.api tadanyeShAM tatra satve.api cha 'avirodhaH' ma tadvAchake ekavidhe.api shabde vede.aprAmANyAkhyo virodhaH | kutaH? vAchyAnAmapyatItAnAgatAnAM devAnAM parasparaM 'samAnanAmarUpatvAt' samAne ekavidhe nAmarUpe yeShAM te tathoktAH, teShAM bhAvastattvaM tasmAditi | chandrikAyAM tu - sUtre bhAShye cha tattvapradIpAnusArAdAvR^ittAviti vichChedaM bhAShye muktyAvR^ittAvityasyaikapadyaM chAshritya ekasya padaprAptAvanyasya muktiH, punastasya muktau punaranyasya padaprAptiriti krameNa mukterAvR^ittAvapIti vA, svasvapadasyAvR^ittAvapIti veti TIkAnuktaprakAradvayenApyAvR^ittAvityaMsho vyAkhyAtaH |
(15) nanu sarvadevAnAM samAnanAmarUpatve pramANAbhAvAdasiddho heturityataH prAptaM darshanAdityaMshaM vyAkhyAti -yatheti || 'dhAtA yathApUrvam' iti shruterityarthaH |
(16) nanvetachChrutestattatsvarUpakalpanAniyamaparatvamapi sambhavatIti nAnayA samAnanAmarUpatvanishchayo bhavati| kiM cha devapravAhasya nityatve teShAM samAnanAmarUpatve vA na tadvAchitvena nityavedaprAmANyopaptiH, tadvAchitvasyai- vAsambhavAt | na hyapauruSheyasya vedasyaitAvatkAlamayaM devo mayoktaH, ataH paramenaM vakShyAmIti vimR^ishya vR^ittiH sambhavatItyataH prAptaH smR^iterityaMsha ityAshayena tAM darshayati - anAdIti || nityatvokterupacharitatvavAraNAya - anAdinidhanetyuktam | ato na paunaruktyam | ata eva tattvapradIpe anAdinidhanatvena nityA, na tvanidhanatva- mAtreNetyuktam | bahukAlInatvena vetspi draShTavyam | vedeShvityanantaramuktA iti sheShaH | nirmame ityasyAvR^ittiH | tatheti sheShaH | tenApyevashabdasyAnvayaH | tathA cha 'Adau' sR^iShTikAle 'svayambhuvA' svatantreNa maheshvareNa viShNunA 'anAdinidhanA nityA' AdyantashUnyatayaiva nityA, na tUpachAreNa bahukAlInatAmAtreNAnidhanatvamAtreNa nityA | yA 'vAk' vedarUpA 'utsR^iShTA' uchchAritA | 'tadvedashabdebhyaH' vedagatebhyaH tebhyaH shabdebhya eva, nAnyebhyaH, 'saH' maheshvaro viShNuH 'R^iShINAM' brahmAdivibudhAnAM 'nAmadheyAni nirmame' tAneva shabdAn teShu saN^ketitavAn pratikalpamayaM shabdo.atra shakta iti j~nApitavAn | 'yAshcha' R^iShINAM devAnAM vedeShUktAH dR^ishyante iti dR^iShTayo rUpANi, tAshcha tAni cha tathaiva pUrvakalpIyarUpasAdR^ishyenaiva nirmame iti smR^ityarthaH | chaH samuchchaye | darshanAtsmR^iterityanayoH samAnarUpatvA- dityanenAnvayaH | AgamopalakShakaM chaitat | tathA cha nAsiddhiriti bhAvaH | anena - prAchInAnAM devAnAM muktyA punaH svapadeShvavR^ittAvapi tadanyeShAM tatra vR^ittAvapi na tadvAchake ekavidhe.api shabde.aprAmANyAkhyo virodhaH | kutaH? prAchInAnAM tadanyeShAM chAnyonyaM 'samAnanAmarUpatvAt' tadyogyakarmadharmavattvAchcha | na cha hetvasiddhiH | 'darshanAt' 'yathA pUrvam' iti shruteH 'anAdinidhanA' iti smR^iteshcheti sUtrArtha ukto bhavati | atra tattvapradIpe pralaye kasyApi devasyAbhAvena tadA vedasya vAchyahInatvarUpAprAmANyamAshaN^kya 
bhagavanmAtraviShayatvena tadupapattiriti samAdhAnamabhipretya 'shabde' kadApi vAchyahInatvakR^ito virodhaH aprAmANyam | kutaH? mukhyavAchyasya viShNoH sarvadA vidyamAnatvAt | kuta etat? 'ata eva' shabdAtteShAM devAnAM prabhavaniyamAdikarturapIshasya sadA sattvAvagamAt| pratyakShashchAsau mahatAm| kutaH?
