'ataeva' 'puruShamIhate' 'kavayo vayanti' (mahAnA.1-3.) ityAdishrutereva itareShAmanumAnAchcha | yathA yena prakAreNedAnIM devA bhavanti tathA.anyadA.apItyanumAnAchcha tadavagamaH | evam 'ataeva' shabdanityatvAdeva pravoDhu- rnityatvam | tathA viShNossamAnanAmarUpatvAdanyeShAM tadabhAvAchcha 'avirodhaH' na tasya sarvashabdavAchyatvavirodhaH | samAnAni sadR^ishAni nAmAni yeShAM rUpANAM tAni tathoktAni, tAdR^ishAni rUpANi yasya sa tathoktaH tasya bhAvasta- smAt | na hi viShNvanyarUpANAM sadR^ishanAmarUpatvaM, shabdapravR^ittihetuvaikalyAt | na chAtra mAnAbhAvaH, 'yathApUrvam' iti darshanAt | yathA pUrvaM pUrNaj~nAnaH sarvasvatantraH sarvanAmarUpasthitastathaiva sa dhAtA sUryAdInakalpayaditi shruteH | ataH sUryAdiklR^ipteH prAgapi pralaye shabdaprAmANyAvirodha iti siddhamiti | idamevAbhipretya TIkAyAM 'na cha' ityAdinA shaN^kottare darshite | 'atItaviShayatvasya cha' iti parihArottaraM chAbhihitam |
(17) nanu na devAnAM vedavidyAdhikAro yuktaH | tathA hi dvividhA vedavidyAH - muktiphalArthAstaditaraphalArthA iti | mokShetaraphalA api dvividhAH | brahmakarmavidyAbhedAt | tatrAdyA yathA - madhuvidyA | dvitIyA yathA - agni- ShTomavidyA | tatra na tAvaddevAnAM mokShetaraphalakadvividhavidyAsvadhikAro yujyate, tatsAdhyAnAM mokShetaraphalAnAM madhye keShAJNchidyogyAnAM prAptatvena ayogyAnAM cha prAptumashakyatvena arthitvAbhAvAditi jaiminimatAvalambenAkShipatsUtramunyasya vyAchaShTe - madhvAdiShviti || prathamAdipadena shiShTavAkyaM, tathA 'devo bhUtvA devAnapyeti' (bR^i.6-1-2.) iti vAjasaneyavAkyaM, tathA 'sa UrjamupagachChati' iti shrutyantaravAkyaM, dvitIyamadhuvidyAntgataM 'rudrANAmevaiko bhUtvA' (ChAM. 3-7-2.) ityAdikaM cha gR^ihyate | prApyaphalatvAt aprApyaphalatvAdityubhayathA vichChedaH | asyobhayatrAnvayaH | vasvA- dipadAnAmiti sheShaH | tatrAdipadena devarudrAdipadAnAM grahaNam | yadvA - prAptapadAnAmityatratyaM padAnAmityetadbuddhyA vivichyAtra dharmitvena sambadhyate | prAptapadAnAmiti bahuvrIhiH, karmadhArayashcha | tatrAdyo hetugarbhavisheShaNarUpaH | dvitIyasyobhayatrAnvayaH | devAnAmiti sUtre adhyAhR^itaM padaM, prakaraNalabdhaM vA | madhushabdo 'madhu' ityupakramyA- mnAtaprathamadvitIyAdyamR^itavidyAparaH | atrAdishabdena vasvAdipadaphalakakarmavidyA vAjasaneyoktavAgAdividyAshcha gR^ihyante | etachchAvartanIyam | asambhavAditi sautro heturatrApi saMyojyaH | tadupapAdakoktyaiva taduktirbhavatIti tasya sAkShAda- nuktiH | yadvA - prAptapadAnAmaprApyaphalatvAdityuktyaiva tasyoktatvAdasambhavAditi na saMyojyam | tathA chetthaM bhAShya- yojanA - madhvAdividyAsu 'asau vA Adityo devamadhu' iti prastutyAmnAtena 'sa etadevAmR^itaM veda vasUnAmevaiko bhUtvA agninaiva mukhenaitadevAmR^itaM 
dR^iShTvA tR^ipyati' ityAdivAkye 'padAnAM' vasvAdipadAnAM 'prApyaphalatvAt' madhvAdi- vidyAsUktopAsanAprApyaphalatvashravaNAt 'prAptapadAnAM cha' vasvAdidevAnAM prAptasvasvapadatvena 'asambhavAt' tadarthitvA- sambhavAt 'devAnAM' devaiH prAptapadAnAM punastaiH 'aprApyaphalatvAt' aprArthyaphalatvAditi vA | dvitIyavidyAdyamR^ita- vidyAphalAnAM rudrAdipadAnAM cha vasvAdidevAnAm 'aprApyaphalatvAt' prAptumayogyaphalatvAt tatrApyarthitvAsambhavAtteShAM madhvAdividyAsu 'anadhikAram anadhikArAbhAvaM jaiminirmanyata' iti | jaiminigrahaNena Aptatamena jaimininaivaM matatvAchcha na teShAmadhikAra iti yuktyantaraM sUchyate | anena - 'madhvAdiShu' 'asau vA Adityo devamadhu' ityAdi- madhuvidyAsu devAnAm 'anadhikAram' anadhikArAbhAvaM jaiminirmanyate tasmAddhetoH 'asambhavAt' taistadvidyAsUktaphalAnAM madhye keShAJNchidyogyAnAM prAptatvena keShAJNchitprAptumayogyatvena teShAM tatrArthitvAsambhavAditi Aptatamo jaiminirmanyata iti sUtrArtha ukto bhavati |
ChAndogye hi - 'asau vA AdityaH' ityanena Adityasya viShNoH paramAnandatvena madhutvamuktvA 'sa etat' ityAdinA madhushabditasya bhagavata AdityamaNDalasya pUrvadakShiNapashchimottarordhvarashmiShu sthitAnAM prathamAmR^itAdishabda- paJNchakavAchyavAsudevasaN^karShaNapradyumnAniruddhanArAyaNAkhyapaJNcharUpANAM madhye prAchyAditattaddiksthataiH tattatpadayogyairvasu- rudrAdityamarutsAdhyapadoktaR^ijurUpapaJNchagaNasthairdevaiH krameNa agnivAyvindrasomaviriJNchapradhAnakaiH agnyAdimukhenaikaiko- pAstau kR^itAyAM tadaparokShaj~nAnajanitatatprasAdadvArA vasvAdipadaprAptistattadgaNasthAnAM bhavatItyuchyate | tathA cha 'yaH' adhikArI 'etat amR^itaM' vAsudevAkhyaM rUpam 'evam' uktaprakAreNa 'veda' 'sa cha vasUnAmapyeko bhUtvA' vasubhogyadeshakAlAdhipo bhUtvA 'agninA mukhena' tatprAdhAnyena tadupadesheneti yAvat | 'etadevAmR^itaM' vAsudevAkhyaM 'dR^iShTvA' sAkShAtkR^itya 'tR^ipyati' mukto bhavatItyarthaH | evaM 'yo' devatvayogyo adhikArI vAkprANachakShuHshrotra- manohR^idayanAmakaM brahmopAste sa devatvamapyeti tato 'devo bhUtvA' svottamadeveShu sAyujyaM prApya devAn shvetadvIpagatabhaga- vadrUpavisheShAn chaturmukhabrahmaNA sahApyeti | so.adhikArI 'Uraà¤¼à¥jam' annam 'upagachChati' yatheShTaM prApnoti iti shrutyantarArthaH |
(18) nanu mAstu mokShetaraphalavidyAsu adhikAro devAnAM, tathApi 'satyaM j~nAnamanantaM brahma' (tai.2-1-1.) ityAdimokShArthavidyAsvadhikAro bhaviShyati, tatrArthitvasambhavAt ityAshaN^kAM pariharatsUtraM paThitvA vyAchaShTe - jyoti- ShIti || jyotiShIti sUtrapadAnuvAdaH | tasya vyAkhyAnaM - sarvaj~natva iti | yadyapi j~nAne iti vyAkhyeyaM, tathApi viShayAvisheShitaj~nAnasyAnirUpyatvAt, yatkiJNchidviShayake j~nAne viShayatayA sarvabhAvasyAsiddhatvAt tajj~nApanAya sarvaj~natva iti vyAkhyAtam | tena sUtre vastUnAmityantarbhAvasambandhij~nApakaM padamadhyAhAryamiti sUchitaM bhavati | chaH samuchchaye | asya hetorasambhavAdityanuvR^ittahetudvArA madhvAdiShu anadhikAraM manyata iti pUrveNAnvayaH | anena 
madhvAdiShvityAdishabdena mokShArthavidyA api grAhyAH | jyotishshabdashcha AvartanIyaH jyotiShIva jyotiShIti | saptamI cha chaitrarathasya buddhau shAstrArtha itivat yujyate iti sUchitam | kathaM vastUnAM j~nAne antarbhAva ityataH sarvaj~natve bhAvA- diti svapade varNayati - Aditya iti | sarvavastUnAmAdityaprakAshe antarbhAvavat tadgR^ihItatvavat tajj~nAne taduparIti prastutadevatAkartR^ikaj~nAne sarvavastUnAm 'antarbhAvAt' viShayIbhUtatvAdityarthaH | abhiprAyaM vyanakti - nityeti | devAnAM sArvaj~nena 'vidyAnAM' sarvabrahmakarmavidyAsAdhyaj~nAnAnAM 'nityasiddhatvAt' niyamena prAptatvAdityarthaH | yadvA - 'vidyAnAM' j~nAnasAdhanavidyAnAM nityaM niyamena 'siddhatvAt' upalabdhatvAdityarthaH | devAnAM vedadraShTR^itvAditi bhAvaH | yadvA - 'vidyAnAM' mokShataditaraphalasAdhanaj~nAnasAdhanavidyoktArthAnAM 'nityasiddhatvAt' niyamena tairj~nAtatvAdityarthaH | tathA cha na devAnAmubhayavidyAsAdhyaj~nAne.arthitA sambhavatIti bhAvaH | anayorapi paJNchamyantayoH pUrvavadanvayaH | na chAsya hetoH pUrvasUtroktAsambhavahetUpapAdakatvAt kathamatra chashabda iti vAchyam | pUrvaM phalamukhena atra cha sAdhanamukhena arthitvA- sambhavasya abhipretatvena asya hetordvitIyAsambhavopapAdakatve.api asambhavasAmAnye upapAdakatvena chashabdopapatteH | yadyapi bhAShye 'jyotiShi' iti sUtraM kiM devAnAM mokShetaraphalArthAyAm? uta mokShaphalArthAyAM vidyAyAmadhikAra iti pakShadvaye.api sAdhAnamukhena doShoktiparatayA pratIyate | TIkAyAM tu mokShArthavidyAyAmapi na devAnAmadhikAraH, tatra phale.arthitAsattve.api tatsAdhanavidyopAsanAtmakaj~nAne.arthitvAbhAvAt, vidyAyAshcha j~nAnArthatvAt, j~nAnasya cha prAptatvA- diti dvitIyapakShamAtradoShoktiparatayA vyAkhyAtam | tathA cha visaMvAdo bhavati | tathApi mokShetaraphalakavidyA- svanadhikAra iti prAchInapakShe na kevalaM madhuvidyAphale vasutvAdau prAptatvAt devAnAmarthitvAbhAvAt tadvidyAyA- madhikArAbhAvo doShaH | kintu vasutvAdiphalasAdhanaj~nAne.apyarthitvAbhAvAt adhikArAbhAva ityasambhavadoShe upapAdakA- ntaramuktaM bhavatIti TIkAyAmuktatvAnna visaMvAdaH | ata eva na chashabdAnupapattiH | prAchInapakShavivakShayA tadupapatteH | hetvantareNa etatsAdhayatIti sattarkadIpAvalI cha AdyapakShavivakShayA pravR^ittA | dvividhavidyAsamuchchaye vA chashabdaH | anena - na kevalaM mokShetaraphalArthaM madhvAdiShvanadhikAraM manyate jaiminiH | kintu Adishabdena vA AvR^ittajyotishshabdena vA gR^ihItAyAM 'satyaM j~nAnam' iti mokShArthavidyAyAmapi | kutaH? 'jyotiShIva' AdityaprakAshe iva 'jyotiShi' sarvaviShayakadevatAj~nAne sarvavastUnAM viShayatayA 'bhAvAt' mokShasAdhanaj~nAnasya siddhatvAt | ata eva na mokShe, tasyApi siddhaprAyatvAdarthitvAsambhavAt | na kevalaM vasvAdidevAnAM phale.arthitvAbhAvAt madhvAdiShvanadhikAraM jaiminirmanyate, kintu 'jyotiShi' vasutvAdiphalasAdhanaj~nAne.apyarthitvAsambhavAt | so.api kutaH? 'jyotiShi' devAnAM j~nAne 'bhAvAt' sarveShAM vastUnAM viShayatayA antarbhAvAtphalasAdhanaj~nAnasya siddhatvAditi yAvaditi vA sUtrArtha ukto bhavati |
(19) evaM devairmokShetarayogyaphalAnAM prAptatvAt ayogyAnAM prAptumashakyatvAt mokShasyApi 
brahmaj~nAnitvena arthato labdhatvAdarthitvAbhAvena teShAM kAsvapi vidyAsu adhikArAbhAve jaiminimatAvalambinA samarthite punaradhikAraM samarthayatsUtraM paThitvA vyAchaShTe - bhAvamiti || phalavisheShabhAvAdityanena sUtre pUrvasmAdbhAvAdityasya anuvR^ittiH sUchitA | prAptapadAnAmiti | padyata iti padaM prApyaphalamAtram | apItyanena visheShArtho.api | tushabdo.apyarthaH | apishcha yadyapi tathA.apItyarthe ityuktaM bhavati | devAnAmiti sUtre sheShoktiH | madhvAdiShvityanuvR^ittapadAnuvAdaH | atra Adishabdena mokShataditaraphalArthAsheShabrahmakarmavidyA gR^ihyante | 'adhikAram' adhikArabhAvamiti | anena 'bhAvam' ityasyArtha uktaH | manyata iti sheShoktiH | astItyasya kartR^isApekShatvAt taM darshayati - prakAshavisheSha iti | j~nAnA- tishaya ityarthaH | hishabdo yata ityarthe | tathA chetthaM yojanA - bAdarAyaNastu bhagavAn devAnAM madhvAdyasheShavidyAsu adhikArabhAvaM manyate | na cha prAptaphalatvAttatra arthitvAbhAvo doShaH | yadyapi devAH prAptapadAH brahmaj~nAnitvAtsiddha- mokShataditaraphalAH prAptumashakyAyogyaphalAshcha | tathApi prAptapadAnAmapi devAnAM madhvAdividyAsUktopAsanAkarma- karaNAbhyAM phalavisheShabhAvAtsvasvayogyasya j~nAnamAtreNa asAdhyasya mokShaphale atishayasya bhAvAt siddherarthitva- sambhavAt | na cha phale.atishayasya siddhatvena tatrArthitvasambhave.api tatsAdhanavidyAnAM nityasiddhatvAt vidyAvichArasya j~nAnArthatvAt tatrArthitvAsambhava iti vAchyam | 'hi' yato bhagavaditareShAM nirupacharitasArvaj~nAbhAvAt vidyAvichAreNa 'prakAshavisheShaH' j~nAnavisheShaH 'asti' sambhavatIti | anena sUtravR^ittirdarshitA | atra bAdarAyaNapadaM pUjArtham |
(20) nanu tattadvidyoktopAsanakarmakaraNAbhyAM tattadvidyoktaphalAdanyadapi phalaM prakAshavisheShashcha devAnAM bhavatItyetat kuto j~nAyate ityAshaN^kAM parihartumuktArthe hishabdasUchitAM smR^itiM darshayati - yAvaditi || kriyata iti sheShaH | svArthe tal | bhAvabhavitrorabhedavivakShayA vA | siddhyatyasyeti sheShaH | cho hetusamuchchaye | yadvA - AdyashchaH prakAshasya cheti sambadhyate | phalasamuchchAyakashchAyam, asambhavasamuchchaye cha | sambhavAdityAvartate | tathA cha 'pare tattve' paramAtmasvarUpe 'asau vA AdityaH' (ChAM.3-1-1.) ityAdinokte tadviShaye 'devAnAM' devairvasvAdibhiH 'yAvat' yAvadadhikaM 'sevA' 'eShA sevA' ityuktA shravaNAdirUpopAsanA kriyate 'tAvat' tAvadadhikaM teShAM 'sukhavisheShatA' svargApavargAdisukhe.atishayaH svasvayogyo j~nAnamAtreNa sAdhyaH siddhyati | yato.ataH 'paraM' svatantraM harimekamR^ite.anyeShAM 'prakAshasyAsambhavAt' nirupacharitasArvaj~nyAbhAvAt | ata eva vidyAvichAreNa sAdhyasya prakAshasya j~nAnavisheShasya sambhavAt, ata evArthitvasya sambhavAtteShAM devAnAM 'sAmarthyayogAt' sAmarthyasambhavAchcha vidvattAsambhavAchchApi prAptapadAnAmapi 'devAnAM' devaiH 'sarvamupAsanaM' sarvavidyoktopAsanaM sarvayaj~nAdikarma cha 'nityaM' niyamena 'vidhIyate' shrutiShu kartavyatvena bodhyata iti yojanA | chaH samuchchaye | aprakAshasyeti pAThe nirupacharitasArvaj~nyAbhAvasyetyarthaH 
| tadA prakAshasya chashabdena grahaNam | sambhavAdityasya siddhatvAt sattvAdityarthadvayam | pAThadvaye.apyanyeShAmiti sheShaH | ekashabdo avadhAraNArtho viriJNchasyApi varjyatvanivArakaH skAnde uktamiti sheShaH | ataH phalavisheShabhAvAdasti hi prakAshavisheSha ityanayornAsiddhiriti vAkyasheShaH |
(21) nanvastvevamasambhavAdityuktayuktiparAbhavaH | tathApi devAnAmadhikArAbhyupagatAvAptatamajaiminimatavirodha ityata Aha - ukteti || uktaM cha tat phalaM cha uktaM phalaM yasyeti cha vigrahaH | tathA cha tattadvidyoktaphalArthaM tatphala- kaprAgAptaj~nAnArthaM cha yo.ayamadhikArastadabhAvamAtraM 'jaiminimatam' jaiminyabhimatamityarthaH | mAtrashabdena phalAntarA- rthAdhikArAbhAvo vyAvartyate | kimato yadyevamityata Aha - ata iti jaiminyuktasya sUtrakAreNApyaN^gIkR^itatvAt, sUtrakR^iduktasya cha jaimininA anirastatvAnna tayorvirodhaH ityarthaH |
(22) nanu kimanayormatayorviShayavailakShaNyakalpanena virodha eva kiM na syAdityata Aha - sarvaj~nasyeti || tushabdo visheShArthaH | evakAro bhinnakramaH | tathA cha yasmAt 'munayo' jaiminyAdyAH nirupacharitasarvaj~nasya 'kR^iShNasya' dvaipAyanasya 'ekadeshavichintitaM' vichintitArthaikadeshaM tanmataikadeshameva svIkR^itya tadeva brUyuH, nAnyat | tasmAt 'tanmataM' teShAM kR^iShNamunInAM mataM parasparaM na viruddhyata ityarthaH | brAhma ityanantaraM uktamiti sheShaH | ato viShaya- vailakShaNyameva kalpyaMna matavirodha iti bhAvaH || 8 ||
|| iti devatAdhikaraNam ||
|| 9. apashUdrAdhikaraNam ||
(1) atrAdhikaraNe trivarNetarasya shUdrasya vedoktabrahmavidyAdhikAro nirAkriyate | prAsaN^gikatvAt nAdhyAyAdi- saN^gatiranveShaNIyA | shrutyAdisaN^gatiM viShayAdikaM cha sUchayati - manuShyeti || nimittasaptamIyam | adhikAropa- yogitayokte manuShyatve avisheShAditi vA | na kevalaM dvijAtInAM, kintu shUdrasyApItyaperthaH | tathA cha shUdrasyApi vedavidyAdhikAraH prApnoti | kutaH? 'manuShyAdhikAratvAt' ityanena manuShyANAmadhikArasyoktatvAt | adhikAropa- yogitayokte manuShyatve cha shUdrasya dvijAtibhyaH 'avisheShAt' visheShAbhAvAt | nanu na manuShyatvaM vedavidyAdhikAro- payogi, kintu vishiShTabudhyAdimattvamevetyato.apyAha - avisheShAditi | shUdrasya vishiShTabuddhyAdimattve.api anyebhyaH 'avisheShAt' visheShAbhAvAdityarthaH | evamavisheShAkhyayuktimabhidhAya shUdrasya vedavidyAdhikArAdarshanAt, anadhikAra ityato liN^gadarshanamAha pautrAyaNokteriti || ChAndogye pautrAyaNasya vaidikasaMvargavidyAdhyayanokterdarshanAdityarthaH | nanu pautrAyaNAkhyapuruShasya shUdratvameva kuta ityataH tajj~nApakamAha - aha hAretvA shUdreti | pautrAyaNokteriti | 
pautrAyaNaM prati raikkoktestatkartR^ikasambodhanAdevetyarthaH | nanvadhikArAbhAve.api pautrAyaNo vedavidyAM vichArayAmAseti kiM na syAdityatopyAha - pautrAyaNokteriti | pautrAyaNaM prati raikkeNa nispR^iheNa muninA saMvargavidyopadeshAdityarthaH | anadhi- kAriNaM prati munerupadeshAsambhavAt | pautrAyaNasya arthAchChrutAvadhikArokteshcheti vA yojanA | adhikAra ityanantara- mato virodha ityanukR^iShyate | tasyokta ityanenAnvayaH | anenoktanyAyena uktArthe shrutyAdipramANavirodhAkShepAt pUrveNA- syAkShepikI saN^gatiH, vedavidyAdhikArAkhyo viShayaH, sayuktikapUrvapakShashcha darshito bhavati |
ChAndogye chaturthAdhyAye saMvargaprakaraNe hItthamAkhyAyikA - pautrAyaNo nAma rAjA prAsAdAgre nishAyAM shayAno.a- bhUt | tadA prAsAdopari haMsapakShiNo.agaman | uparipatatAM parasparaM vArtAM kurvatAM teShAM madhye dvAvagragAminAvAstAm | tatraika ekamuvAcha | kimiti? are pautrAyaNIyaM tejastvaM mAgamaH | tatsambandhe tadIyaM tejastvAM dahediti | evamuktaH paro haMsaH kamityAkShepavachanena rAjAnamanAdR^itya raikvamunimeva prashashaMsa | tachChrutvA paritaptamanA rAjA talpAdutthita- stvarayA svasArathimAhUya raikvagaveShaNAyAdidesha | sa tatra tatra raikvamanviShyan nAvidamiti prathamamAgataH | punasta- llakShaNoktipUrvakaM rAj~nA tanmArgaNAyAdiShTaH punaranviyaShya kvachitpradeshe raikvamavalokya punA rAjAnaM pratyetyAha - raikva- mavidamiti yathAvR^ittamavadat | tadA rAjA svasArathivachanena raikvamunisthAnaM nishchitya tasmAttattvaM vividiShurgurudakShiNAM gR^ihItvA tatsamIpaM jagAma | atha dvAri shakaTasyAdhasthAt sthitaM raikvaM dR^iShTvA sambodhya dakShiNAM nivedya mahyaM vidyAM brUhItyuvAcha | tadA taM pautrAyaNaM paro lokavilakShaNo raikvaH pratyAchakhyau | kimiti? ahahAretvA shUdretyAdi | atra ahetisambodhanaM, hAra itveti bhinnapadatve visargalope guNe hAretveti bhavati | tathA cha he shUdra hAraH kaNThamAlAkhyaM bhUShaNaM itvA rathaH | tattvapradIparItyA shakaTo vA | gobhissaha tavAstvityarthaH hAretvAnAvityekapadatvapakShe dvivachanasya ekavachanAdesho vA AkArAdesho vA kartavyaH | pratyekaM cha astu iti kriyAsambandhaH |
(2) siddhAntayatsUtramavatArayati - ata iti || avisheShAkhyayukteH shravaNasUtre nirAkariShyamANatvAt, pUrvapakShyuktaliN^gadarshanasya anyathopapattipradarshanAya pravR^ittasya tadAdravaNAdityasya anvayayogyArthAkAMkShotthApakaM sUtrasya phalitArthaM darshayati - neti | 'asau' raikveNa sambodhitaH pautrAyaNo 'na shUdraH' jAtyA shUdro na, kintu kShatriya ityarthaH | tarhi kathamasya shUdreti sambodhitatvaM yujyate rUDhyabhAvAdityato yogAdevetyAshayena tachChabdapravR^ittinimitta- pradarshakaM tadAdravaNAditi sUtrAMshaM sAvadhAraNaM matvA vyAchaShTe - shucheti | 'shuchA' shokena raikvaM kShattAraM vA pratyAshugama- nameva 'shUdratvam' shUdretisambodhane nimittaM, na tu jAtirityarthaH | anena tadAdravaNAdityasya sUtre shUdratvamityadhyAhR^itena shUdreti sambodhitatvarUpArthabodhakena padenAnvayaH sUchitaH | tathA cha na sambodhanAnupapattiriti nedaM shUdrasya 
vedavidyA- dhikAre liN^gamityato na shUdrasya vedavidyAdhikAra iti naJNAvR^ittyA anvayaH | evetyanena ayaM shUdrashabdaH shuchAdravaNA- chChUdra iti nairukta eva, na tu 'shucherdashcha' ityuNAdisUtreNa rapratyaye dhAtoshchadIrghe chakArasya dakArAdeshe cha niShpanno rUDha ityuktaM bhavati | pautrAyaNa ityanena buddhisthaparAmarshakedaMshabdArthaH shuchetyanena prAguktavAchisautradvitIyatachChabdArthaH, tvapratyayena nimittArthakapaJNchamyarthashcha darshitaH | sUtrakArasya sadA sarvaj~natvena shugasyetyuktiH | bhAShye 'saH' iti shrutyanusAreNa asAviti parokSheNoktishcha yuktA |
(3) kasmAnnimittAdasya shoka ityasyottaratayA pravR^ittaM shugasya tadanAdarashravaNAditisUtrakhaNDaM vyAchaShTe - kamvara iti || kaM u are iti padachChedaH | 'are' haMsa etadvachanaM kamenamuddishyAttha 'santaM' nirduShTaM 'sayugvAnaM' sashakaTaM raikvamityevetyarthaH | u iti nipAtaH, asya nindArthaH | asmin rAj~ni vaktumananurUpamidam, evaM vaktuM raikva eva yogya ityarthaH | 'etatsantaM' nindyaM santamAtthetyarthaH tattvapradIpe abhihitaH | 'etatsantam' atra santamiti vA | ityanAdarashravaNAditi | anAdaro nindA | tathA cha ityevaMrUpasya haMsakR^itAnAdarabodhakavAkyasya haMsAt svAnAdara- vAkyasya vA shravaNAdityarthaH | shravaNAdityanantaraM prAptayetisheShaH | asya shuchetyanenAnvayaH ||
(4) nanu shrutAnAdarasyApi rAj~naH kuH shokotpattiH j~nAyate | na cha pratyakShAttannishchayaH | anAdarashravaNarUpa- parabuddherapratyakShatvena tataH shokotpatterapratyakShatvAt | na cha kAraNAnumAnAt kAryAnumitiH | kAraNasya kAryAvinA- bhAvAbhAvAdityataH pravR^ittaM 'sUchyate hi' iti sUtrasheShaM vyAchaShTe - saheti | hetyAshcharye | 'saH' shrutAnAdaraH pautrAyaNaH 'saJNjihAna eva' shayanIyAduttiShThanneva 'kShattAraM' sArathiM prati raikvagaveShaNAyovAcheti shrutyarthaH | iti sUchyate hIti | ityetadvAkyArthAnyathA.anupapattyA j~nAtena raikve vyAsaktamanaskatvena kAryeNa tatkAraNaM shugasya 'sUchyate' j~nAyata ityarthaH| kAraNasya kAryAvinAbhAvAbhAve.api kAryasya kAraNAvinAbhAvasyAvashyaM bhAvAditi bhAvaH | asya tadanAda- rasya shravaNAt prAptayA shuchA.a.adravaNameveti pUrveNAnvayaH | shokenAdravaNAkhyanimittaparij~nAnaM cha raikvamuneH sArvaj~nyAdupapadyate | taduktaM  ChAndogyabhAShye -
rAjA pautrAyaNaH shokAchChUdreti muninoditaH |
prANavidyAmavApyAsmAtparaM dharmamavAptavAn || iti ||
'shokAt' shokenA.a.adravaNAdityarthaH | athavA - shokashabdopapadAt AN^apUrvakAt 'atasAtatyagamane' 
ityasmAt kvipi rUpametat tathAtve yata iti sheShaH | nanu sUtre taddravaNAdityetAvatA pUrtau AN^prashleShaH kimartha iti chet - na, shrutau shUdretivaktavyatve.api shokAdhikyaj~nApanArthaM shUdreti UkArarUpo yo dIrghasvaraH shrutaH tadarthavyaktavyarthatvAt | na cha shUgdretivaktavye shrutau shUdretyuktiH kathamiti vAchyam | 'tasmAdrugdrAvaNAt rudraH' iti shrutau gakArasya dakArA- deshena yathAprayogastathopapatteH | ata eva tattvapradIpe tR^itIyasya tR^itIyo.atishayArthatvAdityuktam | 'rujaM drAvayate' iti smR^itAvivopapatteshcha | anena - shuchA 'AdravaNAt' raikvaM prati shIghragamanAdeva nimittAdasya pautrAyaNasya shUdratvaM shUdreti sambodhitatvam, na tu varNAvaratvAt | shukcha shokashchAsya tadanAdarashravaNAdAsIt | taditi shrutyuktaparAmarshaH| kriyAkartR^ibhAvaShShaShThyarthaH | tathA cha 'tasya anAdarashravaNAt' haMsakR^itAnAdarashravaNAt ityarthaH | tattvapradIparItyA tasmAddhaMsAt svAnAdarashravaNAdityarthaH | madhyamapadalopI samAsa iti kechit | nanu shrutAnAdarasyApi kutaH shokotpa- ttirj~nAyate, parabuddheH shokapadoktaduHkhAnubhavasya apratyakShatvAdityata uktaM - sUchyate hIti || 'hi' yasmAt 'saha' iti vAkyArthAnupapatyA j~nAtena tadvyagramanaskatvAkhyakAryeNa tatkAraNaM shugasya 'sUchyate' j~nAyate | tasmAt ato na shUdreti sambodhanaM shUdrasya vedAdhikAre liN^gamiti naitadbalAchChUdrasya vedavidyAdhikAra iti bhAvaH iti sUtrArtha ukto bhavati |
(5) nanu shUdrashabdo.ayaM kuto yaugiko.aN^gIkriyate, rUDhArtha eva kiM na syAt | yogarUDhyormadhye rUDhereva prAbalyAt | tathA cha pautrAyaNanidarshanenaiva shUdrasya vedavidyAdhikArasiddhirityAshaN^kAM pariharatsUtramupanyasya vyAchaShTe - kShatriyatveti | atra 'ayam' ityataH prAk 'uttaratra' iti sautrapadaM sambandhanIyam | shruteneti sheShaH | tathA cha uttaratra raikvaM prati pautrAyaNasya AdravaNAt, uttaratra tatpratipAdanAnantaram | yadvA - shUdrashabdena sambodhanAt uttaratra 'ayamashvatarI rathaH' iti shrutenetyarthaH | pautrAyaNena dIyamAnasya rathasya anyadIyatvashaN^kAnirAsAya sUtre chaitraratheneti bhAvapradhAnapadaM prayuktam | anyathA chitrarathenetyevAvakShyat | tatra chitrashchAsau rathashcha chitrarathaH tasyAyaM chaitraratha iti vigrahamabhipretya pratyayArthaM pradarshayan tadvyAchaShTe - chitrarathasambandhitveneti || svAbhAvikachitrarathasambandhitvenetyarthaH| atra rathamAtrameva liN^gaM, chitrapadaM tu svarUpakathanArtham | yadvA - apUrvarathayogena kShatriyatvasambhAvanArthaM tatpadam | athavA yadA rathitvenaiva kShatriyatvasya nishchayaH, tadA sutarAM chitrarathitveneti sUchanArthaM tatpadam | yadyapi 'ayamashva- tarIrathaH' ityatra chitrarathamAtrashravaNe.api na tatsambandho.asya shrUyate | tathApi tatpUrvavAkye 'hAretvA tavaiva' iti ShaShThyA itvAshabdArtharathasambandho gamyata iti tasyAshcha rathasambandhe shrutirUpatvAt yuktamuktam | chitro ratho yasyeti chitrarathastasya bhAvaH chaitrarathasteneti vyAkhyAnaM tu bhAve.aN pratyayasya kalpyatvAt shrutibhAShyaviruddhatvAchcha ayuktam| na cha chaitraratheneti sambandhoktimAtreNa 
kathamanyadIyatvashaN^kAnirAsa iti vAchyam | svataH prAptatadIyatve bAdhakAbhAve tadIyatvasyaiva svAbhAvikatvasambhave naimittikagrahaNAyogAt | 'svatvAbhAve dhanAyogAt' ityAdinyAyaprAptatvAt | rathena liN^gAdityanayossAmAnAdhikaraNyAya liN^gAditi paJNchamI vyatyayena vyAchaShTe - liN^ganeti | pautrAyaNasye- tyetat asyetyanuvR^ittapadasya arthakathanam | kShatriyatvAvagaterityasya shuchA.a.adravaNAdevAsya shUdratvaM na tu rUDhyeti pUrve- NAnvayaH | chashabdo liN^gena cheti sambadhyate | tena 'bahudAyI' ityAdivAkyasheShoktaM liN^gaM samuchchIyate | liN^gasya shrutitashcharamatvena anekatvena cha prAbalyasUchanAya vA chashabdaH | evaM sUtre.api chashabdo bhinnakramaH uktaprayojanakashcha | evaM cha rUDhereva prAbalye.apyatra shrutAnekaliN^garUpabAdhakAt shUdrashabdasya yogavR^ittyaN^gIkAra eva yukta iti bhAvaH | 'gardabhAdashvAyAM jAtA ashvataryaH' iti tattvapradIpe | 'gardabhIShu ashvairjAtA asvataryaH' iti vyAsatIrthIye | tadyukto rathaH ashvatarIrathaH tava dakShiNAtvena vartate ityarthaH | raikvaM prati pautrAyaNavAkyametat |
(6) nanu shrutAvashvatarIrathashabdaprayogAt sUtre.api tathaiva prayoktavye kathaM sUtrakR^it chitrarathashabdaM prAyuN^tetyA- shaN^kya ubhayorarthaikyAnna visaMvAda ityAshayena tatrAbhidhAnamAha - ratha iti || tushabdo visheShArtho.avadhAraNe vA | ashvatarIyukta eveti sambadhyate | atra ratha iti vAstavavisheShoktireva, na tu rathatvasyApi shakyakoTipraveshaH | tathA cha sUtre rathatvaprakArakabodhAya rathashabdaprayoga iti na tadvaiyarthyamiti dhyeyam iti brAhme uktatvAt na shrutisUtrayorvairUpya- mityupaskAreNAnvayaH |
(7) evaM sAkShAdeva svAbhAvikarathena pautrAyaNasya kShatriyatvaM prasAdhitam | svAbhAvikarathitve.asya varNAvaraà¤¼tvaM kiM na syAdityaprayojakatvamAshaN^kya maivam-AgantukasyApi rathasya vedaM vinA.ayogAt 'vedasya cha saMskAreti vakShya- mANanyAyena shUdre.ayogAt' rathamAtreNa vedAnumAnadvArA pautrAyaNasya shUdratvAbhAvasiddherityAshayena rathena vedAnumAne vyabhichArashaN^kAparihArAya AgamenobhayavyAptiM darshayati - yatreti | 'tatra' tatraivetyarthaH | tena yatra vahniH tatraiva dhUma ityAdAviva vedasya vyApakatAlAbhaH| ata eva vyatirekapradarshakAMshe na veda iti vedabhAvasya prathamamuktiH| smR^itau rathashabdena AgantukasvAbhAvikasAdhAraNarathamAtrasya vivakShitatvAt, samavyAptyabhiprAyeNa vA yatra veda ityuktiH | ata eva TIkAyAM 'rathasya vedAvinAbhAvAt' iti rathasya vyApyatvamuktvA 'vaidikatvamAtre vidyamAnaM rathitvam' ityanena tasya vyApakatvamuktam | vastutastu - yatra rathastatra veda iti yojanAyAM nAnupapattiH | tathA cha anena vyApti- nishchayAt na vyabhichArashaN^keti yAdR^ishatAdR^isharathamAtreNa vedAnumAnadvArA shUdratvAbhAvanishchayAnna pautrAyaNasya vedabAhyavarNAvaratvaM shaN^kyamiti bhAvaH | etena pUrvapakShiNA shUdre.api vedAN^gIkArAnna tena 
shUdratvAbhAvasAdhanaM yuktamitinirastaM, tasyottarasUtre nirAkariShyamANatvAt | na cha brAhmaNAdisAdhAraNarathitvenAsya vaidikatvanishchaye.api taddvArA ashUdratvasiddhAvapi kathaM kShatriyatvanishchaya iti vAchyam | rathitvamAtrasya vaidikatvavyAptatvoktyA svAbhAvikarathitvasya vaidikavisheShakShatriyatvavyAptatvenApi smR^ityabhipretatvAt | tasya cha kAdAchitkarathavati brAhmaNA- dAvabhAvAttena sAkShAdeva kShatriyatvanishchayopapattiH | na cha 'apalAyanaM cha shUdrasya' ityanena prAptayoddhR^itvAnyathAnupa- pattyA shUdrasya rathitvapratItestatra vyabhichAra iti vAchyam | apalAyanena yoddhR^itvasya padAtitayopapattyA rathitvA- nAkShepakatvAt | brahmavaivarta ityasya uktatvAdityadhyAhAreNa nAsau shUdra ityanenAnvayaH iti j~nAyata iti sheShaH anena - 'AdravaNAt' sambodhanAdvA 'uttaratra' 'ayamashvatarIrathaH' (ChAM.4.2.2.) itishrutena 'chaitrarathena liN^gAt' liN^gena svAbhAvikarathena liN^gena bahudAyitvAdiliN^gena chAsya pautrAyaNasya kShatriyatvAvagateH | asmAt bAdhakAttadAdravaNA- nnimittAdevAsya shUdratvam, na tu jAtyAsau shUdraH | tathA rathena vedanishchayAchcha nAsau shUdra iti sUtrArtha ukto bhavati |
(8) yaduktaM rathitvaliN^gena pautrAyaNasya kShatriyatvAvagamAt, na talliN^gena shUdrasya vedAdhikArasiddhiriti | na tadyuktaM - shUdrasyApi rathitvasambhavAt | na cha rathasya vedavyApyatvAchChUdre cha tadabhAvAdrathasyApyabhAva iti vAchyam | shUdre.api vedAdhikArAN^gIkArAdityAshaN^kAM pariharatsUtramupanyasyati - saMskAreti || atra 'aShTavarShaM brAhmaNamunayIta| tamadhyApayIta' iti shrutau brAhmaNasyaivAdhyayane upanayanApekShA, nAnyeShAmityAshaN^kAparihArAya pravR^ittaM saMskAraparA- marshAdityaMshaM vyAchaShTe - aShTavarShamiti | upanayIteteyanantaram ityupanayanamuktveti sheShaH | 'tam' upanItaM mANavakamAtma AchAryakaraNakAmo.adhyApayItetyarthaH | itishabdAnantaraM shrutAviti sheShaH | 'anyArthavachanaM parAmarshaH' ityAshayena parAmarshapadaM vyAchaShTe - adhyayanArthamiti || adhyayanAN^gatayetyarthaH | adhyApanavAkyasyApi 'svAdhyA- yo.adhyetavyaH' (tai.A.2.15.1.) iti shrutyanurodhena jIvikArthAdhyayanavidhiparatvAditi bhAvaH | 'saMskAraparAmarshAt' upanayanAkhyasaMskAramAtravachanAdityarthaH | tachChabdeneti sheShaH | na tu brAhmaNaparAmarsha iti mAtrashabdArthaH | tathA cha noktashaN^kAvakAsha iti bhAvaH | kechittu - shrutigatabrAhmaNashabdo.atra brahmANana yogyatraivarNikapara ityAhuH | tachchi- ntyam, shaN^kAsamAdhAnAnanuguNatvAt | kuta evaM kalpyata ityataH smR^itAvapyupanayanAkhyadvitIyajanmavata eva sAraNyaka vedAdhyayanavidhAnAdityAshayena sUtre bhAShye cha 'vedaH kR^itsno.adhigantavyaH sarahasyo dvijanmanA' iti smR^itisamuchchayA- rthakashchashabdaH prAyoji | saH parAmarshAdityanenAnveti | parAmarshAchchetyanantaram adhyayanasya saMskArasApekShatvA- vagamAditi sheShaH |
(9) nanvastvadhyayanasya upanayanasaMskArasApekShatvaM, tathApi na shUdrasya vedAdhyayanAbhAvasiddhiH | 
shUdrasyApi saMskArasambhavAdityataH pravR^ittaM 'tadabhAvAbhilApAt' iti sUtrakhaNaà¤¼à¥DaM vyAchaShTe - nAgniriti || abhilApAt abhidhA- nAditi | asya sUtre adhyAhR^itena 'na shUdrasya vedAdhikAro, na vA tadavinAbhUtaM rathitvam' iti sAdhyenAnvayaH | 'agniH', shrautaHsmArtashcha | 'yaj~naH' agnihotrAdiH, daivapitryAdiyaj~no vA | 'kriyA' sandhyAvandanAdirUpA, uttara- kriyA vA | saMskAra upanayanAdiH | 'vratAni' kR^ichChrachAndrAyaNAdIni ||
(10) nanvevaM saMskArAbhAvena vedAnadhikArashcheduttamastrINAmapi tatprasaN^gaH | saMskArAbhAve.api tAsAmadhikAre shUdrasyApi tatprAptirityata Aha - uttameti | tushabdo vedadraShTR^itvAkhyavisheShadyotakaH | 'saMskArAbhAvenAbhAvaH' ityA- kR^iShyate | adhikArasyeti sheShaH | uttamAnAM striya iti vigrahaH, karmadhArayo vA | tathA cha shachI yamI- UrvashyAdyuttamastrINAM shUdravanna saMskArAbhAvena vedavidyAdhikArasyAbhAvo vaktavyaH | kutaH? 'sapatnIM me parAdhama' (mantraprashna 1.16.) ityAdividyAsu tAsAM taddraShTR^itvena adhikAradarshanAditi yojanA | atra 'sapatnIm' iti pratIkagrahaNena 'sapatnIM me parAdhama' patiM me kevalaM kR^idhi, 'uttarA.ahamuttara uttareduttarAbhyaH' iti samagravAkyaM gR^ihyate| shachIvAkyamidam | he bhagavAn 'me sapatnIM' madanyAM matpatipANigR^ihItIM 'parAdhama' parANuda | mama patiM 'kevalaM' mayyevAsaktaM kuru | 'ahamuttarAbhyaH' saundaryeNotkR^iShTAbhyaH madantarAbhyo vA strIbhyaH 'uttarA' utkR^iShTA satI 'uttaret' priyottamaiva 'uttare' sapatnIkleshAduttareyamiti shrutyarthaH | Adipadena 'udatI pashyavaH soma ekebhyaH parvate, () udasau sUryo agAt' (R^i.10.159.1.) ityAdi devamAtR^iyamIpaulomyAdidR^iShTAnAM grahaNam |
(11) tarhi saMskArAbhAvahetoruttamastrIShu vyabhichArassyAdityata Aha - saMskAreti || abhAvo vedAdhikAra- sya | tushabdaH pUrvoktanyAyasya sAmAnyatvAkhyavisheShadyotakaH | ukta iti sheShaH | tathA cha saMskArAbhAvena hetunA yatsUtre vedAdhikArasya abhAva uktaH saH 'sAmAnyena' sAmAnyanyAyena sApavAdaniyamAbhiprAyeNaiva, na tu nirapavAda- niyamena | ato nApavAdaviShaye vyabhichAra ityarthaH | sAmAnyatvavachanena shUdrapratibandI mochitA | tathA cha saMskArA- bhAvena vedAdhikArAbhAva iti sAmAnyavyApteH shachyAdiShu vidyAdhikAradarshanAkhyApavAdakena bhaN^ge.api na shUdrAdAvapi tasya bhaN^gaH kalpyaH, 
tatra vedavidyAdhikAre visheShapramANAkhyApavAdakAbhAvAditi bhAvaH |
(12) evaM strINAM upanayanAbhAve.api pUrvoktavyApteH sAmAnyatvena apavAdasambhavAdasti vedAdhikAra ityuktam| athopanayanAkhyavidhyabhAve.api tatpratinidhisadbhAvAchcha astyadhikAra ityAha - asticheti | chaH adhikArasamu- chchaye | 'tAsAM' strINAM kuta etadityata Aha - strINAmiti | puMsAmiti sheShaH | tathA cha puMsAM yathA upanayanaM saMskAraH, tathA strINAM 'pradAnakarmaiva' vivAhakriyaiva saMskAra iti vyAsasmR^ityarthaH | smR^iterityasya tAsAmityanenA- nvayaH | iti j~nAyata iti sheShaH | tathA cha uttamastrIShviha hetUkR^itasya vidhipratinidhisAdhAraNasaMskArasAmAnyA- bhAvasyAbhAvAt na vyabhichAra iti bhAvaH | na cha saMskAramAtrasya vedAdhikAraprayojakatve adhamastrINAmapi tadApatti- riti vAchyam | niShedhAbhAvasahitasyaiva tasya prayojakatvAbhyupagamAt | nanvevamuttamastrINAM saMskArayuktatvAdeva adhi- kAritvamiti noktanyAyabhaN^ga iti vaktuM shakyatvAt, kimarthaM tAsu saMskArAbhAvamaN^gIkR^itya uktanyAyasya sApavAdatva- vachanamiti chet - na, pradAnAdishUnyatiryagAdInAmapi saN^grahArthatvAt | teShAmapi 'ayamagne jaritA' (R^i.10.142. 1.) ityAdividyAdhikAradarshanena apavAdaviShayatvAt | anena - 'tamadhyApayIta' iti tachChabdena pUrvaprakR^itopanaya- nAkhyasaMskAramAtrasya parAmarshAdvedaH kR^itsna iti smR^iteshchAsya shUdrasya tadabhAvAbhilApAnnAgniriti shrutau saMskArAbhAvA- bhidhAnAt na tasya vedAdhikAra iti sUtrArtha ukto bhavati |
(13) nanu shUdre saMskArAbhAvena vedavidyAdhikArAbhAvoktiranupapannA | 'shUdraM nopanayIta' iti niShedhAbhAvena tasyApi saMskArasambhavAt | 'nAgnirna yaj~naH' iti shrutau tu shUdrasya saMskArAbhAva evochyate na tu asau na kArya iti niShidhyate | ato na tadvirodho.apItyAshaN^kAM pariharatsUtraM paThitvA vyAchaShTe - tadabhAveti | 'iti satyavachanena' vAN^manasayorekarUpayathArthavachanena tajj~nApitenArjaveneti yAvat | 'satyakAmasya' tadAkhyasya R^iSheH etachcha pUrvatrottaratra cha sambadhyate | 'satyavachanena satyakAmasya' ityAdinA sUtre tachChabdo vyastaH anekavibhaktikaH buddhyA vivichyAvartate ityuktaM bhavati | shUdratvAbhAvanirdhAraNe chetyasya naitadbrAhmaNa ityanena sambandhaH | cho.avadhAraNe | shrutAvabrAhmaNa- mAtrasya anupanayanAbhiprAyapratItestadanusAreNa brAhmaNatvAbhAvetyanuktvA shUdratvAbhAveti tadabhAvapadavyAkhyAnena shrutau brAhmaNashabdo brahmANanayogyatraivarNikapara ityuktaM bhavati | etadvAkyasya yadyayamabrAhmaNaH shUdraHsyAttarhmetatsatyavachanaM ArjavavachanaM vAN^manasayoravairUpyeNa vachanaM vivaktuM nArhediti vipakShe 
tarkoktirUpatayA, yo.abrAhmaNaH sa evaM vaktuM nArhati satyavachanahIna iti vyatirekavyAptyuktirUpatayA vA shUdratvAbhaAvanirNAyakatvam | haridrumato.apatyaM hAri- drumataH gautamaH | tasya pravR^itteriti | asya na tadabhAva iti adhyAhR^itapadenAnvayaH | tathA chetthaM mahAvAkyayojanA - satyakAmasya nAhametadvedeti satyavachanena naitadabrAhmaNo vivaktumarhatIti vyatirekavyAptij~nAnena bAdhakatarkeNa cha shUdratvAbhAvanirdhAraNe satyeva tamanumAyaiva tasya satyakAmasyopanayanasaMskAre 'hAridrumatasya' gautamasya 'pravR^itteH' pravR^ittatvAt na shUdrasya tadabhAvaH saMskAraniShedhAbhAva iti | cho hetusamuchchaye | anena - sUtre taditi vyastaM luptavibhaktikaM padaM samastaM cha tantreNopAttam | chashabdo.avadhAraNe bhinnakrameNa, na kevalaM shUdrasya saMskArAbhAvaH shruti- mAtrAt, kintu saMskAraniShedhaj~nApakaliN^gAchcheti samuchchaye cha | netyasti | tadabhAva ityanuShajyate | tathA cha 'tasya' satyakAmasya 'tena' satyavachanena manovAkkAyakarmaNAM avaiparItyamArjavaM tadeva satyatvaM tAdR^ishavachanena tena j~nApitena R^ijutveneti yAvat | naitadabrAhmaNo vivaktumarhatIti vyatirekavyAptiM bAdhakatarkaM chopanyasya 'tadabhAva- nirdhAraNe cha' tasya shUdratvAbhAvanirNaye satyeva tadabhAvamanumAyaiva 'samidhaM somyAharopa tvAneShye' (ChAM. 4.4.5.) iti tasya tasminnupanayanasaMskAre tasya gautamasya pravR^itterdarshanAchcha na shUdrasya tadabhAvaH saMskAraniShedhAbhAvaH | shUdrasya upanayananiShedhAbhAve kathamayaM tadabhAvanirdhAraNe satyeva pravarteta, te j~nAyate niShedho.astIti bhAva iti sUtrArtha ukto bhavati |
ChAndogye hItthamAkhyAyikA - satyakAmo nAma R^iShiH jabAlAkhyaM mAtaramupetyovAcha | kimiti? ahaM vedAdhyayanArtham AchAryamupagachCheyaM tatrAdhyayanasyopanayanasaMskArasApekShatvAt upanayanaM vinA te mAM nAdhyApayeyuH, upanayanaM cha gotrAdyavachane na kuryuH ato.ahaM kiM gotro.asmi tadvadeti | evamuktA jabAlA svaputraM satyakAmamabravIt - he tAta tvaM yadgotro.asItyetat nAhaM vedeti | evamuktaH satyakAmo gautamamupetyovAcha | kimiti? he bhagavan brahmacharyArthaM tvAmupeyamiti | evamukto gautamaH he somya tvaM kiMgotro.asi? tadvadetyuvAcha | evamuktassatyakAmaH punargautamaM pratyAha - nAhametadveda bho iti | bho bhagavan pUjya gautama ahaM yadgotro.asmItyetat vedyaM 'na veda' na jAnAmItyarthaH | evaM satyakAmasya satyavachanenArjavaM j~nAtvA punastaM pratyuvAcha | naitadityAdi | atra brAhmaNashabdo brahmANanayogyatraivarNikaparaH | 'ArjavaM brAhmaNe sAkShAt shUdro.anArjavalakShaNaH' itishrutivyAkhyAnarUpAyAM smR^itau brAhmaNapratiyogitvena shUdrasyopAdAnAt | tathA cha 'etat' ArjavasaMyuktavachanam 'abrAhmaNaH' traivarNiketaraHshUdro 'vivaktuM' sarvathA vaktuM 'nArhati' na yogyaH | atastvamevaM vadan brAhmaNa evAsi, ato he somya samidhamupahara tvAmupaneShya iti |
(14) nanvavisheShAdityuktarItyA shUdrasyApi vishiShTabuddhyAdimattvena adhikAraH siddhyet | anyathA 
tena devatAdyadhikArasiddhirapi na syAditi shaN^kAM pariharatsUtramupanyasya vyAchaShTe - shravaNeti | sUtre 'arthAvadhAraNe' iti shrutyanusArAdarthashabdaH tadavadhAraNaparaH | tathA cha 'shravaNe trapujatubhyAm' iti shrutau shUdrasya vedashravaNAdhyayanArthA- vadhAraNAnAM pratiShiddhatvAdityarthaH | asya na tadabhAva ityanuShaktasAdhyenAnvayaH | adhyayananiShedhAbhAva iti tadarthaH | tathA chAniShiddhatve sati vishiShTabuddhyAdimattvasyaiva vedAdhikAraprayojakatvenAN^gIkR^itatvAt tasya cha shUdre abhAvAnna tasya devaprativandyA vedAdhikAro vAchya iti bhAvaH | shUdreNa vedashravaNe kR^ite sati drutAbhyAM trapujatubhyAM vaN^galAkShAbhyAM tatkarNavivaraparipUraNaM rAjabhaTaiH kAryamiti shrutyarthaH | shiShTaH sugamaH |
(15) shrutau shUdreNa shravaNe kR^ite ityanuktervarNabAhyaviShayeyaM shrutiH kiM na syAdityAshaN^kAnivR^ityarthaM sUtre smR^iteshchetyuktaM, tAM smR^itimudAharati - neti | yathA 'shUdrasya' shUdreNa nAgnissavathA AdhAtavyaH paJNchavidho yaj~no.api nAnuShTheyaH | tathAdhyayanaM kutaH bhavet na kuto.api | tarhi tenAnuShTheyaM paralokasAdhanaM kimiti pR^ichChati - tu kintviti | uttaramAha - kevalaiveti | bhR^itirahitetyarthaH | trayashcha te varNAshcha trivarNAH, teShAM brahmakShatriya- vaishyAnAmityarthaH | 'shushrUShA' paricharyaiveti sambandhaH | vidhIyate | kAryatveneti sheShaH | iti smR^iterityasya shUdrasyai- vAdhyayananiShedhAvagamAt na tadabhAva ityadhyAhR^itenAnvayaH | tathA cha spaShTasmR^itibalAt shruterapi shUdraviShayatvameveti bhAvaH |
(16) nanu shUdrasya vedArthAvadhAraNAderniShiddhatve kathaM vidurAdInAM vaidikArthAvadhAraNamasti | evaM saMskAra- rahitAnAM vedAnadhikAre kathaM kShatriyaH saMskArarahitaH karNaH nikhilAH shrutIradhijagau | na cha vAchyamasAvapavAdaviShaya iti | avihitopanayanatve sati niShiddhAdhyayanAnAM uttamastrItiryagAdInAmevApavAdaviShayatvena niShiddhAdhyayanAnAM shUdrANAM atadviShayatvAdityata Aha - vidurAdInAmiti | Adipadena dharmavyAdhAdayo gR^ihyante | tushabdo visheShArthaH | tamevAha - utpannaj~nAtvAditi | janmAntara eva vedAtparamparayotpannamaparokShaj~nAnaM yeShAM te tathoktAsteShAM bhAvastattvam | tasmAt 'kashchit' asAdhAraNaH itarashUdrAdibhyo vyAvR^itto visheShaH teShvastItyarthaH | yata iti sheShaH | ato na 'nAgniH' ityAdiniShedhaviShayatvaM teShAM, kintu apavAdaviShayatvameveti na tatpratibandyetarashUdrANAM vedAdhikAraH shaN^kya iti bhAvaH | sUtrArthastu - shUdrasya shravaNe 'trapujatubhyAm' iti vedashravaNAdhyayanArthAvadhAraNapratiShedhakashruteH 'nAgnirna yaj~naH' iti spaShTaM shUdrasyaiva vedAdhyayananiShedhakasmR^iteshcha na tasya tadabhAvo vedAdhyayananiShedhAbhAva iti |
|| iti apashUdrAdhikaraNam || 9 ||
|| 10. kampanAdhikaraNam ||
(1) atrAdhikaraNe vajranAma samanvIyate | shrutyAdisaN^gatiM viShayAdikaM sUchayati - yadidamiti || atra traivarNikAnAM vedAt brahmaj~nAnaM mokShadamiti pUrvoktamayuktam | yato 'yadidam' iti shrutau udyatavajraj~nAnAt mokShaH shrUyata iti vAkyopaskAreNa yojanA | anena pUrvAdhikaraNe traivarNikAnAM vedAt brahmaj~nAnaM mokShadamiti yadabhipretaM tasya chAnandamayAdhikaraNe 'netaraH' ityanenoktasya mokShajanakaj~nAnaviShayatvasya viShNoranyatrAkShepAt tenAsya AkShepikI saN^gatiruktA bhavati | vajrashabdo viShaya iti sUchitam | vajrashruteH kulishe rUDhibalAt tathA 'udyatAyudhadordaNDAH' ityAdismR^itau 'tenendro vajramudayachChat' () iti shrutau cha Ayudhe prasiddhodyatatvaliN^gabalAchchendrAyudhamevedaM vajramiti sayuktikapUrvapakShaH sUchitaH | shrutau prANa iti saptamyantaM padam | sthitamitisheShaH | prANa ityasya nimittasaptamItvaM vA vibhaktivipariNAmaM vA Ashritya AvR^ittyA nissR^itamityanenApi sambandhaH | yadityasyAvR^ittiradhyAhAro vA | yaditishravaNAt taditi labhyate | tathA chAyaM siddhAnte shrutyarthaH - 'yatkiJNcha' yatkiJNchit dR^iShTaM shrutaM yatsarvaM jagat 'prANe' prANanAnnimittAt prANashabdavAchye harau sthitaM prANAnnissR^itaM tato jAtaM cha taditaM sarvaM jagat 'yasmAdejati' yatpreraNayA cheShTate tanmahanIyatvAt pUjyatvAt 'mahat' bhIShayatIti bhayaM duShTAnAM bhayaN^karam 'udyataM' sarvaprayatnavat 'udyatatvaM cha prayatnavattvam' utpUrvasya yamestadarthatvAt, iti chandrikokteH | yatIprayatna ityasyedaM rUpam, uchChabda utkarShavAchItyapi kechit | 'vajraM' doShavarjanAt apriyavarjanAdvA tachChabdavAchyam | etadye 'viduH' aparokShato jAnanti te 'amR^itAH' muktAH bhavantIti | yadvA - prANa iti prathamAntaM padaM tathA cha prANo mukhyaprANaH | idaM dR^iShTaM kiJNchAnyachChrutaM sarvaM jagachcha yasmAnnissR^itaM yasmAdejati cha tadetadvajraM ye vidurityarthaH | athavA - yadityasyAvR^ittistatra prathamasya jagadvisheShaNatvaM, dvitIyasya mukhyaprANaparatvam, tR^itIyasya vajraparatvam | sa iti labhyate | tasya prathamAnta- prANapadenAnvayaH | tathA cha yatkiJNchijjagatsarvaM yadyasmAnnissR^itaM sa mukhyaprANaH | yasmAdejati tadvajraM ye viduri- tyarthaH | atra prathamavyAkhyAne mukhyaprANasya jagadantargatatvena bhagavatpreryatvaM dvitIye jagatsAmyena, tR^itIye tu mukhya- prANasyaiva sAkShAdbhagavatpreryatvaM jagatastu mukhyaprANapreryatvamiti bhedaH | pUrvapakShI tu indrAyudhameva vajrapadenoktam | udyatatvamudyamanakarmatvaM tasyaiva liN^gamiti manyate ||
(2) siddhAntayatsUtramavatArya vyAchaShTe - ata iti || 'kampanavachanAt' ityetadrUpAt sarvajagachcheShTakatva- vachanAdityarthaH | yadvA - kampanasya mukhyaprANasya ejatItikampanavachanAchcheShTakatvokterityarthaH | vachanAdityanena kampa- napadaM tadvachanaparamityuktaM bhavati | na cha shrutau vAkyabhedAN^gIkAre kampakatvaM vajre nochyata iti vAchyam | kampakatva- nimittabhayaN^karatvasya vajre abhidhAnAdvAkyabhedAyogAt | udyatavajra iti sUtre sheShoktiH samanvayasUtrAdanuvR^ittasya tadityasyoddeshyavajrapadAnusArAtprANapadAnusArAdvA bhagavAniti vyAkhyAnaM kR^itam | sAvadhAraNaM chaitat | tena tushabdArtho darshitaH | yadyapi vajro bhagavAnevetyetAvadeva vaktavyaM, na tUdyata iti vajravisheShaNamapi | tathApi pUrvapakShyuktodyatatva- liN^gasya prayatnavattvarUpodyatatvArthatayA sAvakAshatvaj~nApanAya udyatetyuktam | 
(3) nanu shrutiliN^gAbhyAM pUrvapakShite kathaM liN^gamAtreNa nirNaya ityato liN^gasya niravakAshatvAdevetyAshayena shruteH prathamadvitIyavyAkhyAnAnusAreNa vajre shrutasya prANataditarasAdhAraNyena sAmAnyato jagachcheShTakatvaliN^gasya viShNoranyatraniravakAshatvaM shrutyA darshayati - kohIti | hishabdo hetau yata ityarthe prasiddhau vA | astIti sheShaH | ato liN^gasya nAnyatra sAvakAshatvaM shaN^kyamiti vAkyasheShaH |
(4) yadA sAmAnyataH sarvajagachcheShTakatvameva viShNvekaniShThaM tadA kimu vaktavyaM shruteH tR^itIyavyAkhyAnarItyA vajre shrutasya sarvajagatpravartakaprANacheShTakatvaliN^gasya viShNvekaniShThatvaM jagachcheShTakatvasya sarvathAnyatrAyogAditi bhAvena tatra shrutiM darshayati - prANasyeti | cho yasmAdityarthe | pUrvashrutisamuchchaye vA | shrutirityanuShajyate | uktaliN^gasya anyatra niravakAshatvaM j~nApayatIti vAkyasheShaH | yadvA - yat jagatpravartakaprANacheShTakatvAdiliN^gaM kampanAdityanena abhisaMhitaM, tasya viShNuniShThatvAsiddhiparihArAya tatra shrutiM pramANayati - prANasyeti | 'prANasya' sarvacheShTakamukhya- prANasya 'prANaM' prakR^iShTacheShTakatvarUpaprANatvapradam 'uta' tathA 'chakShuShashchakShuH' darshanakaraNatvarUpachakShuShTvapradaM paramAtmAnaM ye viduste brahma 'nichikyuH' prApnuyuriti vAjasaneya shrutyarthaH |
(5) shruteH prathamavyAkhyAyAmapi kaimutyavyaktikaraNAya shrutyuktaprANacheShTakatvaM hetUkR^itya pravR^ittAM smR^itimAha - nabhasvata iti || 'api' jagatprerakasyApi 'nabhasvato' vAyoryadA sarvAH cheShTAH 'bhagavato' j~nAnAdi- guNapUrNAddharerbhavanti | tadA kimutAnyasya preryasya vAyubhinnasya jagatashcheShTA harerbhavantIti vaktavyam 
| kuta etat? yato yasya jagataH cheShTA nabhasvato na bhavantyata iti vachanArthaH | skAnda ityanantaramuktamiti sheShaH | ato.api liN^gasya nAnyatrAvakAsha iti bhAvaH |
(6) nanUdyatatvaliN^gasya viShNau sAvakAshatve.api vajrashruterniravakAshatvAtsvabhAvataH prabalatvAchcha kathaM nirava- kAshenApi sarvacheShTakatvaliN^gena vajro viShNureveti nirNaya ityataH shruterniravakAshatvasyaiva asiddherityAshayena pUrvapakShyabhimatavajrashruterapi viShNAvavakAshaM smR^ityA darshayati - chakramiti | 'eShaH' bhagavAn 'chaN^kramaNAt' saMsAre jIvaparibhrAmakatvAt chakram | yathoktaM tattvapradIpe - chaN^krAmayatIti chakramiti | evaM 'varjanAt' daityairdUrAdeva varjyate, na sanmukhIkriyate iti, sattarkadIpAvalIrItyA duShTairvarjyatvAt, sarvadoShavarjanAdvA vajramityuchyate | 'khaNDanAt' duShTAN^gachChedanAt damanAchcha khaDga eSha ityarthaH | evashabdena tadabhedo vyAvartyate | tataH kim, eSha iti cha kaH ityata Aha - hetIti | evaM hariH 'svayaM' sAkShAt anyasambandhamantareNa 'hetinAmA' hetInAM chakrAdisarvAyudhAnAM yAni nAmAni mukhyavAchyatayA tadvAnityarthaH | hetIti sAmAnyagrahaNena bhAShye vajrapadamanyasyApyupalakShakamityuktaM bhavati| brahmavaivarta ityanantaram uktamiti sheShaH | ato na shrutivirodho.apIti bhAvaH | 'uchyate hetinAmA' ityanena vajrAdishabdAnAM viShNau vidvadrUDhirapyastIti sUchitam | tena varjanAdityuktayogasya rUDherdaurbalyAt ayoga iti nirastam| na chaivaM kAThakabhAShye - vajravadbhayadaM cheti vajrashabdasya viShNau gauNatvoktivirodha iti vAchyam | tatra tadvAkyasya yathAkathaJNchit brahmaparatvasiddhirityatraiva tAtparyAt | brahmaparatvasya gauNyApi siddheH gauNatve tAtparyAbhAvAt | atra tu samanvayasUtrapratij~nAtamukhyArthatvAya tAtparyato yogarUDhyorevoktatvAt | sUtrArthastu spaShTaH |
|| iti kampanAdhikaraNam || 10 ||
|| 11. jyotiradhikaraNam ||
(1) atrAdhikaraNe ubhayatraprasiddhajyotirnAma samanvIyate | shrutyAdisaN^gatiM viShayAdikaM cha darshayati - hR^idaya iti | yaddhR^idaye 'AhitaM' nihitaM jyotiH tachChabdavAchyaM sa paramAtmeti jyotirnaye abhihitamityarthaH | tataH kimityata Aha - tatreti jyotirviShaya ityarthaH | itishabdAtparaM shrUyata iti sheShaH | tato.api kimityata Aha - atreti | etadvAkya ityarthaH | shrutaM jyotirityanuShajyate | tathA chAtra shrutaM jyotiH 
tachChabdavAchyo j~nAnAtmako jIva eveti pratIyate | kutaH? 'sasamAnassannubhau lokAvanusaJNcharati' itivachanAt ityAdijIvaliN^gAbhidhAyakavAkya- sheShAditi yojanA | anena 'hR^idyantarjyotiH' iti vAjasaneyavAkyoktajyotiSho viShNutvAkShepamukhena pUrvoktasyApi tadAkShepAttenAsyAkShepikI saN^gatiH uktA bhavati | vAjasaneyoktaM jyotirviShayaH, jIva evedaM jyotiriti pUrvapakShashcha sUchitaH | vAjasaneyake hi ayaM puruShaH 'kiMjyotiH' kiMj~nAnasAdhanaH jIvasya j~nAnasAdhanaM kimiti janakena pR^iShTo yAj~nyavalkyaH 'AdityajyotissamrADiti hovAcha' (bR^i. 6.3.2.) ityanena he 'samrAT' sArvabhauma janakarAja AdityA- khyaj~nAnasAdhanako.ayaM puruSha ityuvAcha | evaMkrameNa prashnottarAbhyAM jAgraddashAyAmAdityachandrAgnivAchAM madhye pUrvapUrvAstamaye uttarottarajyotiShTvaM jIvasyAbhidhAya punaH suptisvapnayorAdityAdiShu chaturShvastamiteShu 'kiMjyotirayaM puruShaH' (bR^i.6.3.2.) iti janakena pR^iShTo yAj~navalkyaH 'AtmaivAsya jyotirbhavati' iti tayorjIvasya svaprakAsha- paramAtmajyotiShTvamuktvA punaH 'katam AtmA' (bR^i.6.3.7.) iti jyotiShTvenokta AtmA katamaH kIdR^isha iti pR^iShTo 'yo.ayam' ityanena jIvadehendriyAdiviviktaH paramAtmetyuttaramAhetyuktam | yo 'vij~nAnamayo' vij~nAnapUrNaH 'prANeShu' indriyeShu antaH hR^idyantashcha niyantR^itvena vartamAno 'jyotiH' jIvasya buddhyAdidyotakaH 'puruShaH' pUrNaShaDguNo- .asti | so.ayamAtmetyarthaH | tasya mahimAnamAha - sa iti | 'saH' AtmA paramAtmA 'samAnaH' avikAraH sadaikarUpaH san 'ubhau lokau' bhUlokadyulokau jAgratsuShuptI vA pratijIvamAdAya tamanusaJNcharatItyarthaH | pUrvapakShI tu, AtmapadaM sa iti padaM cha jIvaparaM ubhayalokasaJNcharaNamapi karmAdhInaM vivakShitaM, tachcha liN^gaM karmavashAttasyaiveti manyate |
(2) siddhAntayatsUtramavatArya darshanapadoktashrutyudAharaNapUrvakaM vyAchaShTe - ata iti | 'viShNureva jyotiH.... viShNurevAnandaH' iti chaturvedashikhAyAmiti 'darshanAt' viShNureva mukhyato jyotishshabdita iti uktatvAt 'jyotiH' tachChabdavAchyo viShNureva, na jIva ityarthaH | viShNurevetyanena tattvityanuvR^ittasya arthaH uktaH | shrutyarthastu spaShTaH | visheShastu - balaM balapradaH | 'sa vai balaM balinAM chApareShAm' iti cha bhAgavate | viShNureva yashaH 'tasya nAma mahadyashaH' (mahAnA.1.10.) iti shrutiriti tattvapradIpe abhihitam | brahmAdishabdavajjyotishshabdo.api viShNvekaniShTha iti j~nApanAya samagravAkyodAharaNam | ata eva shrutAvevakAraH |
(3) jyotirviShNushchettarhyubhayalokasashraNaliN^gavirodha iti shaN^kAmapi sautradarshanapadoktashrutyA pariharati - prAj~neneti || 'iti vachanAt' iti vAjasaneyashrutivAkyAt 'tasyApi' paramAtmano.api lokasaJNcharaNamastyevetyarthaH | na kevalaM jIvasyetyaperarthaH | na tadabhAva ityevashabdArthaH | tathA cha liN^gaM sAvakAshamiti na tadvirodha iti bhAvaH | shArIra AtmA jIvo maraNakAle 'prAj~nena' prakarSheNa AsamantAt j~nena praj~na eva prAj~naH, tena vA paramAtmanA 'anvA- rUDhaH' adhiShThito jIvamAruhya gachChati bhagavAniti bR^ihadbhAShyokteH tadvAhanabhUtaH 'utsarjat' prAktanadehamutsR^ijan dehA- ntaraM lokAntaraM cha 'yAti' gachChatIti vAjasaneyashrutyarthaH | sUtrArthastu spaShTaH | 
|| iti jyotiradhikaraNam || 11 ||
|| 12. AkAshAdhikaraNam || 
(1) atra ubhayatraprasiddhamAkAshanAma brahmANi samanvIyate | shrutyAdisaN^gatiM viShayAdikaM cha darshayati - sarvA- dhAratvamiti | dyubhvAdyadhikaraNa iti sheShaH | tataH kimityata Aha - tachcheti | cho.avadhAraNe | 'ityatra' ityevaM- rUpe ChandogavAkya ityarthaH | anenAtratyAkAshashabdasya viShNvanyatvaparatvoktimukhena pUrvoktasarvAdhAratvasyApi anya- niShThatvAkShepAttenAsyAkShepikI saN^gatiruktA bhavati | Chandogashrutyukta AkAshAkhyo viShayashcha sUchitaH | sayuktikaM pUrvapakShaM darshayati - vainAmeti || sa iti sheShaH | cho.avadhAraNe | tathA cha ChandogyashrutyuktaH AkAshaH prasiddhaH sAkShisiddhaH avyAkR^itAkAsha evAN^gIkAryaH | kutaH? AkAshapadena vainAmeti nipAtadvayadyotitaprasiddhimadarthasyopa- deshAt uktatvAdityarthaH | kechittu - 'sattarkadIpAvalyAM prasiddho bhUtAkAsha evAN^gIkAryaH' iti vachanAt avakAsha- syApi nAmarUpavattvAditi chandrikAkR^idabhipretaM TIkApAThamAshritya AkAshashabdapravR^ittinimittamavakAshatvaM bhUte niravadhi- kamiti sudhokteratrAvakAshashabditaM bhUtameva pUrvapakShaviShayaityAhuH | shrutau vai nAmeti nipAtadvayaM prasiddhau | 'nAma' vAchakashabdaprapaà¤¼JNchaH rUpapadena prAkR^itarUpAntarbhAvitArthaprapaJNchamAtramuchyate | tathA cha AkAsho 'nAmarUpayoH' shabdArtha- prapaJNchayoH 'nirvahitA' nirvoDhA AshrayaH kartAchetyarthaH | 'te' nirvAhyatayA prakR^ite nAmarUpe 'antarA' bhedena | yaditi nAmarUpaprapaJNchAdbhinnaM yadastIti yAvat | yadvA - tachChabdena vAchyaprapaJNchAntarbhUtaM nIlAdirUpaM vAchakaM nAma cha gR^ihyate| tathA cha 'te' nAmarUpe 'antarA' vinA tadrahitamiti yAvat | sAkalyena nAmavAchyaM prAkR^itarUparahitaM cha yadvartate tadbrahmetyarthaH | yadvA - 'te' nAmirUpiNAm 'antarA' bhedena yadastItyarthaH | yathoktaM tattvapradIpe - nAmi cha rUpi cha yannabhavati tadbrahmeti |
(2) siddhAntayatsUtramavatArya vyAchaShTe - ata iti | ityarthAntaratvAdivyapadeshAditi | sUtre bhAShye cha padArtha- tvabodhAyArthashabdaH | shrutyanusArAdantarashabdaH | tAbhyAmiti sheShaH | tathA cha tAbhyAM nAmarUpAbhyAM anyaH arthaH arthAntaraM yadvA tAbhyAM vilakShaNaH arthaH arthAntaraH tasya bhAvastattvam | nAmarUpaprapaJNchabhinnatvaM vA prAkR^itanAma- rUparAhityaM vA | nAmarUparAhityAkhyArthAntaratvavyapadeshAdityarthaH | Adipadena brahmatvaM gR^ihyate | yadvA - nirapekSha- yoreva nAmarUparAhityayorAkAshasya brahmatvasAdhakatvAt arthAntarapadena rUparAhityaM Adipadena nAmarAhityaM cha gR^ihyate| tathA cha evaMrUpArthAntaratvAdyukterityarthaH | 'AkAshaH' ChAndogye shruto.ayamAkAshastachChabdavAchyaH | samanvayasUtrAdanu- vR^ittasya tattvityasyArthamAha - harireveti || anena - ayamAkAsho harireva | kutaH? asya arthAntaratvAdivyapadeshAt 'te yadantarA' iti nAmarUparAhityAkhyavilakShaNArthatvokteH, brahmatvokteshcheti sUtrArtha ukto bhavati |
(3) AkAshe shrutena nAmarUpatvAdiliN^gena kuto viShNutvanishchaya ityatastasya tanniShThatvAditibhAvena tatra pramANatayA AtharvaNIM shrutimAha - avarNamiti | prAkR^itashuklAdivarNarahitaM tadbhinnaM vetyarthaH | yadvA avarNaM na varNyaM 'nApivarNAtmakam' ityarthaH 'yataH' iti shrutiH | 'yato' brahmaNo 'vAcho' nAmAni 'nivartante' ityanAmatvoktiparatayA vyAkhyeyA | AdishabdAt 'ashabdamasparshamarUpam' (kaTha. 1.3.15.) ityAdishrutirgR^ihyate | ityAdishruterityasya tasya viShNoretadarUpatvAdikaM lakShaNamasAdhAraNadharma iti j~nAyate ityadhyAhAreNAnvayaH | hi yasmAttasmAt na liN^gasya vyadhikaraNAsiddhiriti bhAvaH | tasyaivetyevakAreNa vyabhichArashaN^kApi nirastA | yadyapi 'yataH' ityanAmatvashrutireva prathamamudAhartavyA, 'te yadantarA' iti 
nAmarAhityasyaiva prathamamuktatvAt | na tu 'avarNam' ityarUpashrutiH | tathApi vAchakasya nAmno vAchyApekShayA.aprAdhAnyAt vAchyasyaiva pradhAnatvAdvAchyaprapaJNchAntargatarUparAhityashrutireva prathamamudAhR^ite- tyadoShaH |
(4) nanu harernAmarUparAhityaM nopapadyate, sarvashabdavAchyatvAt rukmavarNAdirUpavattvAchcha | anyathA IkShateH rUpopanyAsAchchetyuktavirodhApAtAdityata Aha - anAmeti | 'saH' hariH 'aprasiddhatvAt' sAkalyena svAtmano.anyena shabdAdinA.apramitatvAnnimittAdanAmetyuchyata ityarthaH | na chaivamAkAshashabdavAchyasya prasiddhibodhakanipAtadvayavirodha iti vAchyam | nipAtabodhyaprasiddheH vidheyabhUtanirvoDhR^itvAnvayitvena pUrvapakShirItyA uddeshyAkAshAnvayitvAbhAvAt | nirvoDhR^itvasya cha lokaprasiddhatvAbhAve.api 'eko dAdhAra' ityAdishrutiprasiddhatvAt | tasya chAprasiddhatvAdityanenA- niShiddhatvAt | 'bhUtavarjanAt' bhautikadehashUnyatvAttAdR^isharUparAhityAdvA arUpa ityarthaH | iti brAhme ityasyoktatvAt noktavirodha ityadhyAhR^itenAnvayaH |
|| iti AkAshAdhikaraNam || 12 ||
|| 13. suShuptyadhikaraNam ||
(1) atrAdhikaraNe svapnAdidraShTR^itvaliN^gaM brahmaNi samanvIyate | shrutyAdisaN^gatiM viShayAdikaM cha sUchayati - asaN^gatvamiti | akSharanayodAhR^ite 'agandhamarasam' iti vAjasaneyavAkye paramAtmano asaN^gatvamuktamityarthaH | tataH kimityata Aha - tachcheti | cho.avadhAraNe | itIti evaMrUpe vAjasaneyavAkya ityarthaH | anena svApnAdidraShTR^ittvasya anyaniShThatvAkShepamukhena pUrvoktAsaN^gatvasyApyanyaniShThatvAkShepAt, akSharanayenAsya AkShepikI saN^gatissUchitA| svapnAdidraShTR^itvAkhyo viShayashcha sUchitaH |
(2) tataH kimityataH sayuktikaM pUrvapakShayati - sa cheti | cho.avadhAraNe | 'saH' svapnAdidraShTA | jIva eva bhavet | kutaH taddraShTR^itvasya loke jIva eva prasiddhatvAdityarthaH | siddhAnte shrutau 'saH' iti tachChabdena 'sa vA eSha etasmin samprasAde ratvA charitvA dR^iShTvaiva puNyaM cha pApaM cha punaH pratinyAyaM prati yonyA dravati svapnAyaiva' (bR^i. 6.3.15.) iti pUrvavAkye prakR^itaH paramAtmA parAmR^ishyate | vaishabdaH prasiddhau | samyakprasIdati jIvo.asyAmiti samprasAdaH suptiH | tathA cha sa paramAtmA 'samprasAde' suptau 'ratvA' ramaNaM kR^itvA jIvagataM puNyaM cha pApaM cha dR^iShTvaiva na tvanubhUya 'charitvA' saJNcharitvA 'pratinyAyam' avasthAntaraM pravartanIyamiti nyAyamanusR^itya yadvA tattatkarmanusR^itya 'pratiyoni' pratidehaM sarvadeheShu yadvA pratiyoni tattanmArgamanusR^itya 'punaH' 'svApnAyaiva' jIvasya svapnaprAptaye eva 'Adravati' kaNThadeshamAgachChati | 'saH' paramAtmA 'tatra' svApnAvasthAyAM yatkiJNchidaniShTaM pashyati 'tena' tatkR^itapApaphalena duHkhena 'ananvAgataH' asaMspR^iShTo bhavati | tatra hetuH - asaN^ga iti | hi yasmAdayaM puruShaH 'asaN^gaH' tatkR^itapApaphalasaMsargashUnyaH pramitaH, tasmAdityarthaH | pUrvapakShI tu shrautatachChabdena jIvaM gR^ihItvA sarvaM vAkyaM jIvaparatayA vyAkhyAti |
(3) siddhAntayatsUtramavatArya vyAchaShTe - ata iti | 'vakti' samAdhatte | svapnAdidraShTR^itvaM tasyaivetyatrApi sambadhyate | tena sUtre uddeshyavidheyapratipattyartham anuvR^ittAvR^ittasya tachChabdasya 
vipariNAmassUchitaH | tachChabdena gR^ihItasyApi samanvetavyaliN^gasya spaShTapratipattyarthaM svashabdena nirdeshaH | itishabdAnantaraM suShuptIti sautrapadaM saMyojyam | vyapadeshAditi buddhyA vivichya pUrvasmAdanuShaktaM padam | asaN^ga ityapi hetusUchanAya sUtre adhyAhR^itaM padam | jIvaH para ityanena suShuptyutkrAntipadaM tatprakaraNalakShakamapi jIvaparamAtmaparamapItyuktaM bhavati | tathAtve suShuptishabdaH kartari ktinnantaH | utkrAntishabdaH dehAdutkrAmayitR^iparaH tathA chetthaM yojanA - svapnAdidraShTR^itvaM tasya paramAtmana eva bhavet na jIvasya | kutaH? yato.asAvasaN^gaH shrutaH | na cha svapnAdidraShTuH asaN^gatvashravaNe.api kuto.ayaM viShNuriti vAchyam | yato.ayamasaN^gaH karmAbaddhatvAt paraH paramAtmaiva na jIvaH | tathA cha liN^gasya niravakAshatvAt nAprayojakatvaM shaN^kyamiti bhAvaH | na cha jIve.api Ishvarabhedena asaN^gatvoktiH sambhavatIti vAchyam | prAj~nenetyAdisuShuptyutkrAntiprakaraNadvayagatavAkyayorasaN^gAtsvapnAdidraShTuH IshvarAjjIvasya bhedavyapadeshAditi| prAj~neneti shrutyudAharaNena sUtre suShuptipadaM mokShasyApi grAhakaM, tenAyaM bhedo vyAvahArika iti shaN^kAnirAso.api bhavati| suShuptyutkrAntipadena cha tatprakaraNaM lakShyata ityuktaM bhavati | utkrAntipadaM cha jIvasya dehAdutkramaNarUpamaraNa- vAchi | shrutau prAj~nashabdaH svArthikANantaH | tathA cha 'prAj~nena' sarvaj~nena paramAtmanA 'sampariShvaktaH' samAshliShTaH supto muktashcha dehAdbAhyamAntaraM cha kiJNchana viShayAdikaM na vedeti prathamavAkyArthaH | dvitIyArthastu - prAktanAdhi- karaNe.abhihitaH |
(4) nanu kathamasharIrasya svApnAdidarshanaM yuktaM syAdityata Aha - svapnAdIti | chashabdaH samuchchaye | apyarthe vA | Adipadena jIvagatAvasthA gR^ihyate | tathA cha na kevalamasaN^gatvaM karmAbaddhatvAt parasyaiva yujyate, kintu svApnAdidraShTR^itvaM cha 'tasyaiva' paramAtmana eva jIvAdapi mukhyato yujyate | ataH tasyaiva tadvachanaM yujyate na jIvasya| kutaH? tasyaiva 'sarvaj~natvAt' satyAsheShArthaj~natvAt svapnapadArthAnAM jIvagatAvasthAyAshcha satyatAyA vakShyamANatvAditi bhAvaH | na chAsharIratvaliN^gaM bAdhakaM, yato.atra tasyaiva chichCharIrakasyaiva svapnAdidraShTR^itvamuchyate | na cha 'dR^iShTvaiva puNyaM cha pApaM cha' (bR^i.6.3.15.) ityAdyayoga iti vAchyam | yato.atra AdipadagR^ihItaM puNyapApAdidraShTR^itvaM liN^gAntaraM cha tasyaiva yujyate ata iti yojanA | tatropapattistu bR^ihadbhAShyAdavagantavyA | anena - 'suShuptyutkrAntyoH' 'prAj~nena' iti suShuptyutkrAntiprakaraNayoH suShuptyutkrAntyoH suShuptiyutatvAt suShuptirjIvaH, utkrAmayitR^itvAt utkrAntirIshvaraH, tathA cha jIveshvarayoH 'bhedena' bhinnatvenaiva 'vyapadeshAt' uktatvAt na tayorabhedaH | ato neshvarAbhedenApi jIve asaN^gatvoktiryujyate | kintu tattu tasyaiva Ishvarasyaiva yujyate | ata eva svapnAdidraShTR^itvaM cha tasyaiva vaktuM yujyate na jIvasyeti sUtrArthaH ukto bhavati | 
|| iti suShuptyadhikaraNam || 13 ||
|| 14. brAhmaNAdhikaraNam ||
(1) atrAdhikaraNe brAhmaNanAma samanvIyate| shrutyAdisaN^gatiM viShayAdikaM cha sUchayati - eSha iti | itIti| vAjasaneyakodAhR^itaR^iN^mantra ityarthaH | na kevalaM viShNoH api tu kasyachit brAhmaNasyApItyaperarthaH | idaM cha yo janmAdyadhikaraNeShu viShNorananyApekShayA jagatsraShTR^itvoktyA abhisaMhito 
nityamahimA saH 'eShaH' iti vAkye brAhmaNa- syApi pratIyata iti yattachChabdAdhyAhAreNa yojyam | anena pUrvAbhisaMhitanityamahimatvasya viShNoranyasyApyAkShepAt janmAdyadhikaraNaiH phalamukhena asyAkShepikI saN^gatiruktA bhavati | tathA brAhmaNAkhyaviShayo.api sUchitaH | yadvA - devAnAmiti vAkyaM devatAdhikaraNapratipAdyAnuvAdaparatvenApi vyAkhyAya tenAsyAkShepikI saN^gatiruktA draShTavyA | tathA hi 'tadupari' iti sUtreNa devAnAM viriJNchAdyamarANAM vidyAkarmaNossakAshAt sAdhyA yA nityapadaprAptiruktA, sA na yuktA | kutaH? yataH 'eShaH' iti vAkye brAhmaNapadoditasya viriJNchasya nityamahimA 'pratIyate' pratipAdyata iti vAkyayojanA | shrutau brahmaNA vedenANyate.avagamyate iti vyutpattiH | dIrghavyatyAso viShNorvedagamyatve jIvAdAdhikya- j~nApakaH | tathA cha brAhmaNasya viShNoreShaH pUrvoktamahimA nityaH | kuto? yato.ayaM 'na karmaNA vardhate no kanIyAn' (bR^i.6.4.22.) shubhakarmaNA tatphalena sukhena na vardhate | pApakarmaNA tatphalena duHkhena na hrasate iti shrutyarthaH | sayuktikaM pUrvapakShayati - sa iti | vAjasaneyashruta ityarthaH | chashabdo.avadhAraNe | viriJNcha eveti sambadhyate | ityajashabdAditi | ityevaM rUpeShu pUrvottaravAkyeShu shrutAjashabdAdityarthaH | 'sa eShaH' paramAtmA 'mahAn' aparimitaH 'ajo' janmarahitashcheti shrutyarthaH | pUrvapakShI tu brAhmaNAjashabdavAchyaM viriJNchiM manyate | nanu kathaM brAhmaNo viriJNcho bhavet | taduparIti sUtre devAnAM vidyAkarmabhyAM padaprApteH samarthitatvena brAhmaNe shrutanityamahimatvasya viriJNche asambha- vAt | sAdipadasyAnityatvaniyamAt ityata Aha - devAnAM cheti | cho.avadhAraNe | itItyanantaraM sUtra iti sheShaH | tathA cha taduparIti sUtre viriJNchetaradevAnAmeva vidyAkarmaNoH sakAshAt padaprAptiH 'sUchitA' samarthitA | na tu viriJNchasyApi | tasyeshvararUpatvena devakoTyapraviShTatvAdato viriJNchasya nityamahimattvaM yuktameveti yojanA |
(2) siddhAntayatsUtramavatArayati - ata iti | vAjasaneyake sarvavashitvavAchishabdasyaivAditvAtsUtrasya tadvi- saMvAdamAshaN^kya tatparihArAya sUtrAnukUlatayA sadR^ishashAkhAntaragatavAkyodAharaNapUrvakaM sUtraM vyAchaShTe - sarvasyeti | 'sarvasya' brahmarudrAdeH sakAshAt guNairadhikashchAsau sarvasya patiH pAlakashcheti sarvAdhipatiH | 'sarvasya' jagataH 'IshAnAM' brahmAdInAM anaH preraka iti sarvasyeshAna iti shrutyantarArthaH | sarvavashishabdArthastu sarvamasya vashe yasmAddhariH sarvavashI tata iti bR^ihadbhAShyAdavagantavyaH | 'sa vA eShaH' iti vAjasaneyashrutiH | 'saH' prANashabdoktaH 'eShaH' samAnashabdAbhidheyaH 'AtmA' paramAtmA 'iti na' dR^iShTavanna 'iti na' shrutavanna, kintu dR^iShTashrutavilakShaNa ityarthaH | vaishabdaH prasiddhau | kuta ityataH 'AtmA.agR^ihyo na hi gR^ihyate.ashIryo na hi shIryate.asaN^go na hi sajjate.asito na vyathate na riShyati.........sa eSha AtmA.ajaro.amaro.amR^ito.abhayaH' (bR^i. 2.4.24.) iti vAkyasheShaH pravR^ittaH | atrA- gR^ihya ityAdirAtmana iti netyuktArthe sAkalyena agrAhyatvAdirUpahetusamarpakaH | na hItyAdistu tatra pramANAbhAvAditi hetusUchakaH | yadyapi bR^ihadbhAShye 'itina' ramAvanna 'itina' brahmAdivanna, baddhavanna, muktavannetyanyathA vyAkhyAtam | tathApyatra 'sa yoà¤¼.ato.ashrutaH' (ai.A. 3.2.4.) iti samAkhyAshrutyanusArAdevaM vyAkhyAtamityadoShaH | ityAdIti | ityAdau shrutAH ye sarvAdhipatyAdivAchakAH shabdAH tebhya ityarthaH | AdipadAtsarvavashitvAdivAchishabdasaN^grahaH | anena sautrAdishabdo na kevalaM shAkhAntaroktasarveshAnAdishabdagrAhakaH, kintu vAjasaneyoktasarvavilakShamatvasarvavashitvAdishabda- 
grAhako.apIti uktaM bhavati | evaM hetuM vyAkhyAya sUtre samanvayasUtrAt tattvityanuvartya vipariNamyamAnena tadityane- nAnvayayogyamuddeshyasamarpakaM nityamahimeti padaM chAdhyAhR^ityAhatya niShkR^iShTAM pratij~nAM darshayati - nityamahimeti | idaM cha phalakathanarUpam | shabdebhya iti hetvanvayayogyaM sAdhyaM tu brAhmaNa ityadhyAhR^itaM draShTavyam | anena - ayaM brAhmaNaH tattu viShNureva, na viriJNchaH | kutaH? 'patyAdishabdebhyaH' sarvAdhipatyAdivAchisarvAdhipatyAdishabdebhyo.atra shrutebhyaH | tathA cha nityamahimA.api sa eveti sUtrArtha ukto bhavati |
(3) nanu sarvAdhipatyAdivAchishabdasadbhAve.api kuto brAhmaNasya viShNutvanishchaya ityaprayojakatavashaN^kA- vAraNAya tatra sarvAdhipitvasya viShNvekaniShThatve tAvachChrutimAha - uteti | idaM cha 'puruSha evedaM sarvam' | 'yadbhUtaM yachcha bhavyam' iti pUrvavAkyena saha vyAkhyeyam | tatprakArastu - 'yadbhUtam' atItaM 'bhavyaM' bhaviShyat vartamAnaM cha tatsarvaM 'puruSha eva' paramapuruShAdhInameva | kutaH? yato yasmAt na kevalamamuktasarvAdhipatiH puruShaH, kintu 'amR^itatvasyota' muktasamudAyasyApi 'IshAnaH' adhipatiH | 'vichitrA hi taddhitagatiH' iti vachanAtsamudAyArthe tvapratyayaH | tattvapradIpe tu - bhAvabhavitrorabhedavyapadeshAt bhAve tvapratyayaH | 'amR^itatvasya' mokShasya IshAna iti cheti arthAntaraM choktam | atra hetumAha - yaditi | tR^itIyA dvitIyArthe | tathA cha 'yat' yasmAt 'annena' annaM martyaM saMsArisamUham 'atirohati' atishete, tasmAdityarthaH | muktAvanadhInatve sarvaj~nasya buddhimataH svAdhInasaMsAribhyo mokShapradAnAyogAditi bhAvaH |
(4) idAnIM sarvashabdasambandhikeshAnapadoktasarvaprerakatve shrutimAha - sapteti | akSharanaye vyAkhyAteyaM shrutiH | neti netItyuktadR^iShTashrutasarvavilakShaNatve.api shrutimudAharati - sa iti | iyamapi sarvatrAdhikaraNe vyAkhyAtA | ityAdI- tyAdipadena sarvavashitvAdAvapyevameva shrutyantarAmyudAhartavyAnIti sUchayati | 'tasyaiva' viShNoreva nAnyasyetyevArthaH | 'hi' yasmAtte sarvAdhipatyAdishabdAH ityavagatAH tasmAt nAprayojakatvaM shaN^kyamiti vAkyasheShaH |
|| iti brAhmaNAdhikaraNam || 14 ||
iti shrImatparamahaMsaparivrAjakAchAryANAM sarvatantrasvatantrANAM
shrImadraghunAthatIrthapUjyapAdAnAM shiShyeNa 
shrImajjagannAthayatinA kR^itAyAM
shrImadbrahmasUtrabhAShyadIpikAyAM
prathamAdhyAyasya tR^itIyaH pAdaH 
|| OM ||
